# 5.2 PRACH

## 5.2.0-2 PRACH Additional support: Sathiaseelan Sundaralingam (ID: 11445843)

## 5.2.1 References - content moved to 1.1 under CNI-108168, to be removed

## 5.2.2 Overview

### 5.2.2.1 General aspects

**5.2.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11445900`)

General aspects
L1 Loki HW shall support features:

-FDD FR1CPRI (dmWaves)defined in 5GC002481-AA

-TDD FR1 eCPRI (cmWaves) with & without Beam Forming defined in 5GC002056-AA

-2Rx/4Rx MRC (Note: 4Rx IRC is also introduced for TDD ABIO parity testing but via seperate pre-conditional feature)

-NSA, SA, NSA+SA

-all the features and corresponding functionalities implemented in 5G20B

---

### 5.2.2.2 Functional split

#### 5.2.2.2.0-1 Functional split 5G-L1-UL shall follow the same functional split in 7-2e as in 7-2a for PRACH channel. [CB012115-GA] The requirement is also valid for L1 Odin. [End CB012115-GA]**** (ID: 11445914)

### 5.2.2.3 Interface messaging

**5.2.2.3.0-2**  (ID: `11445936`)

Interface messaging
L1 shall support the following L1L2 and L1L3 interfaces (in addition to other common interfaces offered by higher layers) for PRACH:

-L1L2: UlData\_PrachReceiveReq (original location 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_232, now 5G\_L1\_IF\_233\_replaced([11514296](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2oWPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

-L1L2: UlData\_PrachReceiveInd (original location 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_233, now 5G\_L1\_IF\_234\_replaced([11514309](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2oWvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

-L1L3: UlCell\_SetupReq (original location 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_151, now 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

**[RP003187-A, RP003187-H] The requirement is also valid for** L1 Thor. **[End RP003187-A, RP003187-H]**\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also valid for L1 Odin.** [End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| *Technology* | *Feature / support* |
| FR1 FDD CPRI | Supported |
| FR1 FDD OBSAI | **[CB010969-SR-CB] Supported** [End CB010969-SR-CB]\*\*\*\* |
| FR1 TDD 7-2e eCPRI | **[CB011178-A]Supported**[End CB011178-A]\*\*\*\* |
| FR1 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | supported |
| FR1 TDD 7-2e eCPRI | **[CB007595-B] supported** [End CB007595-B]\*\*\*\* |

---

## 5.2.3 Start-up configuration

### 5.2.3.1 Overview

**5.2.3.1.0-1**  (ID: `11445957`)

Overview
Startup

L1-SW in Loner and Loki shall read the RAD parameters from the configuration file at startup time i.e. when L1 boots up. Those parameter values shall be untouched until next reboot.

The RAD parameter are defined in 5G\_L1\_3822\_replaced([11494983](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fEqxAPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Loner and 5G\_L1\_3823\_replaced([11494976](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fEqKAPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Loki.

---

### 5.2.3.2 Robustness and configuration validation

## 5.2.4 Cell configuration

### 5.2.4.1 Overview

#### 5.2.4.1.1 Configuration acquisition

**5.2.4.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11445992`)

Configuration acquisition
The L1 shall support the PRACH cell level parameters (prachFormat, prachStartSymbol, prachScs, firstPrachRootSeqIndex, prachSequenceType, prachCohCombLen, totalNumberOfRAPreambles and prachZeroCorrelationZoneConfig) specified in 5G\_L1\_446\_replaced([11479019](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fDNYdvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_450\_replaced([11478967](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fDMxbvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Where prachCohCombLen can be overwritten by L1 if needed.

In addition to the PRACH parameters, the bandwidth, CPRI compression, Number of available Rx branches, number of uncorrelated Rx branches to be used for dtx thresholds and frequency shift to be supported with DSS are shown in the below sections.

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| *HW* | *Technology* | *Feature / support* |
| Loner | FR1 FDD CPRI | Supported |
| FR1 TDD CPRI | Supported |  |
| FR1 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported |  |
| FR2 TDD CPRI | Supported |  |
| FR2 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported |  |
| Loki | FR1 FDD CPRI | Supported |
| FR1 FDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported |  |
| FR1 TDD CPRI | Supported |  |
| FR1 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported |  |
| FR2 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported |  |
| Thor | FR1 FDD CPRI | Supported |
| FR1 FDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported |  |
| FR1 TDD CPRI | Supported |  |
| FR1 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported |  |
| FR1 TDD 7-2e eCPRI | **[CB007595-B] Supported** [End CB007595-B]\*\*\*\* |  |
| FR2 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported |  |
| Odin | FR1 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | **[CB012115-IA] Supported** [End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\* |
| FR1 FDD CPRI | **[CB012115-JA] Supported** [End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\* |  |
| FR1 TDD 7-2e eCPRI | **[CB012115-GA]Supported**[End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\* |  |
| FR1 FDD 7-2a eCPRI | **[CB012115-LA]Supported**[End CB012115-LA]\*\*\*\* |  |

### 5.2.4.2 PRACH configuration index

#### 5.2.4.2.1 Support overview

##### 5.2.4.2.1.1 Loner and Loki

**5.2.4.2.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11446022`)

Loner and Loki
Content of this requirement is frozen and valid until 23R3 release. For later releases please refer to the objects below

L1 shall support the following configuration indices:

Supported PRACH formats in Loner HW:

For FDD (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-2):

Format 0: [5GC000836-E] 12, 13, 14 [End 5GC000836-E], [CB007488-A]15[End CB007488-A].

Format 1: [5GC000938-A] 40, 41, 42, 43 [End 5GC000938-A]

For TDD FR1 (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-3):

 Format A2: [5GC000425] 87...90, 92, 93, 94, 96, 97, 98, 100, 101, 102, 104 [End 5GC000425]

 Format B4: [5GC001304-A] 145...152, 156...160, 161, 162 [End 5GC001304-A]

 Format C2: [5GC001301-A] 189…192, 194…198, 201, 202, 203, 205, 206 [End 5GC001301-A]

 Format 0:   [5GC001349-A] 0...7, 9, 12, 14, 17, 19 [End 5GC001349-A]

For TDD FR2 (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-4):

 Format A2: [5GC000580-F]31, 34, 38, 41, 43, 52, 53 [End 5GC000580-F]

 Format C2: [5GC001300-A] with 120 kHz: 175, 177, 178, 182, 185, 187, 196.[End 5GC001300-A]

Supported PRACH formats in LoKi HW:

For FDD (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-2):

 Format 0: [5GC001868-D] [5GC001787-A] 12, [End 5GC001787-A] 13, 14, 15  [End 5GC001868-D][5GC000938-C] 8, 9, 10, 11[End 5GC000938-C]

 Format 1: [5GC000938-C] 36, 37, 38, 39, 40, 41, 42, 43 [End 5GC000938-C]

[CB007814-C]

5G-L1-UL shall support PRACH format 0 with supported prachConfigurationIndex in range 8...15 in ABIO for FR1 FDD eCPRI.

5G-L1-UL shall support PRACH format 1 with supported prachConfigurationIndex in range 36...43 in ABIO for FR1 FDD eCPRI.

[End CB007814-C]

For TDD FR1 (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-3):

[CB007326-A]

 Format A2: [5GC001868-A] 87...90, 92, [5GC001787-D] 93 [End 5GC001787-D], 94, 96, 97, 98, 100, 101, 102, 104.[End 5GC001868-A]

 Format B4: [5GC001868-F] 145...152, 156...160, 161, 162.[End 5GC001868-F]

 Format C2: [5GC001868-F] 189…192, 194…198, 201, 202, 203, 205, 206.[5GC001868-F]

 Format 0:   [5GC001349-A] 0...7, 9, 12, 14, 17, 19 [End 5GC001349-A]

[End CB007326-A]

[CB008205-B, CB008205-C]

5G-L1-UL shall support PRACH format 0 with supported prachConfigurationIndex 12 in ABIO for O-RAN compliant FR1 FDD eCPRI.

[End CB008205-B, CB008205-C]

[CB009881-CD, CB009881-CG, CB009881-W]

 Format A2: [5GC000425] 87...90, 92, 93, 94, 96, 97, 98, 100, 101, 102, 104 [End 5GC000425]

 Format B4: [5GC001304-A] 145...152, 156...160, 161, 162 [End 5GC001304-A]

 Format C2: [5GC001301-A] 189…192, 194…198, 201, 202, 203, 205, 206 [End 5GC001301-A]

 Format 0:   [5GC001349-B] 0...7, 9, 12, 14, 17, 19 [End 5GC001349-B]

[End CB009881-CD, CB009881-CG, CB009881-W]

---

##### 5.2.4.2.1.2 Loki

**5.2.4.2.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `11446039`)

Loki
Content of this reuirement is frozen and valid until 23R3 release. For later releases please refer to the objects below

Supported PRACH formats in LoKi HW:

For FDD (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-2):

* Format 0: [5GC001868-D] 12, 13, 14 [End 5GC001868-D] [5GC000938-C] 8, 9, 10, 11, 15 [End 5GC000938-C]
* Format 1: [5GC000938-C] 36, 37, 38, 39, 40, 41, 42, 43 [End 5GC000938-C]

[CB007814-C]

5G-L1-UL shall support PRACH format 0 with supported prachConfigurationIndex in range 8...15 in ABIO for FR1 FDD eCPRI.

5G-L1-UL shall support PRACH format 1 with supported prachConfigurationIndex in range 36...43 in ABIO for FR1 FDD eCPRI.

[End CB007814-C]

[CB008205-B, CB008205-C] 5G-L1-UL shall support PRACH format 0 with prachConfigurationIndex 12 in ABIO for O-RAN compliant FR1 FDD eCPRI. [End CB008205-B, CB008205-C]

[CB009444-I] 5G-L1-UL shall support PRACH format 0 with supported prachConfigurationIndex in range 12, 13, 14 in RINLINE1 for FR1-FDD-eCPRI. [End CB009444-I]

For TDD FR1 (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-3):

* Format A2: [5GC001868-A] 87...90, 92, 93, 94, 96, 97, 98, 100, 101, 102, 104.[End 5GC001868-A]
* Format B4: [5GC001868-F] 145...152, 156...160, 161, 162.[End 5GC001868-F]
* Format C2: [5GC001868-F] 189…192, 194…198, 201, 202, 203, 205, 206.[5GC001868-F]
* Format 0: [5GC001349-B] 0...7, 9, 12, 14, 17, 19 [End 5GC001349-B]

[CB008423] All above Formats shall be supported with CPRI [End CB008423]

[CB009443-C] Format B4 shall be supported in RINLINE1 for FR1-TDD-eCPRI. [End CB009443-C]

[CB009881-CD, CB009881-CG, CB009881-W]

 Format A2: [5GC000425] 87...90, 92, 93, 94, 96, 97, 98, 100, 101, 102, 104 [End 5GC000425]

 Format B4: [5GC001304-A] 145...152, 156...160, 161, 162 [End 5GC001304-A]

 Format C2: [5GC001301-A] 189…192, 194…198, 201, 202, 203, 205, 206 [End 5GC001301-A]

 Format 0:   [5GC001349-B] 0...7, 9, 12, 14, 17, 19 [End 5GC001349-B]

[End CB009881-CD, CB009881-CG, CB009881-W]

For TDD FR2 (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-4):

* Format A2: [CB007596-A] 31, 34, 38, 41, 43, 52, 53 [End CB007596-A]
* Format C2: [CB007403-C] with 120 kHz: 175, 177, 178, 182, 185, 187, 196.[End CB007403-C]
* Format C0: [5GC001305-A] 146, 149, 153, 156, 158, 166, 167. [End 5GC001305-A]
* Format B4: [CB007723-A][CB007539-B] 114, 117, 118, 122, 125, 128, 133, 135[End CB007539-B] [End CB007723-A], 121, 124, 126, 127, 136
* Note: The PRACH configuation indices mentioned are introduced via 7723. However, for extended cell range feature only indices with startSymbol = 0 are applicable.
* Note: For conformance test purposes only, PRACH configuration indices 22, 25, 26 are supported for FDD (introduced in PR644863). Refer to 5G\_UP\_IF\_410 in the 5G UP External Interfaces module.

---

##### 5.2.4.2.1.3 Loner, Loki, Thor, Odin

**5.2.4.2.1.3.0-2**  (ID: `13444198`)

Loner, Loki, Thor, Odin
Summary of valid PRACH configuration indexes:

For FDD (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-2):

 Format 0: [8...15].

 Format 1: [36...43].

For TDD FR1 (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-3):

 Format 0: [0...7, 9, 12, 14, 17].

 Format A2: [87...90, 92, 93, 94, 96, 97, 98, 100, 101, 102, 104].

 Format B4: [145...152, 156...160, 161, 162].

 Format C2: [189…192, 194…198, 199, 200 (supported with 15kHz PRACH SCS), 201, 202, 203, 205, 206, 210 (supported with 15kHz PRACH SCS)].

For TDD FR2 (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-4):

 Format A2: [31, 34, 38, 41, 43, 52, 53, 32, 36, 37, 40, 47, 48, 49, 55, 56].

 Format C2: [175, 177, 178, 182, 185, 187, 196, 176, 180, 184, 191, 194, 198, 199].

 Format C0: [146, 149, 153, 156, 158, 166, 167, 145, 147, 151, 155, 162, 163, 164, 169, 170].

 Format B4: [114, 117, 118, 121, 122, 124...128, 133, 135, 136, 119, 123, 129, 131, 138, 139].

L1 shall use parameter *UlCell\_SetupReq->prachConfig-> prachConfigurationIndex  from L1 – 5G-CP-RT interface to define requested value.*

Supported values for *prachConfigurationIndex parameter for different L1 HW and technologies for FR1 FDD are shown in the table:*

#### 5.2.4.2.2 Board specifics

**5.2.4.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `11446079`)

Board specifics
L1 shall support the following configuration indices in Thor of ASOG&ASOH:

PRACH configuration index is set during cell setup procedure using UlCell\_SetupReq -> prachConfigurationIndex IE.

For FDD (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-2):

* Format 0:   12

Number of allocated PRBs should be 6 in this configuration.

For TDD FR1 (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-3):

* Format B4:  148.

Number of allocated PRBs should be 12 in this configuration.

---

#### 5.2.4.2.3 Planning considerations

##### 5.2.4.2.3.0-1 Planning considerations L1 shall support the same PRACH configuration index for all TDD subcells belonging to the same cell. The subcells shall be seperated with firstPrachRootSeqIndex which is an IE of UlCell_SetupReq message (See PrachConfig structure in 5G_L1_IF_153_replaced( 11513459 )). (ID: 11446093)

### 5.2.4.3 PRACH root sequence index

#### 5.2.4.3.1 Support overview

**5.2.4.3.1.0-2**  (ID: `11446124`)

Support overview
L1 shall support following PRACH root sequence indices:

For FDD (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-2):

  Format 0: [0…837]

  Format 1: [0…837]

For TDD FR1 (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-3):

  Format 0: [0…837]

  Format A2: [0…137]

  Format B4: [0…137]

  Format C2: [0…137]

For TDD FR2 (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-4):

  Format A2: [0…137]

  Format C2: [0…137]

  Format C0: [0…137]

  Format B4: [0…137]

L1 shall use parameter *UlCell\_SetupReq->prachConfig->* firstPrachRootSeqIndex from L1 – 5G-CP-RT interface to define requested value.\*\*

Loner
For CPRI and unrestricted set (short and long format), the L1-SW in Loner shall write/configure the HW with swCount defined by floor(LRA/Ncs).  This parameter defines the number of preambles that can be accommodated in a root sequence for given Ncs.  When Ncs= 0, floor(LRA/Ncs) = 1. Where Ncs is deduced from the parameter zeroCorrelationZoneConfig which is received in the UlCell\_SetupReq message and LRA defines the PRACH preamble sequence length (139 for short and 839 for long format). The valid range is [1…64] [0...15].

The text is set against a white background.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_5222.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0] value |  |  |
| 0 |  | 0 |  |  |
|  | 1 |  | 2 |  |
|  | 2 |  | 4 |  |
|  | 3 |  | 6 |  |

|  | 5 |  | 10 |  |
|  | 6 |  | 12 |  |
|  | 7 |  | 13 |  |

### 5.2.4.6 PRACH formats

#### 5.2.4.6.1 Overview

**5.2.4.6.1.0-1**  (ID: `11446301`)

Overview
L1 shall process following PRACH formats:

FR1 FDD: {0,1}

FR1 TDD: {0, A2, B4, C2\_30kHz, C2\_15kHz}

FR2:        {A2, B4, C0, C2\_30kHz}

L1 shall use parameter *UlCell\_SetupReq->prachConfig->prachFormat from L1 – 5G-CP-RT interface to define requested format.*

Supported values for *prachFormat parameter for different L1 HW and technologies are shown in the table:*

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| L1 HW and technologies |  |  | *prachFormat* |
| FR1 FDD | Loner | CPRI | {0,1} |
| Loki | CPRI |  |  |
| OBSAI |  |  |  |
| 7-2a-eCPRI |  |  |  |
| Thor | CPRI |  |  |
| 7-2a-eCPRI |  |  |  |
| OBSAI |  |  |  |
| Odin | **[CB012115-JA]CPRI**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\* |  |  |
| **[CB012115-LA]7-2a-eCPRI**[End CB012115-LA]\*\*\*\* |  |  |  |
| FR1 TDD | Loner | CPRI | {0, A2, B4, C2\_30kHz} |
| 7-2a-eCPRI |  |  |  |
| Loki | CPRI | {0, A2, B4, C2\_30kHz, C2\_15kHz} |  |
| 7-2a-eCPRI |  |  |  |
| Thor | 7-2a-eCPRI |  |  |
| **[CB010575-D] CPRI** [End CB010575-D]\*\*\*\* |  |  |  |
| 7-2e-eCPRI | **[CB007595-B] {B4}** [End CB007595-B]***\** \*[CB009514-F]** {0, A2, C2\_30kHz} **[End CB009514-F]** |  |  |
| Odin | **[CB012115-IA]7-2a-eCPRI**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\* | {0, A2, B4, C2\_30kHz, C2\_15kHz} |  |
| **[CB012115-GA]7-2e-eCPRI**[End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\* |  |  |  |
| FR2 TDD | Loner | CPRI | {A2, C2} |
| 7-2a-eCPRI | {A2, C2} |  |  |
| Loki | 7-2a-eCPRI | {A2, B4, C0, C2} |  |
| Thor | **[CB010576-A] 7-2a-eCPRI**[End CB010576-A]\*\*\*\* | {A2, B4, C0, C2} |  |

**[CB007491-A] For Loki and Thor in FDD, the high speed cell flag (NRCELL/actHighSpeedCell, refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) can be activated together with PRACH long formats F0 or F1. The sequence type can be set to unrestricted, restricted set type A, or** [CB007491-B] restricted set type B **[End CB007491-B]** [End CB007491-A].***\****\*

**[CB007491-G] In Loki and Thor, the L1 shall support PRACH long format F0 with unrestricted set or restricted set A or restricted set B for high speed cells in TDD FR1. Note that restricted set type B can only be used in high speed cells (i.e. NRCELL/actHighSpeedCell is set to true, refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))** [End CB007491-G]\*\*\*\*

**[CB009422-A] 5G\_L1\_UL shall support all the listed PRACH formats 0, A2, B4, C2 for 30kHz (as defined in the table above) for a new 5G FR1 TDD frame structure (DDDSUUUUUU) in Loki and Thor with FR1-TDD-CPRI and FR1-TDD-e-CPRI-7-2a** [End CB009422-A].\*\*\*\*

#### 5.2.4.6.2 Symbol configuration

##### 5.2.4.6.2.1 Symbol duration

**5.2.4.6.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11446321`)

Symbol duration
L1 shall support following duration of PRACH preambles in number of symbols for one time occasion (where 1 symbol is 1 symbol with pusch scs) and in us:

For FDD (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-2):

  Format 0: {0 in 3gpp}, but actually {13 pusch symbols, xxx us}

  Format 1: {0 in 3gpp}, but actually {32 pusch symbols, xxx us}

For TDD FR1 (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-3):

  Format 0: {0 in 3gpp}, but actually {26 pusch symbols, xxx us}

  Format A2: {4 pusch symbols, xxx ms}

  Format B4: {12}

  Format C2: {6}

For TDD FR2 (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-4):

  Format A2: {4}

  Format C2: {6}

  Format C0: {2}

  Format B4: {12}

#### 5.2.4.6.4 PRACH periodicity

**5.2.4.6.4.0-1**  (ID: `11446426`)

PRACH periodicity
For FDD, L1 (Loner and Loki [RP003187-K] and Thor [End RP003187-K]) shall support PRACH periodicity 20 ms defined in Table 6.3.3.2-2 of 38.211 for PRACH format 1

[RP003187-K] The requirement is also valid for Thor[End RP003187-K]

[CB007814-C] 5G-L1-UL shall support PRACH periodicity 20 and 40 ms defined in Table 6.3.3.2-2 of 38.211 for PRACH format 1 in ABIO for FR1 FDD eCPRI. [End CB007814-C]

[CB011178-A] 5G-L1-UL shall also support requirements above for FR1 FDD 7-2a eCPRI for Thor. [End CB011178-A]

---

#### 5.2.4.6.5 TDD FR1

##### 5.2.4.6.5.1 Format 0

###### 5.2.4.6.5.1.1 Support overview

###### 5.2.4.6.5.1.1.1 Loner

**5.2.4.6.5.1.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11446460`)

Loner
For Loner, L1 shall support PRACH format 0 in TDD FR1 CPRI and eCPRI mode (5GC0001349-A and 5GC0001349-B):

PUSCH SCS = 30 kHz, PRACH SCS = 1.25 kHz

Unrestricted set only

Ncs index = 1..15

PRACH occasion can be assigned on two 30 KHz consecutive UL slots.

PRACH FDM (several frequency occasions): no FDM

SSB per RACH occasion: 1

Support both SA and NSA

Support all bandwidths: 100MHz, 90MHz, 80MHz, 70MHz, 60MHz, 50MHz, 40MHz, 30MHz, 20MHz

Applicable for 5GC001116 and 5GC001070 frame structures, but not usable with 5GC001208 frame structure.

---

###### 5.2.4.6.5.1.1.2 Loner, Loki

###### 5.2.4.6.5.1.1.2.1 CPRI

**5.2.4.6.5.1.1.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11446482`)

CPRI
For TDD FR1, L1 shall support PRACH format 0 with the following conditions:

1) The PRACH reception only support non-coherent combining for long format.

2) The PRACH reception algorithm shall support decimation filter chain to reduce FFT size to 1536.

3) Support start symbol 0 (start symbol 7 is not supported).

4) Support the CP length for PRACH F0, and one PRACH occasion occupy two 30kHz slots.

5) Support the SC offset  =1 (parameter k\_bar).

6) Support up to 60km/h speed with small UE frequency offset, or support 3km/h speed with maximum UE frequency offset.

7) Periodicity=160 ms (configuration index=0), 80 ms (configuration index=1), 40 ms (configuration index=2), 20 ms (configuration index=3..6) and 10 ms (configuration index=7..19)

[Before-CNI-122313-A]

[CB009881-CG] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.[End CB009881-CG]

[CNI-122313-A]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313-A]

---

###### 5.2.4.6.5.1.1.2.2 eCPRI

**5.2.4.6.5.1.1.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `11446496`)

eCPRI
For Loki, L1 shall support PRACH format 0 in TDD FR1 eCPRI mode (5GC0001349-B):

PUSCH SCS = 30 kHz, PRACH SCS = 1.25 kHz

Unrestricted set only

Ncs index = 1..15

PRACH occasion can be assigned on two 30 KHz consecutive UL slots.

PRACH FDM (several frequency occasions): no FDM

SSB per RACH occasion: 1

Support both SA and NSA

Support all bandwidths: 100MHz, 90MHz, 80MHz, 70MHz, 60MHz, 50MHz, 40MHz, 30MHz, 20MHz[CB008278-A], 10MHz [End CB008278-A]

Applicable for 5GC001116 and 5GC001070 frame structures, but not usable with 5GC001208 frame structure.

[Before-CNI-122313-A]

[CB009881-CG] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE 1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI with bandwidth 100MHz, 90MHz, 80MHz, 50MHz, 40MHz, 20MHz. [End CB009881-CG]

[CNI-122313-A]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313-A]

---

###### 5.2.4.6.5.1.1.3 Thor, Odin

**5.2.4.6.5.1.1.3.0-1**  (ID: `11446511`)

Thor, Odin
**L1 Thor shall support PRACH format 0 for TDD FR1 with the following conditions:**

1) The PRACH reception only support non-coherent combining for long format.

2) The PRACH reception algorithm shall support decimation filter chain to reduce FFT size to 1536.

3) Support start symbol 0 (start symbol 7 is not supported).

4) Support the CP length for PRACH F0, and one PRACH occasion occupy two 30kHz slots.

5) Support the SC offset  =1 (parameter k\_bar).

6) Support up to 60km/h speed with small UE frequency offset, or support 3km/h speed with maximum UE frequency offset.

7) Periodicity:

**[RP003187-A] 20 ms (configuration index=3..6)** 160 ms (configuration index=0), 80 ms (configuration index=1), 40 ms (configuration index=2), 10 ms (configuration index=7, 9, 12, 14, 17~~, 19~~) **[End RP003187-A]**\*\*\*\*

**[CB009514-F] The requirement is also applicable for Thor(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e** [End CB009514-F]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\*

Time and frequency occasions
**PRACH long format 0 for TDD**

**For L1 Loner:**

Below functionality shall be supported in CPRI and eCPRI platforms with **5GC001349-A (CPRI) and** 5GC001349-B (eCPRI).\*\*\*\*

Time and frequency occasions to be processed are given by the field *prachOccasions in the* UlData\_PrachReceiveReq message.\*\*

For PRACH format 0,  one PRACH frequency/time occasion is supported with starting symbol = 0. Each element of the array should have value 0x0000 or 0x8000. Each non-zero element of the array (i.e. 0x8000) corresponds to a valid PRACH occasion in the frequency domain.

With starting symbol = 0, and 1 time occasion allocated, the first element of the above mentioned array has value 0x8000, and all the other values of this parameter is 0x0000.

Note that the slot size for PRACH format 0 is based on SCS 30kHz.

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a visual representation of a "PRACH format 0 sequence." The sequence is depicted as a series of vertical bars within a light blue rectangular area. There are approximately 30 such bars, with a slightly thicker, darker vertical line dividing the sequence into two sections. The rightmost section of the sequence contains fewer bars, and the very last bar is white, while the others are light blue. Below this visual representation, a text label clearly states "PRACH format 0 sequence." The background of the image is black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_5259.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

**For L1 Loki:**

Above functionalities shall be supported in eCPRI platform with the CFAM feature **5GC001349-B.**

**[CB007326-A] FR1-TDD-eCPRI is supported for ASOE.** [End CB007326-A]\*\*\*\*

**[Before-CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB009881-CG] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.**[End CB009881-CG]\*\*\*\*

**[CNI-122313-A]**

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

**[End CNI-122313-A]**

**For L1 Thor:**

**[RP003187-A]**

Above functionalities shall be supported with TDD eCPRI fronthaul on **L1 Thor.**

**[End RP003187-A]**

**[CB010575-D] Above functionalities shall be supported on FR1 TDD CPRI** [End CB010575-D]\*\*\*\*

**[PR630013]For L1 on Loki, Thor** [PR634395] and Loner **[End PR634395]:**\*\*\*\*

At least the first one RACH occasion (corresponding to the first time and frequency index) shall be enabled in UlData\_PrachReceiveReq message otherwise the request shall be ignored by 5G\_L1\_UL.

**[End PR630013]**

**[CB009514-F] The requirement is also applicable for Thor(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e** [End CB009514-F]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\*

###### 5.2.4.6.5.1.3 Interworking

###### 5.2.4.6.5.1.3.1 Beamforming

**5.2.4.6.5.1.3.1.0-1**  (ID: `11446550`)

Beamforming
PRACH format 0 shall work for all FR1 TDD gNB deployment options. For beamforming deployments, only eCPRI fronthaul (FH) and radio units are considered. For non-beamforming deployments both CPRI and eCPRI FH and radio units are considered.

**[CB008325-5G-AA] On L1** Thor PRACH format 0 shall work with FR1 TDD eCPRI FH. TDD CPRI and beamforming are not requested to be supported. **[End CB008325-5G-AA]**\*\*\*\*

**[Before-CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB009881-CG] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE 1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.** [End CB009881-CG]\*\*\*\*

**[CNI-122313-A]**

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

**[End CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB009514-F] 5G-L1-UL(BB) shall support  for Thor(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e** [End CB009514-F]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\*

Channel multiplexing and UL buffering
PRACH format 0 shall interact with 5GC001348 (Channel multiplexing on PRACH slots), CB006064/CB007950 (long PUCCH TDD) and 5GC001120 (UL Buffering: Loner only).

**[RP003187-B, RP003187-I] The requirement is also valid for** L1 Thor. **[End RP003187-B, RP003187-I]**\*\*\*\*

**[CNI-122313-A]**

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

**[End CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB010969-SR-CB] This requirement shall be supported by L1 Thor in FR1-FDD-OBSAI.** [End CB010969-SR-CB]\*\*\*\*

**PRACH short format A2**

Three PRACH frequency/time occasions (0,0), (0,1), and (0,2) are available in one PRACH slot, as shown in the following figure:

where the first index is the frequency index and the second one is the time index.

Three PRACH frequency/time occasions (0,0), (0,1) and (0,2) are supported in one PRACH slot with starting symbol = 0.

The first element of the prachOccasions in UlData\_PrachReceiveReq array has value 0xE000, all the other elements of the array have value 0x0000.

For TDD FR1, one PRACH frequency/time occasion (0,0) is also supported with starting symbol = 9. The first element of the prachOccasions in UlData\_PrachReceiveReq array has value 0x8000, all the other elements of the array have value 0x0000.

##### 5.2.4.6.5.3 Format B4

###### 5.2.4.6.5.3.1 Time and frequency occasions

**PRACH short format B4**

**In Loner, Loki , and Thor one PRACH frequency/time occasion (0,0) is supported in one PRACH slot with starting symbol = 0 and 2.**

The first element of the *prachOccasions in* UlData\_PrachReceiveReq array has value 0x8000, all the other elements of the array have value 0x0000.\*\*

The background of the image is black.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_5271.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

For L1 on Loki, Thor and Loner:

At least the first one RACH occasion (corresponding to the first time and frequency index) shall be enabled in UlData\_PrachReceiveReq message otherwise the request shall be ignored by 5G\_L1\_UL.

**[CB010784-A] L1 in** Loki **[CB010784-D] and Thor** [End CB010784-D] when external delay compensation is active, i.e. the dedicated interface parameter **addExtDelayCompensation (refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_153\_replaced([11513459](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) has a non-zero value, only starting symbol 0 is supported.** [End CB010784-A]***\******\***

**[CB010575-D] 5G-L1-UL for FR1 TDD CPRI Thor shall support PRACH format B4 with the functionality described above** [End CB010575-D]\*\*\*\*

**[CB010988-B] For L1 in** Thor **with TDD FR1 CPRI** when external delay compensation is active, i.e. the dedicated interface parameter **addExtDelayCompensation (refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_153\_replaced([11513459](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) has a non-zero value, only starting symbol 0 is supported.** [End CB010988-B]***\******\***

**[CB009514-F] The requirement is also applicable for Thor(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e with the starting symbols {0,2} with** addExtDelayCompensation equals "0".  **[End CB009514-F]**\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

###### 5.2.4.6.6.1.1 Time and frequency occasions

**5.2.4.6.6.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11446795`)

Time and frequency occasions
**PRACH long format 0 for FDD**

In **Loner HW, starting from 5G19A (**5GC000836-E) PRACH long format 0 is supported. Time and frequency occasions to be processed are given by the field *prachOccasions in the* UlData\_PrachReceiveReq message.**\***\*

For long PRACH formats, there is a single time occasion per PRACH slot. Each element of the array should have value 0x0000 or 0x8000.

Each non-zero element of the array (i.e. 0x8000) corresponds to a valid PRACH occasion in the frequency domain.

Note that the slot size for PRACH format 0 is based on SCS 15 kHz.

**[5GC001868-D] For FDD, 5G-L1-UL shall also support PRACH long format 0 as above configurations and it shall also report the respective information to 5G-L2-PS as described above in** Loki L1 HW **[End 5GC001868-D]**\*\*\*\*

### 5.2.4.7 Coherent combining

#### 5.2.4.7.1 Overview

**5.2.4.7.1.0-1**  (ID: `11447032`)

Overview
In **TDD, to improve the PRACH detection performance and reduce the computation resources for short formats only, the PRACH sequence repetitions could be divided into several groups according to the parameter *prachCohCombLen received in \*UlCell\_SetupReq message.***\*

If *prachCohCombLen >1, the coherent combining is performed in each group before non-coherent combining of the groups. If* prachCohCombLen = 1, it means there’s no coherent combining.\*\*

For PRACH short formats:

* Preamble format A2, repetition number is 4, so the coherent combining size prachCohCombLen = 4 and group size equals to 1;
* Preamble format B4, repetition number is 12, so the coherent combining size prachCohCombLen = 4 and group size equals to 3;
* **[5GC001301-A] Preamble format C2, repetition number is 4, so the coherent combining size prachCohCombLen = 4 and group size equals to 1.** [End 5GC001301-A]\*\*\*\*

The PRACH coherent combining algorithms are described in section 2.5.4 of the 5GMax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**[5GC001868-A] 5G-L1-UL shall also support PRACH coherent combining algorithm and use the IE *prachCohCombLen as explained above, except that value is not configured by cellSetup. in **Loki L1 HW** [End 5GC001868-A]***\*\*\*\*

**[5GC002056-AA] In** Loki, L1 is expected to use different prachCohCombLen (different than the one provided in the UlCell\_SetupReq message), i.e. A2=4, C2=4 and B4=6 are being used currently. **[End 5GC002056-AA]**\*\*\*\*

**[CB007723-C/CB007539-B]**

Set value 12 for PRACH short formats B4 if cellExtension is set to 69:0-6.9 km [**CB007723-D/CB007539-B] or 110:5-11km. [**End CB007723-D/CB007539-B]\*\*\*\*

**[End CB007723-C/CB007539-B]**

**[CB008792-A, CB008827-5G-A] [FR1-TDD]**

If ~~MRBTS/NRBTS/NRCELL/~~actHighSpeedCell=TRUE

Set value 2 for PRACH short formats A2, B4 and C2.

**[End CB008792-A, CB008827-5G-A]**

~~Set value 4 for PRACH short formats A2,B4~~ ~~[CB007723-C]~~ ~~if rangeExtension is set to 10:1x\_range~~ ~~[End CB007723-C]~~ ~~and C2~~~~.~~ ~~Set value 1 for PRACH long formats 0.~~

Note: In case of eCPRI of Loki, eDEC decompress the frequency domain samples and forward the samples to FD AGC (TD path of PRCH is bypassed). The rest of the processing (blocks after FD AGC) are common between CPRI and eCPRI except the coherent combining. i.e. coherent combining (also known as preamble pre-combining) of repeated preambles is done outside PRACH IP block (in eDec) in Loki devices (this is different to ABIL where coherent combining is part of PRCH IP block). Pre-combined (coherently combined) FD samples are to FD AGC.

For PRACH long formats, *prachCohCombLen = 1 (applicable for Loner L1 HW, Loki L1 HW* *[RP003187-A, RP003187-H] and* *L1 Thor* *[End RP003187-A, RP003187-H]).***\***\*

**[RP003187-D] In** L1 Thor for PRACH short formats, L1 is expected to use different prachCohCombLen (different than the one provided in the UlCell\_SetupReq message), i.e. A2=4, C2=4 and B4=6 are being used currently.\*\*\*\*

**[End RP003187-D]**

**[Before-CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB009443-C] This requirement for format B4 shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.** [End CB009443-C]\*\*\*\*

**[CB009881-CG, CB009881-W] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.** In **Loki, L1 is expected to use different prachCohCombLen (different than the one provided in the UlCell\_SetupReq message), i.e. A2=4, C2=4 and B4=6 are being used currently.**[End CB009881-CG, CB009881-W]***\****\*

**[CNI-122313-A]**

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

**[End CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB010575-A] This requirement shall be supported in L1 Thor HW for FR1-TDD-CPRI.** [End CB010575-A]\*\*\*\*

**[CB009514-F] The requirement is also applicable for Thor(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e** [End CB009514-F]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\*

Supported values

  Format 1: {1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 8, 12}

  Format A2: {1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 8, 12}

  Format B4: {1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 8, 12}

  Format C2: {1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 8, 12}

  Format A2: {1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 8, 12}

  Format C2: {1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 8, 12}

  Format C0: {1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 8, 12}

  Format B4: {1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 8, 12}

### 5.2.4.8 PRACH bandwidth parts and scs

#### 5.2.4.8.1 PRACH scs

##### 5.2.4.8.1.1 SCS acquisition

**5.2.4.8.1.1.0-2**  (ID: `11447090`)

SCS acquisition
For PRACH short formats, 5G-L1-UL obtains the SCS value for PRACH channel from the parameter prachScs in message UlCell\_SetupReq (refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). ~~The SCS of PRACH is the same as that of data channel: for below 6GHz, the SCS of PRACH is 30kHz; for above 6GHz, the SCS of PRACH is 120kHz.~~

For PRACH long formats, the SCS of PRACH is directly obtained from the prach format itself as per 38.211 table 6.3.3.1-1.

**[Before 5GC001981-A,**5GC000580-F] For single antenna reception (example broken antenna scenario with 2RX nominal configuration), 5G-L1-UL uses the the IE *dtxThresholdPrachSingleRx (received in UlCell\_SetupReq message) for PRACH DTX detection.**[End 5GC001981-A, 5GC000580-F]***\***\*

**[Before 5GC001981-A,**5GC000836-K] For FDD, the broken antenna scenario has not been supported. Therefore, the IE *dtxThresholdPrachSingleRx is irrelevant to FDD. Only 2RX is supported for PRACH for FDD.**[End 5GC001981-A,**5GC000836-K]****\****\*

**[RP003187-A, RP003187-H] 5G-L1-UL shall also support *1.25kHz (prachScs=UNUSED) as explained above in **L1 Thor. Single antenna reception support for PRACH is not needed.** [End RP003187-A, RP003187-H]***\*\*\*\*

**[RP003187-B] 5G-L1-UL shall also support *prachScs=30kHz as explained above in **L1 Thor. Single antenna reception support for PRACH is not needed.** [End RP003187-B]***\*\*\*\*

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| *Technology* | *Feature / support* |
| FR1 FDD CPRI | supported |
| FR1 FDD OBSAI | **[CB010969-SR-CB] Supported** [End CB010969-SR-CB]\*\*\*\* |
| FR1 FDD 7-2a eCPRI | **[CB011178-A]Supported**[End CB011178-A]\*\*\*\* |
| FR1 TDD CPRI | **[CB010575-D] supported** [End CB010575-D]\*\*\*\* |
| FR1 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | supported |
| FR1 TDD 7-2e eCPRI | **[CB007595-B] supported (without single antenna reception)** [End CB007595-B]\*\*\*\* |

##### 5.2.4.8.1.2 Support overview

**5.2.4.8.1.2.0-2**  (ID: `13446465`)

Support overview
L1 shall support following PRACH subcarrier spacing:

For FDD (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-2):

·  Format 0: {1,25kHz}

·  Format 1: {1,25kHz }

For TDD FR1 (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-3):

·  Format 0: {1,25kHz }

·  Format A2: {30kHz}

·  Format B4: {30kHz }

·  Format C2: {15kHz, 30kHz}

For TDD FR2 (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-4):

·  Format A2: {120kHz}

·  Format C2: {120kHz }

·  Format C0: {120kHz }

·  Format B4: {120kHz }

L1 shall use parameter *UlCell\_SetupReq->prachConfig->prachScs  from L1 – 5G-CP-RT interface to define requested subcarrier spacing.*

If value of *prachScs  parameter is equal to {UNUSED} then L1 shall get real value of subcarrier spacing directly from 38.211 table 6.3.3.1-1 based on format.*

Note: currently, for value {UNUSED} it is used only {1,25kHz}.

#### 5.2.4.8.2 Bandwidth parts

##### 5.2.4.8.2.1 Carrier split principals

**5.2.4.8.2.1.0-2**  (ID: `11447141`)

Carrier split principals
In case of carrier split (after activation of CB006911-A), carriers below (and equal to) 50 MHz are expected to be split into two equal parts according to the configured SCS and carrier bandwidth. The 5G-L1-UL of Loki shall assume that the split is calculated on a sub-carrier basis. i.e. in case of 40 MHz with 216 PRBs and 15 kHz SCS, total number of sub-carriers (12 x 216 = 2592) is splitted into 2 carrier parts/AxCs each with 1296 sub-carriers (1296 = 12 x 216/2). The bandwidth of the resulting split carrier/AxC is 1296\*15 kHz = 19.44 MHz. The frequency offset of each part relative to the configured carrier frequency of 40 MHz carrier is +/- 9.72 MHz.

The requirement is also applicable for 40 MHz case for Thor for FR1-FDD-CPRI

[CB008935-A] The requirement is also applicable for 50 MHz case for Thor for FR1-FDD-CPRI.

In case of 50Mhz with 270 PRBs and 15 kHz SCS, total number of sub-carriers (12 x 270 = 3420) is splitted into 2 carrier parts/AxCs each with 1620 sub-carriers (1620 = 12 x 270/2). The bandwidth of the resulting split carrier/AxC is 1620\*15 kHz = 24.3 MHz. The frequency offset of each part relative to the configured carrier frequency of 50 MHz carrier is +/- 12.15 MHz. [End CB008935-A]

---

##### 5.2.4.8.2.2 Carrier split scenarios

###### 5.2.4.8.2.2.1 40MHz carrier split

###### 5.2.4.8.2.2.1.1 2 x 20MHz carriers

###### 5.2.4.8.2.2.1.1.0-1 2 x 20MHz carriers 5G-L1-UL of Loki [RP003187-M] and Thor [End RP003187-M] shall support FDD 40 MHz provided via 2x20 MHz carrier streams each with 30.72 Msps. The 5G-L1-UL shall assume PRACH occasion is located on one of the carrier 20 MHz carrier streams. (ID: 11447175)

###### 5.2.4.8.2.2.1.2 Sampling rate with CPRI compression

###### 5.2.4.8.2.2.1.2.0-1 Sampling rate with CPRI compression 5G-L1-UL of Loki [RP003187-M] and Thor [End RP003187-M] shall assume that CB006911-A/CB007146-A and CB006115-A are mutually exclusive. i.e. when CPRI compression feature is activated via CB006115-A, each 20 MHz streams of the 40 MHz supported via CB007146-A/CB006911-A will be processed with sampling rate 23.04 Msps. Otherwise (i.e. CB006115-A is not activated), the sampling rate of each 20 MHz carrier supported via CB006911-A/CB007146-A is 30.72 Msps. (ID: 11447188)

###### 5.2.4.8.2.2.2 50MHz carrier split

###### 5.2.4.8.2.2.2.0-1 50MHz carrier split 5G-L1-UL of Loki and Thor shall support FDD 50 MHz cell bandwidth provided via 2x25 MHz carrier streams each with 30.72 Msps. The 5G-L1-UL shall assume PRACH occasion is located on one of the carrier 25 MHz carrier streams. [CB011006] 5G-L1-UL of Loki and Thor shall support FDD 50 MHz cell bandwidth without carrier split. [End CB011006] (ID: 11447204)

### 5.2.4.9 PRACH stream eAxC allocations

**5.2.4.9.0-1**  (ID: `11447219`)

PRACH stream eAxC allocations
For PRACH reception, the number of streams (i.e., ceAxCId) follows the following:

*Note that N is the number of SSB's mapped to one RACH occasion as configured by the IE 'nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion' in the PrachConfig structure (refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_153\_replaced([11513459](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*

If N=1, the number of PRACH streams at the input of the DU is 4 for all subcells types except C2 where it is 2. If N>1, the number of PRACH streams is N\*2.

In detail, for TDD FR1 eCPRI 7.2a the PRACH spatial stream configurations are:

 For subcell type C2, when N=1 there are 2 PRACH streams, and when N>1 there are N\*2 PRACH streams.

 For subcell type C4, when N=1 there are 4 PRACH streams, and when N>1 there are N\*2 PRACH streams.

 For subcell type C8, when N=1 there are 4 PRACH streams, and when N>1 there are N\*2 PRACH streams.

**[CB010630-D] This requirement should also be supported in Thor for FR1 TDD 7-2e, for all the subcell types applicable in 7-2e split.** [End CB010630-D]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\*

---

### 5.2.4.10 Receiver algorithm tuning and configuration

#### 5.2.4.10.1 General aspects

**5.2.4.10.1.0-1**  (ID: `11447245`)

General aspects
**Receiver Configuration**

Upon reception of UlCell\_SetupReq message the L1-SW shall perform the following:

1) Extract PRACH cell specific parameters (5G\_L1\_3848\_replaced([11494413](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fEnGq_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) from UlCell\_SetupReq message

2) Calculate the configurable parameters for PRACH detection algorithm using the cell specific parameters and RAD tables

3) Calculate the PRACH detection thresholds

4) Write or configure the values into receiver entity

For the task details please refer the documents referenced in 5G\_L1\_3905\_replaced([11445864](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_zfIfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**[RP003187-A, RP003187-H] The requirement is also valid for** L1 Thor. **[End RP003187-A, RP003187-H]**\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\*

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |

| FR1 TDD CPRI | Supported |  |
| FR1 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported |  |
| FR2 TDD CPRI | Supported |  |
| FR2 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported |  |
| Loki | FR1 FDD CPRI | Supported |
| FR1 FDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported |  |
| FR1 TDD CPRI | Supported |  |
| FR1 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported |  |
| FR2 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported |  |

| FR1 FDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported |  |

#### 5.2.4.10.2 Receiver type and rx order

##### 5.2.4.10.2.1 Receiver type

**5.2.4.10.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11447270`)

Receiver type
For FR1 TDD CPRI, L1 in Loner shall support 4Rx MRC receiver:

-Inclusion of 4Rx

-DTX thresholds handling for 4Rx

-Broken antenna handling

Where dtx thresholds are calculated via run-time algorithm in which nRx is one of the input parameters.

Rx order support
**PRACH receiver algorithm**

**FDD:**

**TDD:**

**[5GC001848-A] Receivers with 4 and 2 antenna streams are supported. Use of 2Rx or 4Rx  is configurable per cell during cell setup phase by using IE ulSubcellType.**

**[End 5GC001848-A]**

Refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for configured ulSubcellType.

Note: The corresponding AxC mapping can be found in 5G\_UP\_2501.

##### 5.2.4.10.2.3 High speed and rx order

###### 5.2.4.10.2.3.1 C4

###### 5.2.4.10.2.3.1.1 Loner

**5.2.4.10.2.3.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11447319`)

Loner
As from 22R4, after activation of CB006662, the 5G-L1-UL of Loner shall process the PRACH restricted set for TDD FR1 as follows when C4 subcell is configured with eCPRI:

When ulSubcellType == C4 AND prachDtxThresholdSelection == 2Rx, the L1 shall process the Rx streams ceAxCIndex\_item\_0 and ceAxCIndex\_item\_1 for PRACH detection with 2Rx dtx thresholds.

When ulSubcellType == C4 AND prachDtxThresholdSelection == 4Rx, the L1 shall process the Rx streams ceAxCIndex\_item\_0, ceAxCIndex\_item\_1, ceAxCIndex\_item\_2 and ceAxCIndex\_item\_3 for PRACH detection with 4Rx dtx thresholds.

Please note that above requirement is valid only for BF eCPRI RU. i.e. when BF is not enabled, prachDtxThresholdSelection is expected to be 4Rx.

---

###### 5.2.4.10.2.3.2 C8 and 7.2e subcell types

###### 5.2.4.10.2.3.2.1 Thor

**5.2.4.10.2.3.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11447343`)

Thor
When C8 subcell is configured and actHighSpeedCell=True in UlCell\_SetupReq,  L1 shall support  4Rx PRACH

**[CB012115-IA]  The support for 4Rx PRACH is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-GA] In 7.2e subcell types. the support for 4Rx PRACH is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\*

---

#### 5.2.4.10.3 PRACH reception with beamforming for TDD FR1

##### 5.2.4.10.3.1 Processing for C4 subcell type

###### 5.2.4.10.3.1.1 Loner and Loki

**5.2.4.10.3.1.1.0-2**  (ID: `11447383`)

Loner and Loki
**PRACH Reception with Beamforming for TDD FR1**

For beamforming and C4 subcell type (reception with 4 spatial streams, i.e, ceAxCId) case and for **[CB012192-A] one SSB per RO (RACH Occasion) mapping** [End CB012192-A]:\*\*\*\*

* PRACH signal received from the 2 spatial streams associated to the 2nd beam duplicates the signal received from 2 spatial streams associated to the 1st beam (more precisely the PRACH associated SSB beam).
* Due to the signal duplication, the PRACH reception via 4 spatial antenna streams could be seen as reception with 2RX antennas.

The processing of the signal associated to the 2nd beam depends on the L1 HWs as given in the following table:

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **L1 HW** | **PRACH received in the spatial streams associated to the 1**st **beam**\*\*\*\* | **PRACH received in the spatial streams associated to the 2**nd **beam**\*\*\*\* | **First Feature** |
| **Loner** | Processed | Processed for unrestricted set, ignored for restricted set type A |  |
| **Loki** | Processed | Ignored |  |

See also 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6364\_replaced([11106032](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koS33PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**[CB012192-A] Note: if multiple SSBs are mapped to one RO, refer to 5G\_L1\_17019\_replaced([11447536](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_7a9vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details on the PRACH stream processing.** [End CB012192-A]\*\*\*\*

---

###### 5.2.4.10.3.1.2 Thor, Odin

**5.2.4.10.3.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `11447399`)

Thor, Odin
**PRACH Reception with Beamforming for TDD FR1**

For beamforming and C4 subcell type **(reception with 4 spatial antenna streams) case:**

* PRACH signal received from the 2 spatial streams associated to the 2nd beam duplicates the signal received from 2 spatial streams associated to the 1st beam (more precisely the PRACH associated SSB beam).
* Due to the signal duplication, the PRACH reception via 4 spatial antenna streams could be seen as reception with 2RX antennas.

**[CB007487-C]L1 Thor shall process the PRACH received in the spatial streams associated to the 1st beam and ignore the streams associated to the 2nd beam. See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6364\_replaced([11106032](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koS33PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).** [End CB007487-C]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\*

---

##### 5.2.4.10.3.2 Processing for C8 and 7.2e subcell type

**5.2.4.10.3.2.0-2**  (ID: `11447425`)

Processing for C8 and 7.2e subcell type
**PRACH Reception with Beamforming for TDD FR1**

**[CB012192-A] With one SSB to RO (RACH Occasion) mapping** [End CB012192-A], for beamforming and C4 subcell type **or C8 subcell type (reception with 4 spatial antenna streams) case:**\*\*\*\*

* PRACH signal received from the 2 spatial streams (i.e., ceAxCId) associated to the 2nd beam duplicates the signal received from 2 spatial streams associated to the 1st beam (more precisely the PRACH associated SSB beam).
* Due to the signal duplication, the PRACH reception via 4 spatial antenna streams could be seen as reception with 2RX antennas.

L1 Thor shall process the PRACH received in the spatial streams associated to the 1st beam and ignore the streams associated to the 2nd beam. See 5G\_UP\_ALG\_6364\_replaced([11106032](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koS33PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| *Technology* | *Feature / support* |
| FR1 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | supported |
| FR1 TDD 7-2e eCPRI | **[CB010630-D] supported** [End CB010630-D]\*\*\*\* |
| FR1 TDD CPRI | supported |

**[CB012192-A] Note: if multiple SSBs are mapped to one RO, refer to 5G\_L1\_17019\_replaced([11447536](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_7a9vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details on the PRACH stream processing.** [End CB012192-A]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-GA] For 7.2e subcell types and reception of 4Rx PRACH, the requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\*

#### 5.2.4.10.4 pfa target

##### 5.2.4.10.4.1 Support overview

###### 5.2.4.10.4.1.1 pfaTarget acquisition

**5.2.4.10.4.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11447456`)

pfaTarget acquisition
L1 **ABIL/Loki shall support all the pfaTargetPrachId values specified in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1277/5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1278:**

0: none;

1: 0.01;

2: 0.001;

3: 0.0005;

4: 0.0001;

5: 0.005;

6: 0.05;

7: 0.1

Note: The value 0 does not map to any real pfa target, it means 5G-L1-UL shall use pre-stored DTX threshold instead of run time calculation.

When pfaTargetPrachId = none (0), the L1-SW shall obtain the pre-calculated values for given configuration (prachFormat, number of Rx antennas, prachCohCombLen and zeroCorrelationConfigIndex/Ncs) from a RAD file (rd\_thresholds.conf) and write those into L1-FPGA (for ABIL) and PRACH receiver entity (ABIO) without any modifications. As stated the value depends on parameters such as prachFormat, Pfa, Number of Rx antennas, prachCohCombLen and zeroCorrelationConfigIndex. The pre-computed values associated with pfaTargetPrachId = 0.0005 and rdPrachThresholOffsetDb  = 1 dB are relevant as from 5G19B.

**[CB007814-G] This requirement also applies to ABIO FR1-FDD-eCPRI.** [End CB007814-G]\*\*\*\*

**[Before-CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB009881-CG] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.**[End CB009881-CG]\*\*\*\*

**[CB009444-B] This requirement is applicable for RINLINE1 for FR1-FDD-eCPRI.** [End CB009444-B]\*\*\*\*

**[CNI-122313-A]**

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

**[End CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-LA]\*\*\*\*

#### 5.2.4.10.6 SSB and RACH Occasion multiplexing

##### 5.2.4.10.6.1 Supported mapping

**5.2.4.10.6.1.0-1**  (ID: `11447520`)

Supported mapping
In Loki and Thor **TDD FR1 with BF enabled, in addition to the legacy one-to-one mapping the gNB shall also support the mapping of multiple SSB beams to one PRACH occasion. The SSB per PRACH occasion configuration can be:**

ssb-perRACH-Occasion = {1, 2, or 4}.

The support for multiple SSB mapping to one occasion shall be available for PRACH formats: long format 0 (1.25kHz SCS), short format B4 (30kHz SCS) and short format C2(with 30KHz or 15KHz PRACH SCS).

The number of SSBs mapped to a RO is a cell level configuration carried by the IE 'nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion' in the PrachConfig structure (refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_153\_replaced([11513459](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**[CB010630-D] 5G-L1-UL shall support this requirement for Thor and FR1 TDD eCPRI 7-2e split.** [End CB010630-D]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\*

---

##### 5.2.4.10.6.2 Reciever configuration

**5.2.4.10.6.2.0-1**  (ID: `11447536`)

Reciever configuration
The PRACH processing is according to the following in cases where multiple SSBs are mapped one RO (RACH Occasion).

For each RO, the gNB-DU shall receive the PRACH signal from 2*M spatial streams (i.e., ceAxCId), where M is the number of SSBs mapped to the RO (Refer to the* *eCpriConfig structure* *in 5G\_L1\_IF\_15392\_replaced([11514303](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2oWfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).*\*\*\*

The receiver consists of M sub-receivers, each sub-receiver shall process 2 continuous spatial streams (i.e., 2rx per SSB) and detect the preambles associated with the SSB using 2rx dtx threshold.

There are totalNumberOfRAPreambles/N preambles associated to one SSB with range: m*(totalNumberOfPreambles/N) … (m+1)*(totalNumberOfPreambles/N)-1 where m=0,…,M-1, N is the SSB-occassion mapping as configured in the IE 'nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion' (5G\_L1\_IF\_153\_replaced([11513459](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and the total number of RA preambles as configured in the IE 'totalNumberOfRAPreambles' (5G\_L1\_IF\_153\_replaced([11513459](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Note: for any given occasion M<=N.

Each sub-receiver shall identify all the roots which are used to generate the preamble range assigned to the SSB according to the root sequence and cyclic shift configurations (refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1435\_replaced([11105620](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koNYSvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the sub-receiver shall perform PRACH reception for all the preambles related to the identified roots, for details refer to section "8.1.2 Sector Beam Based Beamforming" of the 5GMax Massive MIMO Algorithm Specification (5G\_UP\_ALG\_700\_replaced([11101361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knWcsvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Finally, the sub-receiver shall filter out a total of 'totalNumberOfRAPreambles/N' preambles that are assigned to the SSB.

**[CB010630-D] The requirement shall be supported for Thor and FR1 TDD in eCPRI 7-2e split.** [End CB010630-D]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\*

---

#### 5.2.4.10.7 Threshold offset determination and adjustments

##### 5.2.4.10.7.1 Dtx threshold determination

###### 5.2.4.10.7.1.1 prachDtxThresholdSelection

###### 5.2.4.10.7.1.1.1 Loner

**5.2.4.10.7.1.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11447573`)

Loner
For the dtx threshold, calculation the L1-SW in Loner (after introduction of 5GC002244 in 5G21A), ABIO (after introduction of 5GC001294 in 5G21A) [CB007326-A]and ASOE [End CB007326-A] shall use the value received in IE prachDtxThresholdSelection. For example in case of BF on TDD FR1 ulSubcellType can indicate ulSubcellType as C4 (4Rx) but prachDtxThresholdSelection can be 2Rx. In this case, L1 is expected to perform 4Rx with 2Rx threshold.

[Before-CNI-122313-A]

[CB009443-C] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI without BF, i.e. prachDtxThresholdSelection cannot be 2Rx.[End CB009443-C]

[CNI-122313-A]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313-A]

---

###### 5.2.4.10.7.1.1.2 Loki, Thor, Odin

###### 5.2.4.10.7.1.1.2.1 Dependency to ulSubcellType

###### 5.2.4.10.7.1.1.2.1.1 C4

**5.2.4.10.7.1.1.2.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11447586`)

C4
The **L1-SW in** Loki and **[RP003187-B] Thor [End RP003187-B] (after introduction of 5GC001294 in 5G21A) shall use the value received in IE "prachDtxThresholdSelection" to select the number of Rx antennas to be processed in case of BF on TDD FR1 when ulSubcellType indicates ulSubcellType as C4 (4Rx) but prachDtxThresholdSelection is 2Rx. In this case, L1 is expected to perform 2Rx MRC with 2Rx threshold. i.e. following scenarios are possible in case of 4Rx MRC:**\*\*\*\*

• When ulSubcellType == C4 **[PR617917]~~(numCeAxCIndex of UlData\_PrachReceiveReq is 4 )~~**[End PR617917]\*\*\*\*

AND prachDtxThresholdSelection == 2Rx, the L1 shall process the the Rx streams ceAxCIndex\_item\_0 and ceAxCIndex\_item\_1 for PRACH detection with 2Rx dtx thresholds.

• When ulSubcellType == C4**[PR617917]~~(numCeAxCIndex of UlData\_PrachReceiveReq is 4 )~~**[End PR617917] AND prachDtxThresholdSelection == 4Rx, the L1 shall process the Rx streams ceAxCIndex\_item\_0, ceAxCIndex\_item\_1, ceAxCIndex\_item\_2 and ceAxCIndex\_item\_3 for PRACH detection with 4Rx dtx thresholds.\*\*\*\*

**[Before-CNI-122313]**

**[CB009443-C] This requirement above shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI without BF.**[End CB009443-C]\*\*\*\*

**[CNI-122313]**

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

**[End CNI-122313]**

**[CB011178-A] 5G-L1-UL shall also support requirements above for FR1 FDD 7-2a eCPRI for Thor.** [End CB011178-A]\*\*\*\*

**[CB009514-F] The requirement is also applicable for Thor(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e** [End CB009514-F]\*\*\*\*

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | **Thor** | **Loki** | **Odin** |
| **FR1-FDD-CPRI** |  |  |  |
| **FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI** | Supported |  |  |
| **FR1-FDD-OBSAI** |  |  |  |
| **FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI** |  | Supported | **[CB012115-IA] Supported**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\* |
| **FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI** | Supported |  | **[CB012115-GA] Supported**[End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\* |

###### 5.2.4.10.7.1.1.2.1.2 A8

###### 5.2.4.10.7.1.1.2.1.2.0-1 A8 L1SW for the ulSubcellType == A8 shall accept only prachDtxThresholdSelection == 2Rx and reject the CellSetup if prachDtxThresholdSelection is set to any other value. (ID: 12874839)

###### 5.2.4.10.7.1.2 dtx Threshold calculation

###### 5.2.4.10.7.1.2.1 TDD FR1

**5.2.4.10.7.1.2.1.0-2**  (ID: `11447617`)

TDD FR1
For TDD (which supports PRACH long and short formats) L1-SW in Thor shall calculate dtx thresholds for 1 to NRx antennas configured (e.g. 1...4 in case of 4Rx) for preamble detection algorithm implemented in HW. Where number of RX antennas configured shall be deduced from ulSubcellType parameter of UlCell\_SetupReq message. The dtx threshold calculation requires pfaTargetPrachId,  zeroCorrelationConfigIndex, prachCohCombLen and prachFormat (in addition to number of Rx antennas) from UlCell\_SetupReq message.

**[RP003187-B] The requirement is also valid for TDD FR1 eCPRI for** L1 Thor. **[End RP003187-B].**\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\*

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| *Technology* | *Feature / support* |
| FR1 TDD CPRI | Supported |
| FR1 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | supported |
| FR1 TDD 7-2e eCPRI | **[CB007595-B] supported** [End CB007595-B]\*\*\*\* |

---

###### 5.2.4.10.7.1.2.2 FDD

**5.2.4.10.7.1.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `11447633`)

FDD
For FDD (which supports PRACH long formats) L1-SW (**Loner, Loki [RP003187-I] and Thor [End RP003187-I]) shall calculate dtx thresholds for single Rx antenna and for Rx antenna configured (e.g. 2Rx or 4Rx) for preamble detection. Where single antenna threshold is required for MAD algorithm. i.e. Single antenna threshold is used as AntInactiveThresDb\_FDD. The number of RX antennas configured shall be deduced from ulSubcellType parameter of UlCell\_SetupReq message. The dtx threshold calculation requires pfaTargetPrachId and zeroCorrelationConfigIndex (in addition to number of Rx antennas) from UlCell\_SetupReq message.**

**[RP003187-I] The requirement is also valid for** L1 Thor. **[End RP003187-I]**\*\*\*\*

**[CB007814-G] This requirement also applies to ABIO FR1-FDD-eCPRI.** [End CB007814-G]\*\*\*\*

**[CB008205-B, CB008205-C] 5G-L1-UL shall also support requirements above in ABIO for O-RAN compliant FR1 FDD eCPRI.**[End CB008205-B, CB008205-C]\*\*\*\*

**[CB009444-B] This requirement is applicable for RINLINE1 for FR1-FDD-eCPRI.** [End CB009444-B]\*\*\*\*

**[CB011178-A] 5G-L1-UL shall also support requirements above for FR1 FDD 7-2a eCPRI for Thor.** [End CB011178-A]\*\*\*\*

|  |  |  |  |  |

| **FR1-FDD-CPRI** | Supported | Supported | Supported | **[CB012115-JA]Supported**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\* |
| **FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI** | **[CB011178-A] Supported** [End CB011178-A]\*\*\*\* | **[CB007814-G] Supported** [End CB007814-G]\*\*\*\* | **-** | **[CB012115-LA]Supported**[End CB012115-LA]\*\*\*\* |
| **FR1-FDD-OBSAI** | **[CB010969-SR-CB] Supported** [End CB010969-SR-CB]\*\*\*\* |  |  |  |

##### 5.2.4.10.7.2 Offset adjustments

###### 5.2.4.10.7.2.1 Loner

###### 5.2.4.10.7.2.1-1 Loner

###### 5.2.4.10.7.2.1-2 Loner

#### 5.2.4.10.8 Support for external delay

##### 5.2.4.10.8.1 Overview

**5.2.4.10.8.1.0-1**  (ID: `11447688`)

Overview
In Loki [**CB010784-D] and Thor** [End CB010784-D], the 5G-L1-UL shall support **CB010784: FR1 TDD cell support for 3rd party delay compensation, which is designed to serve ring cell deployments. The PRACH ring cell algorithm can support the following deployment scenarios.**\*\*\*\*

 the ring cell starting point is configured with a shift that corresponds to the air delay (from the gNB to the ring cell starting point), as described in 5G\_UP\_7842.

 the ring cell starting point is configured with a shift that corresponds to the external DAS delay (from the gNB (BBU+RU, excluding remote antennae) to the RRUs), as described in 5G\_UP\_7849.

From the PRACH receiver algorithm's point of view, both scenarios are considered as ring cell deployments.

In order to support the ring cell deployments, a configurable delay is added to the time offset which indicates the start of the PRACH data sequence. Furthermore, after preamble detection, the initial TA estimation shall be adjusted to incorporate the configured external delay.

Details of the PRACH ring cell algorithm are described in section "2.5.26 Processing for CB010784" of the 5GMax algorithm specification (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_695\_replaced([11101310](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knWcovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). If the configured external delay exceeds a certain amount, performance degradation can occur, for details on the performance impacts, refer to "the performance degradation for UE with far distance in CB010784 v8.pptx" with link at <https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:p:/r/sites/ASCOP/AS%20Documents/FS1TAs-CFAMs/CB/CB010500%20-%20CB010999/CFAM/CB010784%20FR1%20TDD%20cell%20support%20for%203rd%20party%20delay%20compensation/Additional_materials/the%20performance%20degradation%20for%20UE%20with%20far%20distance%20in%20CB010784%20v8.pptx?d=wd8401aba657e449a845ee0a603a84220&csf=1&web=1&e=CPb0CH> .

The ring cell support is enabled if the value of the IE addExtDelayCompensation is non-zero. L1 receives the addExtDelayCompensation IE in the UL cell setup request message, for details concerning the IE, refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_153\_replaced([11513459](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The ring cell deployment support is restricted to PRACH format B4, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_21124\_replaced([11105963](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koSQw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The supported configuration is as below:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | **Loner** | **Loki** | **Thor** | **Thor RU** | Odin |
| **FR1-TDD-CPRI** | **-** | supported | **[CB010988-B]** supported **[End CB010988-B]** | **-** |  |
| **FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCRPI** | **-** | supported | supported | **-** | **[CB012115-IA]** Supported [End **CB012115-IA]** |
| **FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCRPI** | **-** | **-** | **-** | **-** | **[CB012115-GA]** Supported [End **CB012115-GA]** |

---

##### 5.2.4.10.8.2 Supported values

**5.2.4.10.8.2.0-1**  (ID: `11447706`)

Supported values
L1 shall support following PRACH additional external delay:

For FDD:

 Format 0: 0 us

 Format 1: 0 us

For TDD FR1:

 Format 0: 0 us

 Format A2: 0 us

 Format B4: from 0 to 203 us with step size  0.1us

 Format C2: 0 us

For TDD FR2:

 Format A2: 0 us

 Format C2: 0 us

 Format C0: 0 us

 Format B4: 0 us

L1 shall use parameter *UlCell\_SetupReq->prachConfig-> addExtDelayCompensation from L1 – 5G-CP-RT interface to define requested value.*

L1 on Loner shall ignore this parameter.

L1 on Loki and Thor shall ignore this parameter for all formats for FDD, for all formats for TDD FR2, and for formats *{0, A2, C2}  for TDD FR1.*

1 unit of *addExtDelayCompensation parameter = 0.1us.*

Min  supported value of *addExtDelayCompensation = 0 (0 us)*

Max supported value of *addExtDelayCompensation = 2030*(230 us)\*\*

Default value = 0.

Supported values for *addExtDelayCompensation*parameter for different L1 HW and technologies for FR1 FDD are shown in the table:\*\*

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| L1 HW and technologies |  | *prachFormat 0* | *prachFormat 1* |
| Loner | FR1-FDD-CPRI | ignored | ignored |
| Loki | FR1-FDD-CPRI |  |  |
| FR1-FDD-OBSAI |  |  |  |
| FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI |  |  |  |
| Thor BB | FR1-FDD-CPRI |  |  |
| **[CB010754] FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI** [End CB010754]\*\*\*\* |  |  |  |
| **[CB010578] FR1-FDD-OBSAI** [End CB010578]\*\*\*\* |  |  |  |
| Odin | **[CB012115-JA] FR1-FDD-CPRI**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\* | ignored | ignored |
| **[CB012115-LA] FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI**[End CB012115-LA]\*\*\*\* |  |  |  |

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

##### 5.2.4.10.8.3 Supported format

**5.2.4.10.8.3.0-1**  (ID: `11447729`)

Supported format
The supported PRACH formats for CB010784-FR1 TDD cell deployment with 3rd Party System delay compensation is given as follows:

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **PRACH format** | **PRACH SCS** | **Maximum Cell size (PRACH cell coverage) [m]** | **Maximum cell range (distance corresponding to the external delay + maximum cell size) [m]** | **First Feature** |
| short format B4 | 30 kHz | 1933 | Approximately 22000 (using the speed of light in fiber) or 32360 (using the speed of light in vacuum) | CB010784 |

When external delay compensation (synonymous with ring cell delay compensation) is active, i.e. the dedicated interface parameter **addExtDelayCompensation (refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_153\_replaced([11513459](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) has a non-zero value,, the supported PRACH configuration indices are:**

o Indices: 145, 146, 148, 152, 157, 159, 161

**Note: for detailed feature level design information on supported config indices, refer to the sub-chapter on PRACH configuration located inside CFAM 1.1.2 Feature Overview. The L1 SW shall not implement any explicit checking on the configuration index, i.e., no checking by L1 concerning whether the config index is one of the above-listed values. From system perspective, the config indices listed above are recommended for use when the external delay compensation feature is active. If a config index other than the feature recommended ones is used when the feature is active, there may be performance degradations such as detection errors.**

The supported configuration is as below:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | **Loner** | **Loki** | **Thor** | **Thor RU** | Odin |
| **FR1-TDD-CPRI** | **-** | supported | **[CB010988-B]** supported **[End CB010988-B]** | **-** |  |
| **FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCRPI** | **-** | supported | supported | **-** | **[CB012115-IA]** supported **[End CB012115-IA]** |
| **FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCRPI** | **-** | **-** | **-** | **-** | **[CB012115-GA]** supported **[End CB012115-GA]** |

#### 5.2.4.10.9 Support for high speed cells

##### 5.2.4.10.9.1 PRACH sequence type restricted set A

**5.2.4.10.9.1.0-1**  (ID: `11447753`)

PRACH sequence type restricted set A
**[CB006662-A, CB009027-5G-A]**

L1 **Loner/Loki/[CB009027-5G-A]Thor**[End CB009027-5G-A], FR1-TDD-CPRI, FR1-TDD-eCPRI, shall use highspeed PRACH preamble detector (see section '2.5.20.3 highspeed' of 5GMax algorithm specification, v.10.196 for **Loner, section '2.5.20.6 LokiPRCH' for** Loki (5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))) and **[CB009027-5G-A] section '2.5.20.7' ThorPRCH for** Thor **[End CB009027-5G-A] in case of restricted set type A (prachSequenceType = restrictedTypeA).*****\******\***
