#### 5.2.4.10.10 Support for extended cells

##### 5.2.4.10.10.1 Overview

**5.2.4.10.10.1.0-1**  (ID: `11447801`)

Overview
L1 shall support following PRACH extended cell range:

For FDD:

 Format 0: {normal mode}

 Format 1: {normal mode}

For TDD FR1:

 Format 0: {normal mode}

 Format A2: {normal mode}

 Format B4: {normal mode}

 Format C2: {normal mode}

For TDD FR2:

 Format A2: {normal mode, 6.9 km}

 Format C2: {normal mode, 2.3 km, 6.9 km}

 Format C0: {normal mode, 6.9 km}

 Format B4: {normal mode, 6.9 km, 5.5~11 km, **[CB014188-A] 0~11km**[End CB014188-A]}\*\*\*\*

L1 shall use parameter *UlCell\_SetupReq->prachConfig-> cellExtension  from L1 – 5G-CP-RT interface to define requested value.*

The mapping of this parameter is as follows:

10: normal mode;

23: extended range of 0~2.3 km;

69: extended range of 0~6.9 km;

110: extended  range of 5.5~11km;

**[CB014188-A] 115: extended  range of 0~11km**[End CB014188-A]\*\*\*\*

Supported values for *cellExtension  parameter for different L1 HW and technologies for FR1 FDD are shown in the table:*

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| L1 HW and technologies |  | *prachFormat 0* | *prachFormat 1* |
| Loner | FR1-FDD-CPRI | {10} | {10} |
| Loki | FR1-FDD-CPRI |  |  |
| FR1-FDD-OBSAI |  |  |  |
| FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI |  |  |  |
| Thor BB | FR1-FDD-CPRI |  |  |
| **[CB010754] FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI** [End CB010754]\*\*\*\* |  |  |  |
| **[CB010578] FR1-FDD-OBSAI** [End CB010578]\*\*\*\* |  |  |  |
| Odin | **[CB012115-JA] FR1-FDD-CPRI[End CB012115-JA]** |  |  |

**[CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\*

Supported values for *cellExtension  parameter for different L1 HW and technologies for FR1 TDD are shown in the table:*

|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| L1 HW and technologies |  | *prachFormat 0* | *prachFormat A2* |  | *prachFormat B4* | *prachFormat C2* |
| Loner | FR1-TDD-CPRI | {10} |  | {10} | {10} | {10} |
| FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| Loki | FR1-TDD-CPRI |  |  |  |  |  |
| FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| Thor | FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI |  |  |  |  |  |
| **[CB010575-D] FR1-TDD-CPRI** [End CB010575-D]\*\*\*\* |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI | **[CB005914-F]**  {10}  **[End CB005914-F]** |  | **[CB005914-F]**  {10}  **[End CB005914-F]** | **[CB007595-B] {10}** [End CB007595-B]\*\*\*\* | **[CB005914-F]**  {10}  **[End CB005914-F]** |  |
| Odin | **[CB012115-IA] FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI** [End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\* | {10} |  | {10} | {10} | {10} |
| **[CB012115-GA] FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI** [End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\* |  |  |  |  |  |  |
|  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

Supported values for *cellExtension  parameter for different L1 HW and technologies for FR2 are shown in the table:*

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| L1 HW and technologies |  | *prachFormat A2* | *prachFormat C2* | *prachFormat C0* | *prachFormat B4* |
| Loner | FR2-TDD-CPRI | {10} | {10, 23} | Not supported | Not supported |
| FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Not supported | Not supported |  |  |  |
| Loki | FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | {10} | {10, 69, 110, **[CB014188-A]**  (Thor) 115}  **[End CB014188-A]** } |  |  |
| Thor | **[CB010576] FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI** [End CB010576]\*\*\*\* |  |  |  |  |

---

##### 5.2.4.10.10.2 Cell extension configuration

###### 5.2.4.10.10.2.1 Format C2

###### 5.2.4.10.10.2.1.0-1 Format C2 For the extended cell range support (CB007462), control plane shall introduce a new IE cellExtension in the UlCell_SetupReq message to indicate if extended cell range is activated. e.g. if cellExtension = 10 then normal mode and cellExtension = 23 extended range of 2.3 km. The valid range of cellExtension is {10,23} and no other values shall be supported. [CB010576-D] This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.[End CB010576-D] (ID: 11447828)

###### 5.2.4.10.10.2.2 Format B4

###### 5.2.4.10.10.2.2.0-2 Format B4 For the extended cell range 6.9 km and 5~11km and [ CB014188-A] 0~11km [End CB014188-A] support,  control plane shall set cellExtension = 69 or 110  [ CB014188-A] or 115 [End CB014188-A] in the UlCell_SetupReq message to indicate if extended cell range 6.9 km or cell range 5~11km [ CB014188-A] or cell range 0~11km [End CB014188-A] feature are activated.  e.g. if cellExtension = 10 then normal mode, if cellExtension = 69 then extended range of 6.9 km and if cellExtension = 110 then extended range = 5~11km and [ CB014188-A] if cellExtension = 115 then extended range = 0~11km [End CB014188-A]. The valid range of cellExtension is {10,23, 69, 110, [ CB014188-A] 115} [End CB014188-A]} and no other values shall be supported. * * * * This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI. (ID: 12732634)

##### 5.2.4.10.10.3 L1-L2 interface impact

###### 5.2.4.10.10.3.1 Format C2

###### 5.2.4.10.10.3.1.0-1 Format C2 For extended cell range (CB007462), there is no L1/L2 interface change. Both prachOccasions can be enabled. [CB010576-D] This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.[End CB010576-D] (ID: 11447869)

###### 5.2.4.10.10.3.2 Format B4

###### 5.2.4.10.10.3.2.0-2 Format B4 For extended cell range 0~11km , a new enumeration value (115) is introduced in the cellExtension parameter. (ID: 12732630)

##### 5.2.4.10.10.4 Limitations

###### 5.2.4.10.10.4.1 number of cells

**5.2.4.10.10.4.1.0-1**  (ID: `11447910`)

number of cells
L1 in Loki (CB007723-A/C)  shall support:

1. The number of TDD FR2 subcell per Loki shall not exceed 4 starting from 22R2 (CB006950: 2 sectors FR2 8ccDL4ccUL 2T2R; one sector 8ccDL4ccUL per Loki, total 2 sectors per ABIO).
2. The L1-Loki shall support up to 4 TDD FR2 subcell with extended range.

---

###### 5.2.4.10.10.4.2 zero correlation zone config

###### 5.2.4.10.10.4.2.1 Format C2

###### 5.2.4.10.10.4.2.1.0-1 Format C2 For the extended cell range (CB007462), L1 shall support prachZeroCorrelationZoneConfig = 0 with extended cell range (when nSlidingWindows !=0). L1 shall log the error (in the L1 journal) if prachZeroCorrelationZoneConfig received from control plane is other than zero when extended cell range feature is activated (i.e. when cellExtension = 23) [CB010576-D] This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.[End CB010576-D] (ID: 11447935)

###### 5.2.4.10.10.4.2.2 Format B4

###### 5.2.4.10.10.4.2.2.0-1 Format B4 For the extended cell range (CB007723-A/C and CB007723-D), L1 shall support prachZeroCorrelationZoneConfig = 0 with extended cell range (when CB007723 A/C is activated with cellExtension == 69 or CB007723-D is activated with cellExtension == 110). L1 shall log the error (in the L1 journal) if prachZeroCorrelationZoneConfig received from control plane is other than zero when extended cell range feature is activated (i.e. when CB007723 A/C is activated with cellExtension == 69 or CB007723-D activated with cellExtension == 110) [CB010576-D] This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.[End CB010576-D] (ID: 11447951)

##### 5.2.4.10.10.5 Use cases

###### 5.2.4.10.10.5.1 Format C2

###### 5.2.4.10.10.5.1.0-1 Format C2 5G-L1-UL of Loner and Loki shall support CB007462: Extended FR2 cell-range which is designed to serve Fixed Wireless Access deployments, but it does not exclude eMBB (enhanced Mobile Broadband) users. [CB010576-D] This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.[End CB010576-D] (ID: 11447975)

###### 5.2.4.10.10.5.2 Format B4

###### 5.2.4.10.10.5.2.0-1 Format B4 5G-L1-UL of Loki shall support CB007723: Extended FR2 cell-range which is designed to serve Fixed Wireless Access depolyments, but it does not exclude eMBB (enhanced Mobile Broadband)  users. [CB010576-D] This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.[End CB010576-D] (ID: 11447992)

##### 5.2.4.10.10.6 Processing considerations

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.1 Extended FR2 cell range with C2 format

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.1.1 Parameter settings

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.1.1.1 Rad parameter disabling

**5.2.4.10.10.6.1.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11448031`)

Rad parameter disabling
The L1-SW (Loner and Loki) shall disable the following when cellExtension = 23 (CB007462):

a. rdInitialTaValidity = OFF

b. rdGuardShort (Loki) = 0

c. rdGuard (Loner) = 0

[CB010576-D] This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.[End CB010576-D]

---

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.1.1.2 rdSwoffset

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.1.1.2.1 Loner

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.1.1.2.1.0-1 Loner L1-SW of 5G-L1-UL in Loki and Loner shall have new RAD parameters rdSwOffsetShortFormat and rdSwOffsetTsSF with 0 as default values use rdSwoffset = 0 when cellExtension = 23. (ID: 11448055)

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.1.1.2.2 Loki

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.1.1.2.2.0-2 Loki UL repetition for cell ranges 11 km in FR2 [CB014188] UL repetition shall be enabled for cell ranges 11 km (cellExtension == 115) to support coverage extension. [End CB014188] (ID: 12721847)

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.1.2 Processing procedures

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.1.2.1 Loner

**5.2.4.10.10.6.1.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11448093`)

Loner
In Loner, the L1-SW of 5G-L1-UL shall perform the following steps for extended cell range CB007462:

a. Collect the results from both windows

b. Follow the algorithm steps defined in Section 3.11.4 of 5G New Radio Algorithm Specification PRACH channel (<https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:b:/r/sites/L1AS/5GFAST/Shared%20Documents/Fixed%20point%20algorithm%20specifications/5G21B> ).

---

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.1.2.2 Loki, Thor

**5.2.4.10.10.6.1.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `11448109`)

Loki, Thor
In Loki, the L1-SW of 5G-L1-UL shall perform the following steps for extended cell range CB007462:

a.Collect the results from both windows

b.Perform preamble validity check per window per occasion as per 5G21A implementation.

c.Follow the algorithm steps defined in Section 2.5.16 of the 5GMax algorithm definition (<https://nokia.sharepoint.com/sites/5gmax/Shared> Documents/GeneralDocuments/5G Algorithm Specifications).

[CB010576-D] This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.[End CB010576-D]

---

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.1.3 Search windows

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.1.3.1 Symbol count

**5.2.4.10.10.6.1.3.1.0-1**  (ID: `11448134`)

Symbol count
For 2.3 km support (cellExtension == 23 after enabling **CB007462) ~~Leka Rx/MHAB~~ L1 shall receive 5 symbols long PRACH occasion (instead of 4) where symbols 0…3 refers to Normal range and 1…4 refers to extended range**

**[CB010576-D] This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB010576-D]\*\*\*\*

[CB014188] PRACH opportunity allocation shall support extended cell coverage up to 11 km (cellExtension == 115) with adjusted timing advance configuration.[End CB014188]

---

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.1.3.2 Time occasion search

**5.2.4.10.10.6.1.3.2.0-1**  (ID: `11448149`)

Time occasion search
When extended cell range mode is enabled via CB007462 (i.e. cellExtension == 23) the L1 (L1-FPGA in Loner and MHAB in Loki) shall search the given time occasion twice:

a.First window: symbols 0…3 (Normal)

b.Second window: symbols 1…4 (Extended)

[CB010576-D] This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.[End CB010576-D]

---

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.1.3.3 Number of preambles per search window

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.1.3.3.0-1 Number of preambles per search window For extended cell range (CB007462), L1-FPGA/MHAB shall search 64 preambles (unless otherwise stated via totalNumberOfRAPreambles in the UlCell_SetupReq message) per sliding window and provide the associated PRACH measurement output. For extended range (2.3 km) there can be up to 128 preamble measurements. [CB010576-D] This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.[End CB010576-D] (ID: 11448166)

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.1.4 Processing latency

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.1.4.0-1 Processing latency For extended cell range (CB007462), the L1 shall meet the existing message timing requirement for the normal and extended cell range support modes. [CB010576-D] This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.[End CB010576-D] (ID: 11448181)

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.2 Extended FR2 cell range with B4 format

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.2.1 Symbol length

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.2.1.0-2 Symbol length For extended cell range support of 0~11 km, L1 in Thor shall support multiple detection windows, for algorithm details refer to the 5GMax document. (ID: 12732631)

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.2.2 Preamble search

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.2.2.1 Cyclic prefix

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.2.2.1.0-1 Cyclic prefix L1 in Loki (CB007723-A/C and CB007723-D) shall not limit the preamble search to CP length when cellExtension is enabled [CB010576-D] This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.[End CB010576-D] (ID: 11448231)

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.2.2.2 Number of preambles

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.2.2.2.0-1 Number of preambles For extended cell range (CB007723-A/C and CB007723-D), L1-SW shall search 32 preambles (unless otherwise stated via totalNumberOfRAPreambles in the UlCell_SetupReq message) per sliding window and provide the associated PRACH measurement output. For extended range 6.9 km there can be up to 192 preamble measurements to be post processed by L1-SW. [CB010576-D] This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.[End CB010576-D] (ID: 11448247)

###### 5.2.4.10.10.6.2.3 MHAB config

**5.2.4.10.10.6.2.3.0-1**  (ID: `11448264`)

MHAB config
For 6.9 km support (cellExtension == 69 after enabling CB007723-A/C) and for 5~11km support (cellExtension == 110 after enabling CB007723 -D), the L1-SW in Loki shall configure MHAB per sliding window. For each sliding window, the L1-SW shall configure the MHAB with appropriate pre-combining length and StartSymbol such that HW shall process only one IFFT/matched filtering regardless of sliding window index (e.g. For CB007723- A/C, pre-combining length = 12 with StartSymbol=0, 1, 2 respectively for sliding window indices 0, 1, 2 and 3. For sliding window index = 4, pre-combining length = 11 and startSymbol = 3; For CB007723-D, it results in six sliding windows, which starts from 4 symbols shift, i.e., startSymbol = 4, up to 9 symbols shift. The first window

consist of 10 OFDM symbols, each next is 1 symbol less from previous ).

[CB010576-D] This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.[End CB010576-D]

---

#### 5.2.4.10.11 Support for PRACH beam probing

##### 5.2.4.10.11.1 actPRACHProbing

###### 5.2.4.10.11.1.0-1 actPRACHProbing The parameter actPrachBeamProbing indicates whether beam probing is active. It is supported in FDD FR1 Thor. When the parameter is active, refer to 12571993: PRACH Reception with Beamforming for FDD for the PRACH receiver design. (ID: 12787077)

#### 5.2.4.10.12 PRACH Reception with Beamforming for FDD

##### 5.2.4.10.12.1 Processing for A8 subcell type

###### 5.2.4.10.12.1.1 Thor

**5.2.4.10.12.1.1.0-2**  (ID: `12787053`)

Thor
When actPrachBeamProbing in the cell setup message ([11513449: UlCell\_SetupReq message content:](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_KEuW4PvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is active, the prach is processed with 4 sub-receivers. Each sub-receiver shall process 2 consecutive rx streams and preform detection for all the preambles. For each detected preamble, L1 shall report the beam id in addition to peak metric, timing advance, and **[CB008577-D] timing advance for positioning** [End CB008577-D] in the indicator message. For algorithm details, refer to [12772123: The PRACH Receiver Structure:](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_0J85wYlqEfCrqOdGJPoCRA).\*\*\*\*

The variable sized dynamic array (prachBeamProbingResult) of structure [12788173: prachBeamProbingResult\_t](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_5RdilpLgEfCoxNjZXyLbRA) is used to report the above mentioned 4 metrics. When actPrachBeamProbing is inactive, the array has size zero.

If prach beam probing is inactive/diabled, the L1 shall receive the preambles from one SSB with 2 spatial streams and ignore the rest if other streams exist.

---

### 5.2.4.11 Robustness and configuration validation

#### 5.2.4.11.1 Configuration validation and robustness mechanisms

##### 5.2.4.11.1.1 PRACH configuration index

###### 5.2.4.11.1.1.1 Constraints to be satisfied

**5.2.4.11.1.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11448304`)

Constraints to be satisfied
For FDD (ABIL/Loner in all releases starting from 5G19B, Loki before 5G21B), the supported values of the PRACH configuration index shall be constrained to insure the L1 implementation constraints stated below are satisfied:

1. No more than 1 subcell (occasion) per slot per Loner/Loki.
2. minimum separation of 2 slots between configured PRACH slots (i.e. between subcells) per Loner/Loki.

Where PRACH configuration indices and corresponding slots to be supported in 5G21A and beyond are as follows:

1. {8,12,36,40}  = Slot 1
2. {9,13,37,41}  = Slot 4
3. {10,14,38,42} = Slot 7
4. {11,15,39,43} = Slot 9

Before 5G21A, the Loner/ABIL supports only the following (20ms periodicity, format 0):

1. 12 = Slot 1
2. 13 = Slot 4
3. 14 = Slot 7
4. 15 = Slot 9

---

###### 5.2.4.11.1.1.2 Abnormal operation protection

**5.2.4.11.1.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `11448319`)

Abnormal operation protection
For FDD, The supported values of the PRACH configuration index shall be constrained to insure the L1 implementation constraints stated below are satisfied:

1) No more than 1 subcell (occasion) per slot.

2) A minimum separation of 2 slots between configured PRACH slots.

The L1 (L1 FPGA, L1 SW) implementation shall insure that any PRACH configuration which violates this constraints does not result in abnormal operation. More specifically:

(a) L1 FPGA

(i) Any ongoing PRACH processing initiated prior to the PRACH configuration which violates the constraints of item 2 shall complete normally.

(ii) The PRACH configuration which violates the constraints of item 2 shall be ignored and appropriate logging, in L1 SW accessible debug registers, shall occur such that the action taken by the implementation can be determined. This is to facilitate subsequent debug operations.

(b) L1 SW

(i) Shall provide the capability to read the L1 FPGA debug registers and log the content of these registers in logging messages output to higher layers. This debug register logging and message output capability is only expected to only be used in debug scenarios to facilitate debug operations.

**[CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\*

---

##### 5.2.4.11.1.2 zcz and Ncs setting

**5.2.4.11.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `11448335`)

zcz and Ncs setting
Ncs index = 0 for format 0 with unrestricted set is made invalid. The L1-SW shall perform the following:

a. During UL cell setup phase, L1-SW shall check Zero Correlation Zone Flag, the PRACH format and the type.

b. If format = 0 AND Zero Correlation Zone Flag = 0 AND Unrestricted Set type is enabled, the L1-SW shall consider this as an invalid request.

c. The L1-SW shall not respond to the UlCell\_SetupReq message and log the error condition for dubugging purpose.

**[Before-CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB009444-I] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-FDD-eCPRI.** [End CB009444-I]\*\*\*\*

**[CNI-122313-A]**

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

**[End CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-LA]\*\*\*\*

---

##### 5.2.4.11.1.3 cell extension setting

###### 5.2.4.11.1.3.1 Format C2

###### 5.2.4.11.1.3.1.0-1 Format C2 If cellExtension (CB007462) received in the UlCell_SetupReq message is different than 10 or 23, the L1-SW shall not respond to the UlCell_SetupReq but generate error log in the L1 journals. [CB010576-D] This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.[End CB010576-D] (ID: 11448359)

###### 5.2.4.11.1.3.2 Format B4

###### 5.2.4.11.1.3.2.0-1 Format B4 If cellExtension (CB007723-A/C and CB007723-D) received in the UlCell_SetupReq message is different than 10 or 23 or 69 or 110, the L1-SW shall not respond to the UlCell_SetupReq but generate error log in the L1 journals. [CB010576-D] This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.[End CB010576-D] (ID: 11448374)

##### 5.2.4.11.1.4 nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion setting

**5.2.4.11.1.4.0-1**  (ID: `11448390`)

nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion setting
5G-L1-UL shall validate parameter *nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion in* *UlCell\_SetupReq message.*\*\*

If parameter *nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion is not in range specified in 5G\_L1\_IF\_153\_replaced([11513459](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (column "L1 HW support") 5G-L1-UL shall send UlCell\_SetupResp message to 5G-CP-RT with parameter* status=EStatus5G\_NotOk and parameter *cause=0xD0000036.*\*\*

#### 5.2.4.11.2 Error conditions and alarms

##### 5.2.4.11.2.0-1 Error conditions and alarms The 5G-L1-UL of Loner shall assume that for the cells connected to same ABIL plug-in unit is configured with either long or short formats (reference 5GC001349). Mixed long and short formats configuration is considered invalid and L1-SW shall produce error reports in L1 journal when mixed configuration is found. (ID: 11448408)

## 5.2.5 Dynamic configuration

### 5.2.5.1 PRACH online parameter reconfiguration

**5.2.5.1.0-1**  (ID: `12737560`)

PRACH online parameter reconfiguration
[CB014330-SR-A] Two parameters adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDb and pfaTargetPrachId can be reconfigured dynamically now. Parameter adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDb is present when 11th bit of parameter actMap is set, i.e., actMap(LSB+10) = 1.

Parameter pfaTargetPrachId is present when 12th bit of parameter actMap is set, i.e., actMap(LSB+11)=1. For parameter content refer to description in UlCell\_SetupReq [End CB014330-SR-A].

This requirement shall be supported in Odin for [CB012115-IA]TDD--2a-eCPRI[End CB012115-IA] and [CB012115-JA]FDD-FR1-CPRI[End CB012115-JA] and [CB012115-GA]TDD--2e-eCPRI[End CB012115-GA] and [CB012115-LA]FDD--2a-eCPRI[End CB012115-LA].

---

#### 5.2.5.2.2 Processing overview

**5.2.5.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `11448493`)

Processing overview
Upon reception of the *UlData\_PrachReceiveReq message indicating PRACH slot, the 5G-L1-UL shall attempt detection of the preamble sequences transmitted on PRACH.*

The information required to detect random access preambles is the preamble format, the first root sequence index, zero correlation zone configuration, and the target false alarm probability, which are obtained from the *UlCell\_SetupReq message.*

The PRACH reception algorithms are described in section "2.5 RACH" of the 5GMax algorithm specification (see 5G\_L1\_3900\_replaced([11445871](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_zfIvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

5G-L1-UL shall use the parameters *prachPrbOffset and* prachOccasions in the *UlData\_PrachReceiveReq message to determine the allocated PRACH occasions.*\*\*

The configuration of the *prachOccasions is defined for different preamble formats in 5G\_L1\_4279\_replaced([11446795](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_3wnfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L1\_4273\_replaced([11446600](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_3JhfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L1\_4271\_replaced([11446632](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_3JiPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_4277\_replaced([11446723](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_3wl_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).*

The maximum number of preambles per occasion is configurable via the parameter *totalNumberOfRAPreambles received in* UlCell\_SetupReq message.\*\*

5G-L1-UL shall decide the number of root sequences according to the maximum number of preambles and the Ncs value, the Ncs value is derived according to the parameters *prachSequenceType and* prachZeroCorrelationZoneConfig received in *UlCell\_SetupReq message.*\*\*

For each detected preamble, 5G-L1-UL shall provide the PRACH time occasion index, the PRACH frequency occasion index, the preamble index values, the peak metric, and the noise power to 5G-L2-PS in the *UlData\_PrachReceiveInd message. The PRACH time and frequency occasion indices are required by 5G-L2-PS to deduce the initial beam ID to be assigned to the UE which sent the associated preamble.*

**[5GC001868-A] 5G-L1-UL shall also use the IEs received from higher layers (see above) for PRACH reception in Loki L1 HW.****[End 5GC001868-A]**\*\*\*\*

**[CB007814-G] This requirement also applies to ABIO FR1-FDD-eCPRI.** [End CB007814-G]\*\*\*\*

**[RP003187-A, RP003187-H] 5G-L1-UL shall also use the IEs received from higher layers (see above) for PRACH reception in** L1 Thor. **[End RP003187-A, RP003187-H]**\*\*\*\*

**[CB008205-B, CB008205-C] 5G-L1-UL shall also support requirements above in ABIO for O-RAN compliant FR1 FDD eCPRI.**[End CB008205-B, CB008205-C]\*\*\*\*

**[Before-CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB009443-C] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.**[End CB009443-C]\*\*\*\*

**[CB009444-B] This requirement is applicable for RINLINE1 for FR1-FDD-eCPRI.** [End CB009444-B]\*\*\*\*

**[CNI-122313-A]**

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

**[End CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB010575-A] This requirement shall be supported in L1 Thor HW for FR1-TDD-CPRI.** [End CB010575-A]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\*

patternId

##### 5.2.5.3.1.2 Frequency occasions

**5.2.5.3.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `11448547`)

Frequency occasions
L1 shall support following **PRACH number of occasions in frequency:**

For FDD (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-2):

  Format 0: {1}

  Format 1: {1}

For TDD FR1 (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-3):

  Format 0: {1}

  Format A2: {1}

  Format B4: {1}

  Format C2: {1}

For TDD FR2 (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-4):

  Format A2: {1}

  Format C2: {1}

  Format C0: {1}

  Format B4: {1}

L1 shall use parameter *UlData\_PrachReceiveReq->prachOccasions  from L1 – 5G-L2-PS interface to define requested number of occasions in frequency.*

Array of active PRACH occasions in time and frequency.

Value 0 in bitmap means PRACH occasion not allocated; value 1 means PRACH occasion allocated.

0th element in array corresponds to the frequency block with the lowest PRB offset from the edge of allocation (prachPrbOffset).

Each entry in array is 16-bit bitmap of active PRACH occasions in time. Please note that occasion in time is related but not equal to OFDM symbol and maximum envisioned number of allocated occasions is 14 (for PRACH long formats which are not yet supported - Formats 0 to 4).

Most significant bit of the u16 corresponds to the first PRACH occasion in time.

**Currently, as in frequency domain only 1 occasion is supported in L1, L1 shall support different values for one element of  *prachOccasions*and only zero values for all other elements of* prachOccasions.***\*\*

Supported maximum non-zero elements of array *prachOccasions*for different L1 HW and technologies for FR1 FDD are shown in the table:\*\*

| --- | --- | --- | --- |

| Loner | FR1-FDD-CPRI | {1} | {1} |
| Loki | FR1-FDD-CPRI |  |  |
| FR1-FDD-OBSAI |  |  |  |
| FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI |  |  |  |
| Thor BB | FR1-FDD-CPRI |  |  |

##### 5.2.5.3.1.3 Time occasions

**5.2.5.3.1.3.0-1**  (ID: `11448567`)

Time occasions
L1 shall support following PRACH maximum **number of occasions in time:**

For FDD (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-2):

  Format 0: {1}

  Format 1: {1}

For TDD FR1 (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-3):

  Format 0: {1}

  Format A2: {1, 3}

  Format B4: {1}

  Format C2: {1, 2}

For TDD FR2 (38.211 Table 6.3.3.2-4):

  Format A2: {2, 3}

  Format C2: {1, 2}

  Format C0: {3, 7}

  Format B4: {1}

L1 shall use parameter *UlData\_PrachReceiveReq->prachOccasions from L1 – 5G-L2-PS interface to define requested value.*

Array of active PRACH occasions in time and frequency.

Value 0 in bitmap means PRACH occasion not allocated; value 1 means PRACH occasion allocated.

0th element in array corresponds to the frequency block with the lowest PRB offset from the edge of allocation (prachPrbOffset).

Each entry in array is 16-bit bitmap of active PRACH occasions in time. Please note that occasion in time is related but not equal to OFDM symbol and maximum envisioned number of allocated occasions is 14 (for PRACH long formats which are not yet supported - Formats 0 to 4).

Most significant bit of the u16 corresponds to the first PRACH occasion in time.

Currently, as in frequency domain only one occasion is supported so, L1 shall support different values for one element of  *prachOccasions*and only zero values for all other elements of *prachOccasions.*\*\*

| FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Not supported | Not supported |  |  |  |
| Loki | FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | {0xE000 - for 3, 0xFE00 - for 7} | {0x8000 - for 1} |  |  |
| Thor | **[CB010576] FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI** [End CB010576]\*\*\*\* |  |  |  |  |

**Note:**

0x0000 = 0000 0000 0000 0000 - 0 occasions

0x8000 = 1000 0000 0000 0000 - max 1 occasion

0xC000 = 1100 0000 0000 0000 - max 2 occasions

0xE000 = 1110 0000 0000 0000 - max 3 occasions

0xFE00 = 1111 1110 0000 0000 - max 7 occasions

*example #1:*

*prachOccasions [0]=0x8000  // 0x8000 = 1000 0000 0000 0000 - 1 occasion*

*prachOccasions [1]=0x0000*

*prachOccasions [2]=0x0000*

*prachOccasions [3]=0x0000*

*prachOccasions [4]=0x0000*

*prachOccasions [5]=0x0000*

*prachOccasions [6]=0x0000*

*prachOccasions [7]=0x0000*

*example #2:*

*prachOccasions [0]=0x0000*

*prachOccasions [1]=0x0000*

*prachOccasions [2]=0x0000*

*prachOccasions [3]=0xE000  // 0xE000 = 1110 0000 0000 0000 - 3 occasions*

*prachOccasions [4]=0x0000*

*prachOccasions [5]=0x0000*

*prachOccasions [6]=0x0000*

*prachOccasions [7]=0x0000*

*example #3:*

*prachOccasions [0]=0x8000*

*prachOccasions [1]=0x0000*

*prachOccasions [2]=0x0000*

*prachOccasions [3]=0x0000*

*prachOccasions [4]=0x0000*

*prachOccasions [5]=0xA000  // 0xA000 = 1010 0000 0000 0000 - 2 occasions (when max = 3 or 7)*

*prachOccasions [6]=0x0000*

*prachOccasions [7]=0x0000*

---

##### 5.2.5.3.1.4 Time and frequency occasions

**5.2.5.3.1.4.0-1**  (ID: `11448588`)

Time and frequency occasions
L1 shall support following PRACH **number of occasions in time and frequency in slot:**

For FDD:

  Format 0: {1}

  Format 1: {1}

For TDD FR1:

  Format 0: {1}

  Format A2: [1..3]

  Format B4: {1}

  Format C2: {1, 2}

For TDD FR2:

  Format A2: [1..3]

  Format C2: {1, 2}

  Format C0: [1..7]

  Format B4: {1}

**Currently, as in frequency domain only 1 occasion is supported, number of occasions in time and frequency in slot = number of occasions in time*.***

L1 shall use PRACH number of occasions in time and frequency in slot as size of structure *UlData\_PrachReceiveReq-> subcells[x]-> Occasions*from L1 – 5G-L2-PS interface.\*\*

#### 5.2.5.3.2 Format details

##### 5.2.5.3.2.1 Format 0

###### 5.2.5.3.2.1.1 Loner, Loki

**5.2.5.3.2.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11448620`)

Loner, Loki
L1 shall process the Time and frequency occasions given by the field prachOccasions in the UlData\_PrachReceiveReq message. For PRACH format 0, one PRACH frequency/time occasion is supported with starting symbol = 0. Each element of the array can have value 0x0000 or 0x8000. Each non-zero element of the array (i.e. 0x8000) corresponds to a valid PRACH occasion in the frequency domain.

[Before-CNI-122313-A]

[CB009881-CG] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.[End CB009881-CG]

[CB009444-I] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-FDD-eCPRI.[End CB009444-I]

[CNI-122313-A]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313-A]

[PR630013]

L1 on Loki, Thor [PR634395] and Loner [End PR634395] shall assume that following case is an invalid request:

prach\_occasions[8]

[

0x0,

0x0,

0x0.

0x0,

0x0,

0x0,

0x0,

0x0

]

At least the first one RACH occasion (corresponding to the first time and frequency index) shall be enabled in UlData\_PrachReceiveReq message otherwise the request shall be ignored by 5G\_L1\_UL. Also, currently only the first frequency index of the array shall have the RACH occasion. E.g. following case is not valid:

prach\_occasions[8]

[

0x0,

0x8000 or 0xC000 or 0xE000

0x0,

0x0,

0x0,

0x0,

0x0,

0x0

]

If the request with invalid scenario is received the L1-SW shall produce an error prints and make them available in L1 journals. The L1-SW shall not report the error reports to L2. The behavior shall be same after activation of CB008144.

[End PR630013]

E.g. following case is not valid:

### 5.2.5.4 Busy Cell Handling in 4-4 Frame Structure

**5.2.5.4.0-1**  (ID: `12733426`)

Busy Cell Handling in 4-4 Frame Structure
The L1 entity shall support PRACH resource allocation and activation control for busy cell operation under 4-4 frame structure, especially in FR2 range extension scenario with 10-symbol GP.

Rationale: This is required to ensure reliable PRACH transmission during congested network scenarios in extended coverage cells. The 4-4 frame structure with longer guard periods enables better synchronization and collision avoidance in such conditions.

Input Trigger:

From RRC via MAC: Frame structure configuration with BusyCellEnabled flag = TRUE

---

### 5.2.5.7 Support for custom beam set interworking in 4-4 frame structure

**5.2.5.7.0-1**  (ID: `12733446`)

Support for custom beam set interworking in 4-4 frame structure
This feature introduces logic to support interworking between the PRACH receiver and custom beam set configurations under the 4-4 frame structure.

The configuration ensures that PRACH detection and decoding operate correctly even when beamforming settings are customized per beam set.

The receiver must dynamically adapt its antenna port mappings and beam indices to reflect the customized beam sets during PRACH reception occasions configured in the 4-4 frame structure.

Special attention must be paid to timing alignment and signal quality per beam.

How to invoke:

1. The receiver module should fetch the active beam set configuration per PRACH stream based on RRC signaling.
2. Beam configuration should be applied before PRACH detection window starts.
3. L1 must expose interface hooks for upper layers to provide updated beam configuration.
4. The implementation must support fallback to default beam sets when customized ones are not provided or when inconsistency is detected.
5. PRACH detection logic should validate signal power across all configured beams and adaptively select the best.

---

### 5.2.5.8 Receiver algorithm tuning and configuration

#### 5.2.5.8.1 Receiver configuration

##### 5.2.5.8.1.0-1 Receiver configuration Receiver configuration Upon reception of the UlData_PrachReceiveReq the L1-SW writes the PRACH dynamic parameters into L1-FPGA for reception per slot per subcell.  The dynamic parameters which are written into L1-FPGA memory are discussed in the references given in 5G_L1_3905_replaced( 11445864 ). (ID: 11448756)

#### 5.2.5.8.2 Buffered processing

##### 5.2.5.8.2.1 bufferedUlStruct

**5.2.5.8.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11448781`)

bufferedUlStruct
L1-SW shall receive UlData\_PrachReceiveReq messages containing, per subcell, in the IE bufferedUlStruct which provides the actual time to process PRACH of this subcell, 3 new IEs,

bufferedUlStruct.processInRealTime which is of type Bool, where True indicates data process in RT (i.e., same as air interface time given by SFN and Slot IEs), and False indicates data process in NRT (for FDD, RT processing is relevant, i.e., processInRealTime is set to True);

bufferedUlStruct.sfnForProcessing which is of type u16 [0..1023], which indicates the SFN to process the data in RT or NRT;

bufferedUlStruct.slotForProcessing which is of type u8 [0..79], which indicates the Slot to process the data in RT or NRT.

Note that as up to 4 C2/D2 type subcells can be scheduled in a slot, up to 4 UlData\_PrachReceiveReq messages can be received by L1-SW.

---

##### 5.2.5.8.2.2 Exceptions

###### 5.2.5.8.2.2.0-1 Exceptions The PRACH L1 in Loner shall support the requirement defined in 5G_L1_5251_replaced( 11396692 ). i.e. For configuration as 2 cells with 1 UL C4 subcell per cell, in UlData_PrachReceiveReq message, processInRealTime shall be set to TRUE, and slotForProcessing and sfnForProcessing are set to the same values as slot and sfn in the main level of the same message, regardless buffered UL feature activation or not. (ID: 11448797)

### 5.2.5.9 Robustness and configuration validation

#### 5.2.5.9.1 Robustness

##### 5.2.5.9.1.1 Receive request and indication message parity

**5.2.5.9.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11448829`)

Receive request and indication message parity
For TDD long formats, the L1 shall receive only one UlData\_PrachReceiveReq per PRACH indication. The PRACH receive request shall be always on the first slot of the PRACH access window.

**[RP003187-A] This requirement is also valid for** L1 Thor FR1-TDD-eCPRI.**[End RP003187-A]**\*\*\*\*

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

**[End CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB009514-F] The requirement is also applicable for Thor(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e** [End CB009514-F]\*\*\*\*

Receive request validation
**Receive request**

The L1-SW shall perform the following tasks after reception of UlData\_PrachReceiveReq message.

1) Timing validation

2) Parameters validation

3) Receiver configuration

#### 5.2.5.9.2 Validation

##### 5.2.5.9.2.1 Subcell context

**5.2.5.9.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11448870`)

Subcell context
**Parameters validation**

L1-SW shall validate the received request by checking the existence of subcell index. In case of valid request L1-SW prepares the configuration structure to the received request and stores the subcell context.

In case of invalid request, the L1-SW shall discard the UlData\_PrachReceiveReq message and increases a counter “prachReceiveReqReject” by one. The error counter is initialized during subcell setup.

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\*

##### 5.2.5.9.2.2 Message timing

**5.2.5.9.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `11448887`)

Message timing
**Timing validation**

If UlData\_PrachReceiveReq message is received too late by the L1-SW, a warning or error shall be added to respective 5G-L1-UL logging. In any of these cases, 5G-L2-PS doesn’t receive UlData\_PrachReceiveInd message from 5G-L1-UL (L1-SW).

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\*

##### 5.2.5.9.2.3 numCeAxCId setting

**5.2.5.9.2.3.0-2**  (ID: `12706357`)

numCeAxCId setting
5G-L1-UL shall validate numCeAxcIndex in **UlData\_PrachReceiveReq message.**

The allowable range of parameter *numCeAxcIndex depends on parameters from* *UlCell\_SetupReq :* nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion and *ulSubcellType.*\*\*\*\*

Below table define allowable range of parameter *numCeAxcIndex:*

Table1: The allowable range of parameter *numCeAxcIndex*

|  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  |  | nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion |  |  |
| one | two | four |  |  |
| **numCeAxCIndex** | ulSubcellType = C2 | {2} | {4} | {4, 8} |
| ulSubcellType = C4 | {4} | {4} | {4, 8} |  |
| ulSubcellType = C8 | {4} | {4} | {4, 8} |  |
| [Before CB008235-SR-X] ulSubcellType = C4\_2 [End CB008235-SR-X] | {4} | {4} | {4, 8} |  |
| ulSubcellType = C8\_2 | {4} | {4} | {4, 8} |  |
| ulSubcellType = C8\_4 | {4} | {4} | {4, 8} |  |
| ulSubcellType = C8\_8 | {4} | {4} | {4, 8} |  |

If parameter *numCeAxcIndex is not in range specified in table1 5G-L1-UL shall drop* *UlData\_PrachReceiveReq message and shall generate error log in the L1 journals.*\*\*

Table2: Supported L1 HW and technologies.

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| *HW* | *Technology* | *Feature / support* |
| Loki | FR1 FDD CPRI | Supported |
| FR1 FDD OBSAI | Supported |  |
| FR1 FDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported |  |
| FR1 TDD CPRI | Supported |  |
| FR1 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported |  |
| FR2 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported |  |
| Thor | FR1 FDD CPRI | Supported |
| FR1 FDD OBSAI | Supported |  |
| FR1 FDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported |  |
| FR1 TDD CPRI | Supported |  |
| FR1 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported |  |
| FR1 TDD 7-2e eCPRI | Supported |  |
| FR2 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported |  |

##### 5.2.5.9.2.4 prachPrbOffset validation

**5.2.5.9.2.4.0-1**  (ID: `12729146`)

prachPrbOffset validation
5G-L1-UL (BB) shall validate that prachPrbOffset is smaller than ulBandwidth  -  PRACH PRB size(which is indicated by prachFormat and prachScs)

If prachPrbOffset is too large, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall drop the request and log unique error.

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI**[End CB012115-LA]\*\*\*\*

Note: this requirement is derived from interface definition [11514296: UlData\_PrachReceiveReq message content:](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_TDBHkPvwEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)

## 5.2.6 PRACH channel multiplexing and feature interactions

### 5.2.6.1 Beam muting during PRACH occasions

#### 5.2.6.1.0-1 Beam muting during PRACH occasions This requirement specified that the L1 BB implementation shall support interworking between the 4-4 frame structure and the configured custom beam set defined in RRC. The system must ensure that the L1 behavior does not violate beam scheduling constraints under the 4-4 frame structure and must align with configured beam set behavior provided by higher layer (e.g., RRC signaling or control parameters). How to invoke: L1 shall retrieve the beam set configuration through pre-defined interfaces from MAC/RRC layer. During PRACH and UL scheduling, L1 BB shall map the active beam(s) to the frame structure timing, ensuring beam transition points are respected. If beam switching timing conflicts with symbol allocation (e.g., symbol boundary violation due to 4-4 structure), the scheduler shall either delay the activation or pre-assign an alternative beam. Timing checks and validation must be introduced in L1 BB scheduler to handle conflicts. (ID: 12733460)

### 5.2.6.2 PRACH feature interactions

#### 5.2.6.2.1 General

**5.2.6.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11448937`)

General
Content of this requirement is frozen and valid until 23R3 release. For later releases please refer to the objects below

Feature interaction

Feature interaction refers to scenarios where other system features can interact with the PRACH. e.g. Channel multiplexing on PRACH slots, buffered uplink and DSS the key features that impact the PRACH directly or indirectly. Please see below the list of features interacting with PRACH channel.

Channel Multiplexing on PRACH slots introduced via 5GC001348:

The multiplexed uplink channels in the same symbol of the PRACH slot can support the following combinations:

a) PRACH FDM with PUSCH;

b) PRACH FDM/TDM with short PUCCH;

c) combination of the a and b;

PUSCH is with FDM and short PUCCH within the PRACH slots is FDM/TDM manner as in legacy. The multiplexed PRACH and PUxCH is coming from different UE in the PRACH slot.

The FDMed channels from 5GC001348-A onward can come from the same or different subcells.

[5GC002481-AA][5GC002056-AA]Shall be supported also in Loki  L1 HW [End 5GC002481-AA][End 5GC002056-AA]

[CB007814-D]

5G-L1-UL shall support in ABIO for FR1 FDD eCPRI only FDM multiplexing PUSCH on PRACH slots. 5G-L1-UL shall not support short PUCCH (F0, F2) in FDD in ABIO.

The multiplexed PRACH and PUSCH is coming from different UE in the PRACH slot.

The FDMed channels from 5GC001348-A onward can come from the same or different subcells.

[End CB007814-D]

[Before 5GC001348-A] No UE is scheduled with PUSCH transmission in PRACH slot.[End 5GC001348-A]

[5GC001348-A] UE is also scheduled with PUSCH transmission in PRACH slot. The maximum number of PUSCH grants per PRACH slot is specified in 5G\_UP\_318,5G\_UP\_IF\_1637 and depends on the system release. The number of the PUSCH grant in this feature does not take the PRACH UE into account which is applicable for all sub features. [End 5GC001348-A]

Note:

1. For the CPRI fronthaul based RU, the subcell used for PUSCH and PRACH reception depend on the receiving beam of each channel. If they are from the same beam (sector beam/coarse beam/refined beam) then the same subcell can be used otherwise separate subcells shall be used.
2. For the eCPRI fronthaul based RU, in case FD-beamforming is not supported (can not map different beam to the same eAxC) then the subcell used for PUSCH and PRACH reception depend on the receiving beam of each channel. If they are from the same beam (sector beam/coarse beam/refined beam) then the same subcell can be used otherwise separate subcells shall be used.
3. The FDM capacity here assume that there is subcell which can be used for FDM PUSCH receiving in PRACH slot.
4. For the eCPRI fronthaul based RU, in case FD-beamforming is supported with MADE based RU, the PRB allocation in frequency domain shall follow region division limitation of the RU.

[5GC002056-AA, 5GC002481-AA] The PUSCH transmission in PRACH slot shall be supported also in Loki L1 HW.[End 5GC002056-AA,5GC002481-AA]

[RP003187-B, RP003187-I] The PUSCH transmission in PRACH slot shall also be supported in L1 Thor. [End RP003187-B, RP003187-I]

[CB007814-D] The PUSCH transmission in PRACH slot shall be supported also in ABIO for FR1 FDD eCPRI. [End CB007814-D]

[Before 5GC001348-A] No UE is scheduled with short PUCCH F0 transmission in PRACH slot.[End 5GC001348-A]

[5GC001348-A] UE is also scheduled with PUCCH format 0 transmission in PRACH slot. The maximum number of PUCCH format 0 can be multiplexed in PRACH slot is specified in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1089,5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1091 and depends on the system release.[End 5GC001348-A]

[5GC002056-AA, 5GC002481-AA] The PUCCH F0 transmission in PRACH slot shall be supported also in Loki L1 HW.[End 5GC002056-AA, 5GC002481-AA]

[Before 5GC001348-A] No UE is scheduled with short PUCCH F2 transmission in PRACH slot.[End 5GC001348-A]

[5GC001348-A] UE is also scheduled with PUCCH format 2 transmission in PRACH slot. The maximum number of PUCCH format 2 can be multiplexed in PRACH slot is specified in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1089,5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1091 and depends on the system release. [End 5GC001348-A]

Note:

* This feature (5GC001348) does not increase the number of CSI reports per PUCCH symbol. It only introduces FDM of PUCCH format 2 for HARQ feedback.

[5GC002056-AA, 5GC002481-AA] The PUCCH F2 transmission in PRACH slot shall be supported also in Loki L1 HW.[End 5GC002056-AA, 5GC002481-AA]

Channel Multiplexing on PRACH slots introduced via 5GC000885-G and CB006064-A:

5GC000885-G/CB006064-A: Long PUCCH, PUSCH and PRACH are scheduled in same slot

[RP003187-B, RP003187-I] Long PUCCH, PUSCH and PRACH multiplexing in the same slot shall also be supported in L1 Thor. [End RP003187-B, RP003187-I]

Buffered UL Introduced via 5GC001120 (Loner Only):

5GC001120-A Buffered UL: L1 CPRI and basic E2E for FR1 1S-1CC deployment. This is not applicable to Loki.

UlData\_PrachReceiveReq message:

The bufferedUlStruct is introduced for TDD system (for FDD, RT processing is relevant. i.e. processInRealTime is set to true for FDD system). This is a structure used in UlData\_PrachReceiveReq message to control buffered UL (5G\_UP\_1731).

If processInRealTime is set to True, then slotForProcessing and sfnForProcessing are set to the same values as slot and sfn from given message.

If processInRealTime is set to False, then slotForProcessing and sfnForProcessing are set to the slot and SFN selected for delayed (non-real time) processing.

UlData\_PrachReceiveInd:

For indication message bufferedUlRespStruct is introduced for TDD (for FDD processInRealTime is set to True). It is a structure used in UlData\_PrachReceiveInd message to indicate the SFN and NR-slot index of the air interface of the buffered UL slot (5G\_UP\_1731).

5GC001120-B Buffered UL: L1 eCPRI and basic E2E for FR1 1S-1CC 2 NRCELLGRP deployment

5GC001120-C Buffered UL: Basic E2E for FR2 single-NRCELLGRP deployment. This subfeature doesn’t add any development effort for L1 but testing effort applies.

5GC001904 NR-LTE Dynamic Spectrum Sharing (DSS): For Loner and Loki, in order to support the frequency spectrum sharing with NR (i.e. DSS feature), the FDD NR carriers (10, 15 and 20 MHz) shall be shifted by -7.5 kHz. The PRACH channel is also impacted.

5GC001115-A/CB006115-A CPRI compression: Please refer 5G\_L1\_4117\_replaced([11396664](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tu5_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_4116\_replaced([11396672](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tu6PvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB007326-A] ASOE L1 HW supports only FR1-TDD-eCPRI part. [End CB007326-A]

[CB009881-CG, CB009881-W] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI. [End CB009881-CG, CB009881-W]

---

Note:

* This feature (5GC001348) does not increase the number of CSI reports per PUCCH symbol. It only introduces FDM of PUCCH format 2 for HARQ feedback.

Long PUCCH, PUSCH and PRACH are scheduled in same slot

#### 5.2.6.2.3 Loki

**5.2.6.2.3.0-1**  (ID: `11448973`)

Loki
Feature interaction for Loki

Feature interaction refers to scenarios where other system features can interact with the PRACH. e.g. Channel multiplexing on PRACH slots, buffered uplink and DSS the key features that impact the PRACH directly or indirectly. Please see below the list of features interacting with PRACH channel.

Channel Multiplexing on PRACH slots introduced via 5GC001348:

The multiplexed uplink channels in the same symbol of the PRACH slot can support the following combinations:

a) PRACH FDM with PUSCH;

b) PRACH FDM/TDM with short PUCCH;

c) combination of the a and b;

PUSCH is with FDM and short PUCCH within the PRACH slots is FDM/TDM manner as in legacy. The multiplexed PRACH and PUxCH is coming from different UE in the PRACH slot.

The FDMed channels from 5GC001348-A onward can come from the same or different subcells.

5G-L1-UL shall support in ABIO for FR1 FDD eCPRI only FDM multiplexing PUSCH on PRACH slots. 5G-L1-UL shall not support short PUCCH (F0, F2) in FDD in ABIO.

The multiplexed PRACH and PUSCH is coming from different UE in the PRACH slot.

The FDMed channels from 5GC001348-A onward can come from the same or different subcells.

UE is also scheduled with PUSCH transmission in PRACH slot. The maximum number of PUSCH grants per PRACH slot is specified in 5G\_UP\_318,5G\_UP\_IF\_1637 and depends on the system release. The number of the PUSCH grant in this feature does not take the PRACH UE into account which is applicable for all sub features.

Note:

1. For the CPRI fronthaul based RU, the subcell used for PUSCH and PRACH reception depend on the receiving beam of each channel. If they are from the same beam (sector beam/coarse beam/refined beam) then the same subcell can be used otherwise separate subcells shall be used.
2. For the eCPRI fronthaul based RU, in case FD-beamforming is not supported (can not map different beam to the same eAxC) then the subcell used for PUSCH and PRACH reception depend on the receiving beam of each channel. If they are from the same beam (sector beam/coarse beam/refined beam) then the same subcell can be used otherwise separate subcells shall be used.
3. The FDM capacity here assume that there is subcell which can be used for FDM PUSCH receiving in PRACH slot.
4. For the eCPRI fronthaul based RU, in case FD-beamforming is supported with MADE based RU, the PRB allocation in frequency domain shall follow region division limitation of the RU.

The PUSCH transmission in PRACH slot shall be supported also in ABIO for FR1 FDD eCPRI.

UE is also scheduled with PUCCH format 0 transmission in PRACH slot. The maximum number of PUCCH format 0 can be multiplexed in PRACH slot is specified in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1089,5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1091 and depends on the system release.

UE is also scheduled with PUCCH format 2 transmission in PRACH slot. The maximum number of PUCCH format 2 can be multiplexed in PRACH slot is specified in 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1089,5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1091 and depends on the system release.

Note:

* This feature (5GC001348) does not increase the number of CSI reports per PUCCH symbol. It only introduces FDM of PUCCH format 2 for HARQ feedback.

Channel Multiplexing on PRACH slots introduced via 5GC000885-G and CB006064-A:

Long PUCCH, PUSCH and PRACH are scheduled in same slot

NR-LTE Dynamic Spectrum Sharing (DSS): For Loki, in order to support the frequency spectrum sharing with NR (i.e. DSS feature), the FDD NR carriers (10, 15 and 20 MHz) shall be shifted by -7.5 kHz. The PRACH channel is also impacted. [CB010277-A] When the frequency shift is done by O-RU, frequencyShift7pt5khz should be set to false and L1 do not need to perform the -7.5kHz shift for all UL channels. [End CB010277-A]

CPRI compression: Please refer 5G\_L1\_4117\_replaced([11396664](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tu5_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_4116\_replaced([11396672](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tu6PvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

ASOE L1 HW supports only FR1-TDD-eCPRI part.

[Before-CNI-122313-A]

This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.

[CNI-122313-A]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313-A]

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| *Technology* | Thor | Odin |
| FR1 FDD CPRI | Supported | **[CB012115-JA] Supported**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\* |

### 5.2.6.3 PRACH channel multiplexing

#### 5.2.6.3.1 Loner

##### 5.2.6.3.1.1 CPRI FR1 TDD short PRACH format

###### 5.2.6.3.1.1.1 Channel multiplexing

###### 5.2.6.3.1.1.1.0-1 Channel multiplexing L1-SW shall support uplink channel multiplexing in TDD FR1 CPRI for short PRACH preamble format C2, A2, and B4. (ID: 11449030)

###### 5.2.6.3.1.1.2 PUCCH scheduling

###### 5.2.6.3.1.1.2.0-1 PUCCH scheduling Baseband block feature 5GC001958 is used for 2 cells 4DL/2UL without beamforming, and baseband block feature 5GC001962 is used for 1 cell 8DL/4UL with beamforming. Moreover, the scheduling of up to 4 UEs with short PUCCH transmission per UL subcell in PRACH slot should also be supported as earlier. (ID: 11449046)

##### 5.2.6.3.1.2 CPRI FR1 FDD long PRACH format

###### 5.2.6.3.1.2.1 Channel multiplexing

###### 5.2.6.3.1.2.1.0-1 Channel multiplexing L1-SW shall support uplink channel multiplexing in FDD FR1 CPRI for long PRACH preamble format 0. [CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI. [End CB012115-JA]**** (ID: 11449069)

###### 5.2.6.3.1.2.2 PUCCH scheduling

###### 5.2.6.3.1.2.2.0-1 PUCCH scheduling Baseband block feature 5GC001948 is used for the activation of distributed SW deployment. Moreover, the scheduling of up to 2 UEs with short PUCCH transmission per UL subcell in PRACH slot should also be supported as earlier. (ID: 11449083)

##### 5.2.6.3.1.3 Uplink channel multiplexing - eCPRI adaptions for FR1 TDD short PRACH preamble format without FD beamforming

###### 5.2.6.3.1.3.0-1 Uplink channel multiplexing - eCPRI adaptions for FR1 TDD short PRACH preamble format without FD beamforming L1-SW shall support uplink channel multiplexing in TDD FR1 eCPRI for short PRACH preamble format C2, A2, and B4, without FD-beamforming functionality. (ID: 11449101)

##### 5.2.6.3.1.4 Uplink channel multiplexing - eCPRI FD beamforming adaptions for FR1 TDD short PRACH preamble format

###### 5.2.6.3.1.4.0-1 Uplink channel multiplexing - eCPRI FD beamforming adaptions for FR1 TDD short PRACH preamble format L1-SW shall support uplink channel multiplexing in TDD FR1 eCPRI for short PRACH preamble format C2, A2, and B4, with FD-beamforming functionality. (ID: 11449115)

#### 5.2.6.3.2 Loki

**5.2.6.3.2.0-1**  (ID: `11449132`)

Loki
Multiplexing Configurations:

L1 (Loner and Loki) shall support channel multiplexing on PRACH slots with the following combinations defined by 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1581:

The multiplexed uplink channels in the same symbol of the PRACH slot can support the following combinations:

a) PRACH FDM with PUSCH;

b) PRACH FDM/TDM with short PUCCH;

c) combination of the a and b;

PUSCH and short PUCCH within the PRACH slots is TDM manner as in legacy. The multiplexed PRACH and PUxCH is coming from different UE in the PRACH slot.

The FDMed channels from 5GC001348-A onward can come from the same or different subcells.

---

#### 5.2.6.3.3 Thor, Odin

**5.2.6.3.3.0-1**  (ID: `11449148`)

Thor, Odin
**L1 Thor shall support channel multiplexing on PRACH slots.**

The multiplexed uplink channels in the same symbol of the PRACH slot can support the following combinations:

**[RP003187-B, RP003187-I]**

a) PRACH FDM with long PUCCH;

b) PRACH FDM with PUSCH;

c) combination of the a and b.

**[End RP003187-B, RP003187-I]**

PUSCH and long PUCCH within the PRACH slots are multiplexed in FDM manner. The FDM of the channels is done on the same subcells. The multiplexed PRACH and PUxCH is coming from different UE in the PRACH slot.

## 5.2.7 Whitening preprocessing

## 5.2.8 Stream specific processing

### 5.2.8.1 Frontend processing

### 5.2.8.2 Sampling and compression

#### 5.2.8.2.1 FFT engine in Loner

**5.2.8.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11449195`)

FFT engine in Loner

PRACH FFT processing:

With the new receiver in 5G-L1-UL, there will be two FFT engines, the first one is used to process FFT for all other uplink channels except PRACH, the second is used to process FFT and iFFT for PRACH. After PRACH multiplexing with other uplink channels in PRACH slot is introduced by 5GC001348,  the pre-iFFT samples for PRACH will be buffered due to the shared FFT engine, it will cause additional PRACH processing latency. Due that 5G-L1-UL has decoupled PRACH FFT/iFFT from other uplink channels' FFT, there is no impacts on PRACH performance due to the multiplexing.

[End CNI-59405]

---

##### 5.2.8.2.2.1 Loner

### 5.2.8.3 Cyclic prefix removal

#### 5.2.8.3.1 Cyclic prefix adjustment

##### 5.2.8.3.1.1 Loner

**5.2.8.3.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11449419`)

Loner
For TDD CPRI , L1-SW in Loner shall configure the ofdm\_td\_cfg\_0\_1.symbol\_0\_cp. When PRACH start\_symbol=0, the first PRACH symbol's CP value written into SW register include time\_offset (additional 16\*Ts CP samples  according to 3GPP TS38.211) in case of “long” slot

FR1 (30 kHz SCS):

On every slot, CP value configured into L1-FPGA for first PRACH symbol, shall include time\_offset. i.e. ofdm\_td\_cfg\_0\_1.symbol\_0\_cp = (time\_offset + CP), where CP is the cyclic prefix value defined for used PRACH format and timing\_offset = sampling rate used (in Msps)/1.92.

In FR2 (120 kHz SCS):

For every fourth slots (frame slot\_index % 4 = 0; slot\_indexes #0, #4, #8, #12,...,#76), time\_offset should be added into CP value written into L1Low for the first PRACH symbol

i.e. if frame\_slot\_index % 4 = 0, ofdm\_td\_cfg\_0\_1.symbol\_0\_cp = (time\_offset + CP), where CP is the cyclic prefix defined for used PRACH format and timing\_offset=64 (122.88/1.92 = 64).

External delay processing
11449447:
External delay processing
11449447:
External delay processing
11449447:
External delay processing
11449447:
External delay processing
11449447:
External delay processing
In order to support reception of PRACH preambles coming with increased delay it is required to adjust the receiver. The approaches for adjusting the PRACH reception window differ depending on the fronthaul variant.

The delayed PRACH preamble is bounded by the UL slot. If the PRACH preamble doesn't fit into the UL slot borders, spillover PRACH signal energy in DL slot may become a source of UE-to-UE-interference. The remaining part of the PRACH preamble (inside of UL slot) doesn't always consist of 12 symbols (for PRACH format B4), for example in the case of 5 symbols shifted only 9 symbols of PRACH preamble remain inside the Ul slot. The offset in the PRACH reception window is communicated to L1 with the IE **addExtDelayCompensation in the Ul cell setup message (refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G\_L1\_IF\_153\_replaced([11513459](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). External delay compensation shall be applied if the value of** addExtDelayCompensation is non-zero. The configured amount of external delay may not correspond to an integer number of symbols. After the shift in the PRACH reception window, the last symbol may be incomplete and only partially remain inside the UL slot boundary. The incomplete symbol (if the last symbol is incomplete) and all symbols that are fully outside of the UL slot boundary shall be replaced with zeros before further processing. The feature allows for a maximum of 5 symbols which can be shifted out of the UL slot boundary.\*\*\*\*

The following image is an illustration of the PRACH reception window shift:

[image-0][image\_desc]The image displays a diagram illustrating frame structures for wireless communication, specifically focusing on the "PRACH preamble" within an "UL slot". The top section shows a "Frame structure 4:1 (DDDSU)" with segments labeled U, D, D, D, S, U, D.
The main part of the diagram is a timeline divided into symbols, numbered from 13 down to 13, and then from 0 to 3. This timeline is segmented into different "shift" configurations.
There are three rows representing different scenarios:
1. **Legacy no shift**: This row shows a "PRACH preamble" occupying symbols from 0 to 8. The background is green from symbol 0 to 13, and then blue from symbol 0 to 3.
2. **CB010784 2 symbols shift**: This row also shows a "PRACH preamble", but it starts at symbol 2 and extends to symbol 10. The background coloring is the same as the "Legacy no shift" row.
3. **CB010784 5 symbols shift**: This row shows a "PRACH preamble" starting at symbol 5 and extending to symbol 11. Additionally, there is a red-colored segment from symbol 12 to 13, indicating a potential conflict or different usage. The background coloring is consistent with the other rows.
The diagram is annotated with "Start of UL slot" at the beginning of symbol 0 and "End of UL slot" at the end of symbol 13. The vertical lines represent symbol boundaries.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_5600.001.png[/image\_path][/image-0]

In the case of CPRI based RUs. the external delay is handled by adjusting the CP length, as illustrated below:

[image-1][image\_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating the timing of PRACH (Physical Random Access Channel) reception in two different scenarios: "Legacy PRACH reception" and "CB010784 PRACH reception". The diagram shows a timeline representing the "Start of UL slot" and "End of UL slot".
The "Legacy PRACH reception" consists of a single "CP" (Cyclic Prefix) followed by "PRACH Sequences".
The "CB010784 PRACH reception" is shown to be offset in time. It consists of two "CP" segments, followed by "PRACH Sequences". The diagram indicates that the total length of the CP in the CB010784 reception is the sum of the 3GPP CP length and a "time offset (3rd party delay)".
Below the timeline, there are annotations indicating the lengths of the cyclic prefixes and the time offset:
- `CP3GPP length` is indicated as the duration of the CP in the legacy reception.
- `time offset (3rd party delay)` is shown as the difference in start times between the legacy CP and the first CP of the CB010784 reception.
- `CP3GPP length` is also indicated as the duration of the second CP in the CB010784 reception.
- `CPCB010784 length` is shown as the total duration of the cyclic prefix in the CB010784 reception.
A formula is presented in a box on the right side of the diagram:
`CPCB010784 length = CP3GPP length + time offset`
The diagram uses colored rectangles to represent the different components: blue for CP and orange for PRACH Sequences. Dotted lines are used to align different points in time.[/image\_desc][image\_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng\_files/images/HTML\_pukkola\_5G\_L1\_Entity\_Level\_file\_5600.002.png[/image\_path][/image-1]

For CPRI RUs, the amount of the external delay shall determin the CP length adjustment. The L1 receives the external delay configuration through the IE **addExtDelayCompensation and performs the required conversions into number of samples and the PRACH reception window is shifted according to the result of the conversion. After the PRACH reception window shift, the L1 shall process the preamble following normal PRACH receiver processes.**

Regardless of fronthaul variants, after preamble detection the L1 shall adjust the final initial TA estimation by adding the value converted from **addExtDelayCompensation into units of initialTAs .**

The prachCohCombLen (refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_153\_replaced([11513459](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is the same as in normal deployments with short format B4, i.e. 6 for normal scenarios and 2 for HST scenario. The zeroing of symbols that are partially or fully shifted outside of the UL slot boundary shall be done in a balanced manner so that the zeroed symbols are evenly distributed between the coherent combining groups.

For 5GMax reference, read section "2.5.26 Processing for CB010784" in the 5GMax algorithm specification document (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_695\_replaced([11101310](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knWcovvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**Note: For eCPRI based Ru's, the PRACH reception window shift is done at RU.**

**Note: For detailed algorithm descriptions concerning the zeroing of samples and the distribution of the zero-ed samples amongst the coherent combining groups, please refer to section "2.5.26 Processing for CB010784" in the 5GMax algorithm specification document (applicable for CPRI and eCPRI).**

figuration is as below:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | **Loner** | **Loki** | **Thor** | **Thor RU** | Odin |
| **FR1-TDD-CPRI** | **-** | supported | **[CB010988-B]** supported **[End CB010988-B]** | **-** |  |
| **FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCRPI** | **-** | supported | supported | **-** | **[CB012115-IA] Supported [End CB012115-IA]** |
| **FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCRPI** | **-** | **-** | **-** | **-** | **[CB012115-GA] Supported [End CB012115-GA]** |

### 5.2.8.4 Downsampling and decimation

#### 5.2.8.4.1 Decimation preprocessing

**5.2.8.4.1.0-1**  (ID: `11449471`)

Decimation preprocessing
In case of PRACH long format of CPRI implementation, decimation filters are applied. It is necessary to shift the RACH baseband signal into the passband of the decimation filter before filter and decimate the received RACH signal. The decimation filter is symmetrical around 0 and this step consists in centering the frequency region of the PRACH, 6 RB using SCS=15 kHz or 3 RB in SCS=30 kHz in the center.

The L1-SW shall write/configure the appropriate shift (so called **Nshift) values to the receiver entity after reception of UlData\_PrachReceiveReq mesage from 5G-L2\_PS.**

In case of ABIL folowing steps are performed:

**TDD:**

Shift = mod(beta*(ulBandwidth - 2*prachPrbOffset - 3\*2^(1-mu)), 2048)

where

•mu = 1 for FR1 and 3 for FR2

•beta = (2048/(fs/(15000*2^mu)))*6

•fs = Input sampling rate at CPRI interface

•ulBandwidth = the parameter received in the UlCell\_SetupReq message

•prachPrbOffset = the parameter received in the UlData\_PrachReceiveReq message

**FDD**

The principle is same as TDD, but the implementation steps are different because of differences in SIN-COS table inside LEKA PRACH (TDD) and PRACH FDD. i.e. for TDD the length is 2048 while for FDD the length is 49152.

In case of Loki please see the reference 1) listed in 5G\_L1\_4109\_replaced([11445857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_zfIPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**[RP003187-H] In case of** L1 Thor, **decimation filters are applied in ULFE MHAB (as in Loki), please see the references 1 and 3 listed in 5G\_L1\_3900\_replaced([11445871](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_zfIvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).** [End RP003187-H]***\****\*

**[CB010969-SR-CB] This requirement shall be supported by L1 Thor in FR1-FDD-OBSAI.** [End CB010969-SR-CB]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\*

---

#### 5.2.8.4.2 Decimation and downsampling

##### 5.2.8.4.2.0-1 Decimation and downsampling L1 shall apply decimation to convert the sample rate to 1.92 Msps and shall perform 1536 FFT for all carrier BWs and all long formats. (ID: 11449489)

### 5.2.8.5 PRACH demapping

### 5.2.8.6 Coherent combining

#### 5.2.8.6.1 Coherent combining length

**5.2.8.6.1.0-3**  (ID: `13370868`)

Coherent combining length
L1 shall support following PRACH coherent combining length: (TBD)

For FDD:

  Format 0: {1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 8, 12}

  Format 1: {1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 8, 12}

For TDD FR1:

  Format 0: {1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 8, 12}

  Format A2: {1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 8, 12}

  Format B4: {1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 8, 12}

  Format C2: {1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 8, 12}

For TDD FR2:

  Format A2: {1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 8, 12}

  Format C2: {1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 8, 12}

  Format C0: {1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 8, 12}

  Format B4: {1, 2, 3, 4, 6, 8, 12}

For Loner L1 shall use parameter *UlCell\_SetupReq->prachConfig->* prachCohCombLen to define coherent combining length - see 5G\_L1\_13642\_replaced([11447049](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_4-t_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).\*\*

### 5.2.8.7 Whitening

### 5.2.8.8 Frequency domain automatic gain control (FDAGC)

#### 5.2.8.8.1 General aspects

##### 5.2.8.8.1.0-3 General aspects Beamset configuration for extended range up to 11 km in FR2 This is required for FR2 cell extension to support long-range users through optimized DL beamforming and SSB mapping. Beamset configuration shall support reduced SSB mapping and analog beam boosting to cover UEs located at range up to 11 km (cellExtension == 115). (ID: 12721852)

#### 5.2.8.8.2 Implementation detials

##### 5.2.8.8.2.1 Loki

**5.2.8.8.2.1.0-2**  (ID: `11449596`)

Loki
Regarding FDAGC in Loki (in the case of TDD, for FDD please refer to 5G\_L1\_10028\_replaced([11419267](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-cNQvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),  5G\_L1\_4191\_replaced([11419960](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-fQhvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ):

FDAGC shall be enabled only with short PRACH formats and High Speed (as indicated by the IE actHighSpeedCell in the **UlCell\_SetupReq message). The term "FDAGC" in the context of L1 configuration refers to enabling of FDAGC gain calculation (gain to compensate the power measurements) and sub-band whitening (which includes FDAGC scale factor calculation and scaling of frequency domain samples). When FDAGC is enabled:**

1). In case of eCPRI, FDAGC gain is calculated by the DSP using the frequency domain samples of all Rx antennas and all symbols (all symbols after pre-combining) of PRACH occasion. The coherent combining is performed in DSP before FDAGC. The gain value is sent to backend processing block for power measurements. This is to compensate the AGC scaling in the power measurements.

2). In case of CPRI, the gain is configured with a constant value (so called backoff value). The constant scale factor or the backoff value is configured by the L1SW (where the default is 1/sqrt(2)).

When FDAGC is disabled, the subband whitening performed by the FDAGC block of PRCH  (PRACH preamble detector) shall be bypassed and the FDAGC gain (to compensate the power measurements) shall be set to (configured as) 1 (no calculation in DSP or in the ARM).

Notes: The required subband scaling (also known as FDAGC scaling) factor used in the sub-band whitening procedure is calculated by the block called "FDAGC" supported by the PRCH. The FDAGC block of PRCH calculates the FDAGC gain and applies it on the frequency domain IQ samples (which procedure is known as subband whitening).

**[CB012261-A] In LOKI, 5G-L1-UL shall support to enable and disable FDAGC PRACH algorithm via new NIDD parameter (NRBTS/NRCELL/actPrachMultiplexingLevel).**

When NIDD parameter is enabled\_Level1 (actPrachMultiplexingLevel=1), FDAGC is enabled for all configurations except in case of extended cell feature is activated (cellExtension != 10).

When NIDD parameter is disabled (actPrachMultiplexingLevel=0), FDAGC is enabled in LOKI for HST in short PRACH and FDD eCPRI except in case of extended cell feature is activated (cellExtension != 10).

**Note: R&D parameter (rdFdagcEnable) is no more valid and shall be removed from R&D parameter.**

For more details, please check the following table.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **LOKI** |  |  |  |  |  |
| **actPrachMultiplexingLevel** | **cellExtension** | **PRACH** | **HST** | **Technology** | **FDAGC** |
| enabled\_Level1 | = 10 | NA | NA | FR1-TDD FR1-FDD | Yes |
| enabled\_Level1 | = 10 | NA | NA | FR2-TDD | Yes |
| disabled | = 10 | NA | NA | FR2-TDD | No |
| disabled | = 10 | Short | Yes | FR1-TDD | Yes |
| disabled | = 10 | NA | NA | FR1-FDD-eCPRI | Yes |
| disabled | = 10 | NA | NA | NA | No |
| disabled | ≠ 10\* | NA | NA | FR2-TDD | No |

**Note *When cellExtension is not 10, actPrachMultiplexingLevel is always setting to disabled, because NIDD parameter rule prohibits setting it to enabled\_Level1. \*\*[End CB012261-A]***\*

---

##### 5.2.8.8.2.2 Thor and Odin

**5.2.8.8.2.2.0-3**  (ID: `12547277`)

Thor and Odin
Regarding FDAGC in Thor:

The FDAGC shall be enabled/disabled with a RAD flag. FDAGC is applicable for all formats, types, interfaces and regardless of any input condition. The term "FDAGC" in the context of L1 configuration refers to the enabling of FDAGC gain calculation (gain to compensate the power measurements and scale factor for subband whitening) and sub-band whitening (scaling of frequency domain samples by the AGC scale factor).  When FDAGC is disabled, subband whitening performed by the FDAGC block of PRCH shall be bypassed and the FDAGC gain (to compensate the power measurements) shall be set to 1 (no compensation is required). Refer to 5G\_L1\_10139\_replaced([11452436](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAT1dPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the definition of the FDAGC enabling/disabling flag RAD parameter.

Notes:

FDAGC gain calculation (gain to compensate the power measurements and the scale factor for whitening) and sub-band whitening are performed by the FDAGC block supported by the PRCH. The FDAGC gain is an output from the FDAGC block.  The FDAGC gain value is needed to compensate the power measurements by the backend processing block. In the case of Thor, coherent combining is performed by the PRCH (MHAB) before the FDAGC block. CPRI and eCPRI have no differences in the FDAGC gain compensation.

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| *Technology* | *Feature / support* |
| FR1 FDD CPRI | supported |
| FR1 FDD OBSAI | supported |
| FR1 TDD CPRI | supported |
| FR1 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | supported |
| FR1 TDD 7-2e eCPRI | supported |

In THOR, 5G-L1-UL shall support to enable and disable FDAGC PRACH algorithm via new NIDD parameter (NRBTS/NRCELL/actPrachMultiplexingLevel).

In Thor, Despite of the value of NIDD parameter (NRBTS/NRCELL/actPrachMultiplexingLevel), FDAGC is always on for all configuration when PRACH extended cell range is in normal mode (cellExtension = 10).

**Note: R&D parameter (rdFdagcEnable) is no more valid and shall be removed from R&D parameter.**

For more details, please check the following table.

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **THOR** |  |  |  |  |  |
| **actPrachMultiplexingLevel** | **cellExtension** | **PRACH** | **HST** | **Technology** | **FDAGC** |
| enabled\_Level1 | = 10 | NA | NA | FR1-TDD FR1-FDD | Yes |
| enabled\_Level1/disabled | = 10 | NA | NA | FR2-TDD | Yes |
| disabled | = 10 | NA | NA | NA | Yes |
| disabled | ≠ 10\* | NA | NA | FR2-TDD | No |

**Note \*When cellExtension is not 10, actPrachMultiplexingLevel is always setting to disabled, because NIDD parameter rule prohibits setting it to enabled\_Level1.**

[CB012115-IA]  This requirement shall be supported in Odin TDD FR1 7.2a eCPRI. [End CB012115-IA]

**[CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\*

[CB012115-GA]  This requirement shall be supported in Odin TDD FR1 7.2e eCPRI. [End CB012115-GA]

[CB012115-LA]  This requirement shall be supported in Odin FDD FR1 7.2a eCPRI. [End CB012115-LA]
