## 5.2.9 Noncoherent combining

## 5.2.10 Noise and mean absolute deviation (MAD) estimation

### 5.2.10.1 MAD Overview

#### 5.2.10.1.1 Fixed point algorithm reference

##### 5.2.10.1.1.0-1 Fixed point algorithm reference The L1-FPGA shall implement MAD algorithm for TDD according to fixed point algorithms defined in https://nokia.sharepoint.com/sites/L1AS/5GFAST/Shared%20Documents/Fixed%20point%20algorithm%20specifications/5G21A/5G_Algorithm_Specification_PRACH_fixed_point.pdf (ID: 11449738)

#### 5.2.10.1.2 MAD and dtx threshold offset

**5.2.10.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `11449755`)

MAD and dtx threshold offset
For L1 **[Before CB005927-A] Loner and Loki HW TDD FR1, L1 Loner and** [End CB005927-A] Loki HW TDD FR2 **[RP003187-B] and** L1 Thor TDD FR1 **[End RP003187-B], an offset is added to adjust the DTX threshold described in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1466\_replaced([11105812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koP0jvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), for a proper false alarm and miss detection performance, the offset is configurable in 5G-L1-UL.*****\****\*

For L1 Loner and Loki **[RP003187-B] and Thor** [End RP003187-B] HW FDD, the MAD (Mean Absolute Deviation) algorithm is introduced to improve the false alarm performance with inteference. The MAD algorithm can be enabled and disabled in 5G-L1-UL.\*\*\*\*

• If MAD algorithm is enabled, it will adjust the DTX threshold (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1466\_replaced([11105812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koP0jvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) together with an offset.

• If MAD algorithm is disabled, only an offset is used to adjust the DTX threshold.

The MAD algorithm is described in section "2.5.8 Correlated Antenna Processing" of the 5GMax algorithm specification (see ~~5G\_L1\_5G21A\_916~~ 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**[CB005927-A] For L1 Loner HW TDD FR1 and FR2, and Loki HW TDD FR1, the MAD algorithm is also introduced as described above to improve the false alarm performance with interference.** [End CB005927-A]\*\*\*\*

**[RP003187-B] For** L1 Thor TDD FR1, the MAD algorithm is also introduced as described above. **[End RP003187-B]**\*\*\*\*

**[Before-CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB009443-C] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI as part of CB009443.**[End CB009443-C]\*\*\*\*

**[CNI-122313-A]**

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

**[End CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB010575-A] This requirement for L3 Call shall be supported in L1 Thor HW for FR1-TDD-CPRI. For L3 call MAD algorithm is always on.** [End CB010575-A]\*\*\*\*

### 5.2.10.2 MAD variant

**5.2.10.2.0-3**  (ID: `12547365`)

MAD variant
The DU shall support the MAD algorithm.

1. For Loner L1 HW, the MAD statistic is derived from the first available root sequence.
2. For Loki and Thor L1 HWs, with short formats in both normal speed cells and high speed cells,

- when NRBTS/NRCELL/actPrachMultiplexingLevel (refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_153\_replaced([11513459](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to disabled:

 When R&D parameter rdShortPrachMaxMadFlag (see 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27795\_replaced([11110554](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpFiD_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to FALSE the MAD statistic is derived from the first available root sequence.

 When R&D parameter rdShortPrachMaxMadFlag is set to TRUE, the MaxMAD is used where the MAD statistic is derived from the maximum over all available root sequences.

**- when NRBTS/NRCELL/actPrachMultiplexingLevel (refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_153\_replaced([11513459](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to enabled\_Level1:**

  the MaxMAD is used where the MAD statistic is derived from the maximum over all available root sequences, the setting of the R&D parameter rdShortPrachMaxMadFlag has no effect.

1. For Loki and Thor L1 HWs with long formats, the MaxMAD is used where the MAD statistic is derived from the maximum over all available root sequences.

[CB012115-IA] The above requirement shall be supported in Odin TDD FR1 7.2a eCPRI. [End CB012115-IA]

**[CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\*

[CB012115-GA] The above requirement shall be supported in Odin TDD FR1 7.2e eCPRI. [End CB012115-GA]

**[CB012115-LA]The above requirement shall be supported in Odin FDD FR1 7.2a eCPRI.**[End CB012115-LA]\*\*\*\*

### 5.2.10.4 MAD thresholds

#### 5.2.10.4.1 Loner

##### 5.2.10.4.1.1 FDD

**5.2.10.4.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11449831`)

FDD
**MAD algorithm configuration:** FDD\*\*\*\*

(Please refer 5G\_Algorithm\_Specification\_PRACH\_fixed\_point for the MAD algorithm description)

The L1 Loner shall implement MAD algorithm for FDD. This was introduced in Loner in **5G19B via** FGCR6977. The MAD algorithm requires initial threshold settings to be configured by L1-SW. The initial thresholds are needed to define the lower and upper bound of MAD operating region. The lower bound impacts the minimum sensitivity and upper bound defines the highest threshold to be supported when correlation index between the antennas is 1 (very strong correlation). The upper bound is set as single antenna threshold. These thresholds are expected to be optimized for the field scenario (as we cannot do the optimization in labs or in link level simulator). The L1-SW shall configure the MAD as follows:\*\*\*\*

**[PR614472]**

**2Rx**

**[Before 5G21B]**

The L1-SW shall compute the PRACH dtx thresholds for 2Rx as follows:

1.Calculate T1 and Tn using run time calculation defined for FDD long format

2.Tn = (uint16\_t)Tn \* 10^(rdPrachThresholOffsetDb/10);

3.if (rdPrachMadEnable=0) T1=Tn;

**[End before 5G21B]**

**[From 5G21B]**

Calculate T1 and Tn using run time calculation defined for FDD long formats of Loner.

Modify the T1 and Tn as follows:

MAD\_T\_1 (2Rx): Normalized threshold (MAD\_T\_1 = T1 \* 10^((rdPrachThresholOffsetDb+adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDbTmp)/10)).

MAD\_T\_N (2Rx): Normalized threshold (MAD\_T\_N = Tn \* 10^((rdPrachThresholOffsetDb+adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDbTmp)/10)).

**[End From 5G21B]**

Where the rdPrachMadEnable is a RAD parameter presented in const\_customizer.conf file **[Before 22R1]and the rdPrachThresholOffsetDb is a RAD parameter of rd\_thresholds.conf.** [End before 22R1]\*\*\*\*

Where,

rdPrachMadEnable ~~= 1~~: 5G\_L1\_3841\_replaced([11451805](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAQLHfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdPrachThresholOffsetDb ~~= 2 dB (linear value = 1.58).~~: 5G\_L1\_3839\_replaced([11451906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAQyMPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))(Until 5G21B), 5G\_L1\_8913\_replaced([11478382](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fDJHBvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))(from 22R1 onward)

adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDbTmp: 5G\_L1\_6790\_replaced([11447656](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_8CB_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))(Until 5G21B), 5G\_L1\_7034\_replaced([11447664](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_8CCPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))(from 22R1 onward)

Where number of Rx antennas is deduced from prachDtxThresholdSelection (which is an IE of UlCell\_SetupReq message).

**4Rx**

In case of 4Rx, the L1-SW shall compute the PRACH dtx thresholds as follows (this is just to keep the existing implementation provided to TMO USA unimpacted):

1.Calculate T1 and Tn using run time calculation defined for FDD long format

2.if (rdPrachMadEnable=1) T1 = (uint16\_t)T1 \* 10^((rdPrachThresholOffsetDb+adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDbTmp)/10);

3.else { / *turn off FPGA MAD algorithm* /

4.Tn = (uint16\_t)Tn \* 10^((rdPrachThresholOffsetDb+adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDbTmp)/10);

5.T1 = Tn;

6.}

Where,

rdPrachMadEnable ~~= 1~~: 5G\_L1\_3841\_replaced([11451805](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAQLHfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

rdPrachThresholOffsetDb ~~= 3 dB (linear value = 2)~~: 5G\_L1\_3839\_replaced([11451906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAQyMPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))(Until 5G21B), 5G\_L1\_8913\_replaced([11478382](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fDJHBvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))(from 22R1 onward)

adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDbTmp: 5G\_L1\_6790\_replaced([11447656](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_8CB_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))(Until 5G21B), 5G\_L1\_7034\_replaced([11447664](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_8CCPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))(from 22R1 onward)

**[End PR614472]**

For calculation of TN, T1, v1 and VN in Loner, please refer 5G\_Algorithm\_Specification\_PRACH\_fixed\_point.pdf:

<https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:b:/r/sites/L1AS/5GFAST/Shared%20Documents/Fixed%20point%20algorithm%20specifications/5G21B/5G_Algorithm_Specification_PRACH_fixed_point.pdf>

**[CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\*

---

##### 5.2.10.4.1.2 TDD

**5.2.10.4.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `11449850`)

TDD
MAD algorithm configuration: TDD (CB005927)

For Loner (starting from 5G21A), following parameters/configurations are used after [PR582822] (modified in [PR614472]):

if (rdPrachMadEnable=1) {

MAD\_v\_N: MAD Tabulated Vn

MAD\_T\_1 (2Rx): Normalized threshold (MAD\_T\_1 = T1).

MAD\_T\_N (2Rx): Normalized threshold (MAD\_T\_N = Tn \* 10^((rdPrachThresholOffsetDb+adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDbTmp)/10)).

MAD\_T\_1 (4Rx): Normalized threshold (MAD\_T\_1 = T1 \* 10^((rdPrachThresholOffsetDb+adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDbTmp)/10)).

MAD\_T\_N (4Rx): Normalized threshold (MAD\_T\_N = Tn).

[02291843/02328980]

For short formats: MAD\_T\_1 (4Rx): Normalized threshold (MAD\_T\_1 = T1 \* 10^((rdPrachThresholOffsetDbT1+adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDbTmp)/10)).

For short formats: MAD\_T\_N (4Rx): Normalized threshold (MAD\_T\_N = Tn \* 10^((rdPrachThresholOffsetDbTn+adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDbTmp)/10)).

[End 02291843/02328980]

[Before CNI-87001-A]

MAD\_slope\_N : Tabulated ratio max(0, (T1-Tn)/(v1-vN)).

[CNI-87001-A]

MAD\_slope\_N : Tabulated ratio max(0, (T\_MIN-Tn)/(v\_MIN-vN)).

T\_MIN = T1 if unrestricted set and T\_MIN = T3 if restricted set A, v\_MIN = v1 for unrestricted set and v\_MIN=v3 for restricted set type A.

[End CNI-87001-A]

}

else {

MAD\_v\_N: MAD Tabulated Vn

MAD\_T\_N (2Rx/4Rx) = (uint16\_t)Tn \* 10^((rdPrachThresholOffsetDb+adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDbTmp)/10);

MAD\_T\_1 (2Rx/4Rx) =Tn;

MAD\_slope\_N : 0

}

Please refer 5G\_L1\_2083\_replaced([11494969](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fEqJ__vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)): 5G\_L1\_3839\_replaced([11451906](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAQyMPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))(Until 5G21B), 5G\_L1\_8913\_replaced([11478382](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fDJHBvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))(from 22R1 onward) for the default values of rdPrachThresholOffsetDb.

[02591394]

From 22R3 onwards, the L1SW in Loner shall take the rdPrachThresholOffsetDb values for TDD FR1 and 4RX according to the activation flag carried by the IE adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDb (MSB 8 bits). When the activation flag is set to TRUE (i.e. all “0” is referred to FALSE (default); otherwise TRUE), the threshold table can be found in the Table 3.8-5  in the 5G Fast 22R3 document (<https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:b:/r/sites/L1AS/5GFAST/Shared%20Documents/Fixed%20point%20algorithm%20specifications/5G22R3/5G_Algorithm_Specification_5G22R3_PRACH_fixed_point.pdf?csf=1&web=1).>  When the activation flag is set to FALSE, refer to Table 3.8-4 in the 5G Fast document (same reference link as in the case when the flag is set to TURE) for the threshold values.

Note:

Other TDD configuration scenarios (e.g. TDD FR2, or TDD FR1 2RX) are not impacted.

[END 02591394]

For calculation of T1, Tn, v1 and VN in ABIL, please refer

5G\_Algorithm\_Specification\_PRACH\_fixed\_point.pdf:

[Before CNI-87001-A]

[End CNI-87001-A]

#### 5.2.10.4.2 Loki and Thor

**5.2.10.4.2.0-3**  (ID: `11449893`)

Loki and Thor
For Loki (starting from 22R3) and **[RP003187-B] Thor (starting from 23R1-SR)** [End RP003187-B] HWs, calculate TN and T1 using run time calculation defined for TDD and FDD long formats.\*\*\*\*

Modify the TN and T1 as follows:

MAD\_T\_N (2Rx/4Rx): Normalized threshold (MAD\_T\_N = TN \* 10^((PrachThresholOffsetDbTN+adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDbTmp)/10))

MAD\_T\_1 (2Rx/4Rx): Normalized threshold (MAD\_T\_1 = T1 \* 10^((PrachThresholOffsetDbT1+adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDbTmp)/10))

**[PR643618]**

Where PrachThresholOffsetDbTN, PrachThresholOffsetDbT1 refers to thresholds optimised for 3GPP (reference: 5GMax), and the values when actHighSpeedCell=false are below:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Num of antenna | technology | Formats | MAD ON |  | MAD OFF |
| PrachThresholOffsetDbTN | PrachThresholOffsetDbT1 | PrachThresholOffsetDbTN |  |  |  |
| 2Rx | FDD | Long | 2 dB | 0 dB | 2 dB |
| TDD FR1 | Long | 2 dB | 0 dB | 2 dB |  |
| Short | 1.5 dB | 0 dB | 1.5 dB |  |  |
| TDD FR2 | Short | 1 dB | 0 dB | 1 dB |  |
| 4Rx | FDD | Long | 1 dB | 4 dB | 4 dB |
| TDD FR1 | Long | 1 dB | 4 dB | 4 dB |  |
| Short | 1 dB | 1 dB | 1 dB |  |  |

The values when actHighSpeedCell=true are below:

|  |  |  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Num of antenna | technology | Formats | MAD ON |  | MAD OFF |
| PrachThresholOffsetDbTN | PrachThresholOffsetDbT1 | PrachThresholOffsetDbTN |  |  |  |
| 2Rx | FDD | Long | 2 dB | 0 dB | 2 dB |
| TDD FR1 | Long | 2 dB | 0 dB | 2 dB |  |
| Short | 2 dB | 0.5 dB | 2 dB |  |  |
| TDD FR2 | Short | 1 dB | 0 dB | 1 dB |  |
| 4Rx | FDD | Long | 1 dB | 4 dB | 4 dB |
| TDD FR1 | Long | 1 dB | 4 dB | 4 dB |  |
| Short | 1 dB | 1 dB | 1dB |  |  |

NOTE: PrachThresholOffsetDbT1 = 0dB when MAD is OFF.

**[End PR643618]**

Where adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDbTmp refers to the threshold derived from adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDb value received in the UlCell\_SetupReq message:

adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDbTmp = adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDb/10 - 3.

If adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDb is not configured or the value is outside of the valid range {0...60},  the L1-SW shall assume adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDb = 30 for the above calculation.

For the comformance test the value of adjustPrachThresholdOffsetDb sent to L1 in UlCell\_SetupReq message shall be set to 30.

In case of TDD:

if (rdPrachMadEnable=1) {

MAD\_v\_N: MAD Tabulated Vn

}else {

MAD\_slope\_N : 0

}

##### 5.2.12.1.1.0-1 Loki 5G-L1-UL of Loki shall support configurable PRACH search window offset such that preamble with negative time offset can be detected. Minimum negative offset that shall be supported are 390 ns for TDD FR1, 65 ns for TDD FR2 and 1.5625 us for FDD. The value can be translated in samples as round(overSamplingFactor*offset/(1/prach_scs/IFFT_size)). (ID: 11449939)

### 5.2.12.2 Detection thresholds determination

**5.2.12.2.0-1**  (ID: `11449973`)

Detection thresholds determination
L1-SW in **Loner HW shall calculate the** DTX threshold (introduced via **5GC001981-A) according to the *prachFormat, the *pfaTargetPrachId, the* prachZeroCorrelationZoneConfig and the number of valid RX antennas, if the \*pfaTargetPrachId not equal to 0.******\****

If the *pfaTargetPrachId equals to 0, 5G-L1-UL shall use pre-stored DTX threshold instead of run time calculation.*

The *prachFormat,* pfaTargetPrachId and *prachZeroCorrelationZoneConfig are obtained from the* UlCell\_SetupReq message (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).\*\*\*\*

**[Before 5GC002244-A, 5GC001294-B] The number of valid RX antennas are determined according to *ulSubcellType. \*\*[End 5GC002244-A, 5GC001294-B]***\*\*

**[5GC002244-A, 5GC001294-B, CB007814-B] The number of valid RX antennas are determined according to *prachDtxThresholdSelection parameter in the  *UlCell\_SetupReq message (see 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).* \*[End 5GC002244-A, 5GC001294-B, CB007814-B]***\*\*\*

The DTX threshold calculation algorithm has been defined in section "2.5.13 Detection Threshold Set" of the 5GMax algorithm specification.

**[5GC001868-A] 5G-L1-UL shall support PRACH DTX thresholds as descripted above in** Loki L1 HW  **[End 5GC001868-A]**\*\*\*\*

### 5.2.12.3 Preamble detection

#### 5.2.12.3.1 PRACH Detection Window Configuration

**5.2.12.3.1.0-1**  (ID: `12733000`)

PRACH Detection Window Configuration
The L1 baseband entity shall support configuration and triggering of PRACH detection window for extended cell operating in the FR2 bands for range scenarios up to 11 km.

* Support for programmable offset of the detection window relative to synchronization signals (e.g., SSB or DL symbols).
* Support for configurable duration of the detection window in symbol-level granularity.
* Invocation of the detection window parameters by higher layers (via L2 signaling or internal configuration database)

The detection window shall be aligned with PRACH occasions configured for the cell range and numerology. The actual detection timing shall be adjusted dynamically based on slot configuration and beam association (if any).

Rationale: To support robust PRACH detection for UEs located in far-cell areas (up to 11 km, as in CB014188), the gNB needs to adjust its L1 baseband processing window accordingly. Improper configuration may lead to missed detection or incorrect window alignment.

Notes for Implementation: The L1 processes PRACH in extended cells by processing multiple detection window. Algorithm of the processing and combining the result of the processing multiple windows is provided in the

[5GMax section](https://jenkins-5gmax.eecloud.dynamic.nsn-net.net/job/AlgoSpec/job/AlgoSpec_OnDemand/lastSuccessfulBuild/artifact/main.pdf)2.5.13. Number of windows to be processed is derived based on cellExtension in CellSetupRequest.

Processing of the each window is realized by the MHAB configured as described in the 11448256: MHAB config. Localization of the PRACH signal in the time and frequency is communicated to L1 entity via UlData\_PrachReceiveReq.

---

#### 5.2.12.3.3 High power mitigation

##### 5.2.12.3.3.1 Loner

###### 5.2.12.3.3.1.1 Fixed point algorithm reference

[End PR570884] (ID: 11450022)

###### 5.2.12.3.3.1.2 Order of processing

###### 5.2.12.3.3.1.2.0-1 Order of processing [PR570884] The L1-SW of 5G-L1-UL of Loner shall process the High Power Mitigation algorithm in any order (i.e. before or after executing the preamble validity check which is supported in existing implementation, i.e. initial release of 5G21A) but it shall use the raw values (TA, peakMetrics) provided by the L1-FPGA. [End PR570884] (ID: 11450040)

##### 5.2.12.3.4.2 Harmonic removal with restricted sets

**5.2.12.3.4.2.0-4**  (ID: `12521447`)

Harmonic removal with restricted sets
**Highspeed preamble detector and harmonic removal**

Highspeed preamble detector is introduced for the cell which is configured with restricted set (prachSequenceType, see 5G\_L1\_IF\_153\_replaced([11513459](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) since there are harmonic peaks in case of high frequency offset. The combination over main and harmonic windows is implemented to improve missed detection performance, and the harmonic removal is implemented to improve false alarm performance.

Highspeed preamble detector is introduced for the cell which is configured with restricted set (prachSequenceType, see 5G\_L1\_IF\_153\_replaced([11513459](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) since there are harmonic peaks in case of high frequency offset. The combination over main and harmonic windows is implemented to improve missed detection performance, and the harmonic removal is implemented to improve false alarm performance.

* For the combination window the main peak and 1st harmonics are combined in case of restricted set type A. In case of restricted set B, the main peak, 1st harmonics and 2nd harmonics are combined. The algorithms are described in section '2.5.20.3 highspeed' of 5GMax algorithm specification 2.5.20.6 LokiPRCH' for **Loki (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and 2.5.20.7 for** Thor.\*\*\*\*
* L1 **Loki shall use 1024 PDP samples instead of 2048 in PRACH PDP detection** when cell’s total roots number is higher than 32 (section '2.5.20.6 LokiPRCH' of 5GMax algorithm specification). This saves DSP load and avoids reducing the number of preambles, but brings acceptable PRACH performance degradation for low speed UE (about 0.5dB for restricted set type A).\*\*\*\*
* The harmonic removal for highspeed receiver removes the 2nd and 3rd harmonics in case of restricted set type A **and 5th in case of restricted set B. The algorithm is described in section '2.5.17 Harmonic removal' of the 5GMax algorithm specification.**

**Note: the harmonic removal for normal receiver (unrestricted set case) is out of the scope of CB006662 feature.**

The support of highspeed preamble detector in L1 is as follows:

**For Loki**

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Preamble format and restricted set type** |  | **Highspeed preamble detector, TDD** | **Highspeed preamble detector, FDD** |
| Long PRACH Format 0 | restricted set type A | supported | supported |
| restricted set type B | **supported** | supported |  |
| Long PRACH Format 1 | restricted set type A | - | supported |
| restricted set type B | - | supported |  |

**For Thor**

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| **Preamble format and restricted set type** |  | **Highspeed preamble detector, TDD** | **Highspeed preamble detector, FDD** |
| Long PRACH Format 0 | restricted set type A | supported | supported |
| restricted set type B | **supported** | supported |  |
| Long PRACH Format 1 | restricted set type A | - | supported |
| restricted set type B | - | supported |  |

[CB014106-SR-A] This requirement shall be supported in Thor FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI. [End CB014106-SR-A]

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-LA]\*\*\*\*

#### 5.2.12.3.5 Preamble filtering

##### 5.2.12.3.5.1 Total number of preambles

**5.2.12.3.5.1.0-1**  (ID: `11450201`)

Total number of preambles
The total number of PRACH preambles to be searched per PRACH occasion is defined by totalNumberOfRAPreambles which is an IE of UlCell\_SetupReq message (PrachConfig defined in 5G\_L1\_IF\_153\_replaced([11513459](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), original location: 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_152). The value of totalNumberOfRAPreambles shall be less than or equal to 64. The L1-SW shall set this value as 64 if the value is not present in the interface. e.g. if the value is 4, only first 4 preamble indices in the occasions shall be searched for reporting.

**[CB008325-5G-AA] The requirement is also valid for** Thor. **[End CB008325-5G-AA]**\*\*\*\*

**[Before-CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB009443-C] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.**[End CB009443-C]\*\*\*\*

**[CB009444-I] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE 1 HW for FR1-FDD-eCPRI.** [End CB009444-I]\*\*\*\*

**[CNI-122313-A]**

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

**[End CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\*

##### 5.2.12.3.5.2 Number of preambles in the indication message

**5.2.12.3.5.2.0-1**  (ID: `11450218`)

Number of preambles in the indication message
The *numOfPrachPreambles* from *UlData\_PrachReceiveInd defines how many detected preambles are sent to 5G-L2-PS in the given slot.*\*\*

The supported value is: Up to 64 detected preambles are sent to 5G-L2-PS per PRACH slot even when more are detected.

The possible maximum number of detected preambles per PRACH slot according to 3GPP definition is calculated as below:

*Maximum number of detected preambles per PRACH slot = Maximum number of time occasions × Maximum number of frequency occasions × Maximum number of preambles per occasion*

- The supported value for *Maximum number of frequency occasions is 1.*

- The supported value for *Maximum number of preambles per occasion is derived from the* totalNumberOfRAPreambles parameter in *UlCell\_SetupReq message (5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the maximum value of* totalNumberOfRAPreambles  is 64.\*\*\*\*

- The supported value for *Maximum number of time occasions for each PRACH format is described in 5G\_L1\_13562\_replaced([11448567](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAATffvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).*

- The supported value for *Maximum number of detected preambles per PRACH slot for each PRACH format is described in 5G\_L1\_13760\_replaced([11447493](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_7a8fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).*

For each detected preamble, 5G-L1-UL shall fill following IEs in *UlData\_PrachReceiveInd:*

* *prachPreambleIndex which is the preamble index where energy has been detected.*
* *prachPreambleTimeOccasion which is detected preamble's position in time.*

The supported values per format are: [0, .., *Maximum number of time occasions-1].*

* *prachPreambleFreqOccasion which is detected preamble's position in frequency.*

The supported value is 0.

* *initialTa which is the measured timing advance.*

**[RP003187-A] For** L1 Thor FR1-TDD-eCPRI the supported values for *Maximum number of time occasions and* Maximum number of detected preambles per PRACH slot for each PRACH format are described in 5G\_L1\_6413\_replaced([11451521](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAO8-fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). **[End RP003187-A]****\***\*

**RP003187-H] For** L1 Thor FR1-FDD-CPRI the supported values for *Maximum number of time occasions and* Maximum number of detected preambles per PRACH slot for each PRACH format are described in 5G\_L1\_6413\_replaced([11451521](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAO8-fvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). **[End RP003187-H]****\***\*

**[CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\*

##### 5.2.12.3.5.3 Preamble distribution across occasions

**5.2.12.3.5.3.0-1**  (ID: `11450236`)

Preamble distribution across occasions
**5G-L1-UL of Loki shall select 64 preambles, based on energy and preamble load distribution across occasions, when the total number of detected preambles for given slot exceeds 64. For example, when preambles are detected in 3 occasions with 24, 36 and 48 distribution the L1-SW shall select 14, 22 and 28 preambles from each occasion.**

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-LA]\*\*\*\*

---

### 5.2.12.4 Noise power averaging

### 5.2.12.5 PRACH beam probing

#### 5.2.12.5.0-1 PRACH beam probing When actPrachbeamProbing in the cell setup message ( 11517801: UL Cell Setup ) is active, the PRACH receiver design is based on 2rx sub-receivers, there are 4 sub receivers, each one of them carries out preamble reception using a defined beam. A preamble may be detected in up to all of the beams used. The detection results including the beam id are sent in the indicator message. If a preamble is detected in more than one beam, the multiple detections contribute only once to the counting of the total number of preambles, i.e., no per beam based duplicate counting shall be applied. (ID: 12787093)

## 5.2.13 PRACH receive indicator report preparation

### 5.2.13.1 General aspects

**5.2.13.1.0-1**  (ID: `11450269`)

General aspects
Informative text:

The preparation of message differs depending on the platforms, formats, duplex modes and interface. Please refer the respective L1 specification documents for the details. The references are given in 5G\_L1\_3905\_replaced([11445864](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e_zfIfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Please refer 5G\_L1\_4209\_replaced([11420627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-gep_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the scaling details for 5G21B.

---

### 5.2.13.2 PRACH post processing

#### 5.2.13.2.1 Initial TA processing

##### 5.2.13.2.1.1 Extended cells

###### 5.2.13.2.1.1.1 Format C2

**5.2.13.2.1.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11450308`)

Format C2
For extended cell range (CB007462), the L1-SW shall post process the initialTa estimates of L1-HW for the selected preambles as normal (5G21A). Lets call this as initialTa\_post

a)Modify the initialTa\_post for the preambles which are selected from the second window. i.e.

b)Preambles selected from the first window (normal range) shall not be modified for timing, initialTa\_L2PS = initialTa\_post

c)Preambles selected from the second window (extended range) shall be modified as intialTa = initialTa\_post + 127

[CB010576-D] This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.[End CB010576-D]

---

###### 5.2.13.2.1.1.2 Format B4

###### 5.2.13.2.1.1.2.0-1 Format B4 L1-SW in Loki (CB007723-D) shall add additional 512 samples into initialTa for all preambles selected from sliding windows which are belong to 5~11 km cell (cellExtension = 110). Where sliding window processing within this cell and offset to initialTa for given sliding window is same as other extended cell feature (e.g. CB007462). [CB010576-D] This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.[End CB010576-D] (ID: 11450325)

#### 5.2.13.4.2 Received noise power estimation

##### 5.2.13.4.2.1 Noise estimation procedure

###### 5.2.13.4.2.1.1 Loner

###### 5.2.13.4.2.1.1.0-1 Loner If any PRACH preamble is detected per subcell and per slot, then the noisePower (in dBm) for the PRACH bandwidth averaged over all occasions, combined for all Rx antennas, is estimated from the estimated UL receiver noise powers per occasion (normalized to PRACH bandwidth and combined for all RX antennas and repetitions) reported by the L1-FPGA. L1-SW shall average the noise estimates of all occasions, and convert to dBm. (ID: 11450411)

###### 5.2.13.4.2.1.2 Loner, Loki

**5.2.13.4.2.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `11450428`)

Loner, Loki
The L1 shall estimate the noise power for the PRACH bandwidth averaged over all occasions and Rx antennas. It is one value per subcell and per slot. The noise power (in dBm) shall be computed from the estimated UL receiver noise powers per occasion (normalized to PRACH bandwidth and averaged for all RX antennas and repetitions) reported by the HW/DSP and stored in appropriate format supported by the respective HW/SW interface . So, L1-SW shall average the noise estimates of all occasions.  The averaged noise is then converted to dBm by the L1-SW using the rxScalingFactor and other receiver dependent parameters (e.g. agc scalar).

[Before-CNI-122313-A]

[CB009444-I] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-FDD-eCPRI. [End CB009444-I]

[CNI-122313-A]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313-A]

---

###### 5.2.13.4.2.1.3 Thor, Odin

**5.2.13.4.2.1.3.0-1**  (ID: `11450443`)

Thor, Odin
The L1 shall estimate the noise power for the PRACH bandwidth averaged over all occasions and Rx antennas. It is one value per subcell and per slot. The noise power (in dBm) shall be computed from the estimated UL receiver noise powers per occasion (normalized to PRACH bandwidth and averaged for all RX antennas and repetitions) reported by the HW/DSP and stored in appropriate format supported by the respective HW/SW interface . So, L1-SW shall average the noise estimates of all occasions.  The averaged noise is then converted to dBm by the L1-SW using the rxScalingFactor and other receiver dependent parameters (e.g. agc scalar).

**[RP003187-C] The requirement is applicable for** L1 Thor for FR1-TDD-eCPRI **[End RP003187-C]**\*\*\*\*

**[RP003187-J] The requirement is applicable for** L1 Thor for FR1-FDD-CPRI **[End RP003187-J]**\*\*\*\*

##### 5.2.13.4.2.2 Noise estimation algorithm

###### 5.2.13.4.2.2.1 Loner

###### 5.2.13.4.2.2.1.0-1 Loner The noise estimation algorithm on PRACH is described in section 2.5.19 of the 5Gmax algorithm specifications (see 5G_L1_7703_replaced( 11396538 )). For each received PRACH, 5GNB 5G-L1-UL shall estimate the noise power. Then, 5G-L1-UL reports the estimated value to 5G-L2-PS within the parameter noisePower in UlData_PrachReceiveInd message. (ID: 11450468)

###### 5.2.13.4.2.2.2 Loner, Loki, Thor

**5.2.13.4.2.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `11450484`)

For each received PRACH, 5GNB 5G-L1-UL shall estimate the noise power. Then, 5G-L1-UL reports the estimated value to 5G-L2-PS within the parameter *noisePower in* UlData\_PrachReceiveInd message.\*\*

#### 5.2.13.4.3 Noise power measurement calibration and correction

##### 5.2.13.4.3.1 Loner

**5.2.13.4.3.1.0-1**  (ID: `11450510`)

Loner
L1-SW shall compute the noise as part of indication message preparation, to which a correction term pCorPrach is now added. The correction term pCorPrach in dB scale is introduced to calibrate the noise measurements if need be. Before 5GC001163-B, L1-SW shall receive the RAD parameter pCorPrach from parameter file during startup with default value equal to 0. After 5GC001163-B, L1-SW shall receive the IE pCorPrach from message UlCell\_SetupReq, and when "cpriDialectIndication == CPRI-A",

in case of 5MHz, pCorPrach is – 5 dB

in case of 10MHz, pCorPrach is – 2 dB

Other FDD BW do not require any correction (bias is expected to be too small) and hence pCorPrach is 0.

---

#### 5.2.13.4.4 Scale conversion

##### 5.2.13.4.4.1 Loki, Thor, Odin

**5.2.13.4.4.1.0-2**  (ID: `11450542`)

Loki, Thor, Odin
**[Before CNI-126050-A]**

Noise power is converted from dBm value into linear scale using the formula 10.^((noisePower\_dBm-30)/10).

This requirement also applies to ABIO FR1-FDD-eCPRI.

This requirement also applies to Thor FR1-TDD-eCPRI and FR1-FDD-CPRI

5G-L1-UL shall also support requirements above for FR1 FDD 7-2a eCPRI for Thor.

**[CNI-126050-A]**

Estimated noise power is reported to L2-PS in dBm unit*.*

**[End CNI-126050-A]**

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
|  | **Thor** | **Loki** | Odin |
| **FR1-FDD-CPRI** | Supported | Supported | **[CB012115-JA] Supported [End CB012115-JA]** |

#### 5.2.13.4.5 Noise power linear

##### 5.2.13.4.5.1 Loki, Thor

**5.2.13.4.5.1.0-2**  (ID: `11450576`)

Loki, Thor
[Before CNI-126050-A]

For each received PRACH receive request, 5G-L1-UL shall estimate the noise power on PRACH PRBs (common for all the detected preambles and aggregated over all the PRACH PRBs) as described in section 2.5.18 ”Signal and Noise Power Estimation” of the 5Gmax algorithm specifications (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Then power noise shall be averaged over all PRACH resources in slot.

Then averaging shall be done over all RX antennas (spatial streams) in given subcell.

The same noise power value is used for each PRB occupied by PRACH in all allocated by this PRACH PRBs.

L1 shall send noise power using noisePower noisePowerLinear IE in UlData\_PrachReceiveInd message

The unit of noise power estimate is in aW (10-18 Watt) units.

In case of invalid measurement shall send the 10-17 Watt.

This requirement is applied to ABIP as well

Averaging over spatial streams also applies to Thor HW for FR1-FDD-CPRI and FR1-TDD-eCPRI.

5G-L1-UL shall also support requirements above for FR1 FDD 7-2a eCPRI for Thor.

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| HW | Technology | Feature / support |
| Loki | FR1 FDD CPRI | Supported (averaging over all RX antennas) |
| FR1 FDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported (averaging over all RX antennas) |  |
| FR1 TDD CPRI | Supported (averaging over all RX antennas) |  |
| FR1 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported (averaging over all RX antennas) |  |
| FR2 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported (averaging over all RX antennas) |  |
| Thor | FR1 FDD CPRI | Supported (averaging over all RX antennas) |
| FR1 FDD OBSAI | Supported (averaging over all RX antennas) |  |
| FR1 FDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported (averaging over all RX antennas) |  |
| FR1 TDD CPRI | Supported (averaging over all RX antennas) |  |
| FR1 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported (averaging over all RX antennas) |  |
| FR1 TDD 7-2e eCPRI | Supported (averaging over all RX antennas) |  |
| FR2 TDD 7-2a eCPRI | Supported (averaging over all RX antennas) |  |

[CNI-126050-A] Noise power estimation in linear scale is not supported. [End CNI-126050-A]

#### 5.2.13.4.6 Noise power dBm

##### 5.2.13.4.6.1 Loki, Thor, Odin

**5.2.13.4.6.1.0-2**  (ID: `11450608`)

Loki, Thor, Odin
**[Before CNI-126050-A]**

**5G-L1-UL(BB) shall set parameter *UlData\_PrachReceiveInd->subcell->noisePower as INVALID (-140 dBm).***

**[End CNI-126050-A]**

**[CNI-126050-A]**

For each received PRACH receive request, 5G-L1-UL (BB) shall estimate the noise power on PRACH PRBs (common for all the detected preambles and aggregated over all the PRACH PRBs) as described in 5G\_L1\_17108\_replaced([11450350](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAJdYPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Then averaging **shall be done over all RX antennas (spatial streams) in given subcell.**

The same noise power value is used for all PRBs allocated to PRACH.

L1 shall report noise power using *noisePower IE in* UlData\_PrachReceiveInd message.\*\*

The unit of noise power estimate is dBm. Power scaling and conversion to dBm unit shall be done as described in 5G\_L1\_4205\_replaced([11421544](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-hFtfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Loki and 5G\_L1\_8908\_replaced([11422403](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e-hsxPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Thor-BB.

In case of invalid measurement, 5G-L1-UL shall report value -140 dBm.

**[End CNI-126050-A]**

### 5.2.13.5 Time and frequency occasion reporting

### 5.2.13.6 Received peak power calculation

### 5.2.13.7 PRACH measurements

#### 5.2.13.7.1 Timing offsets

##### 5.2.13.7.1.1 Loner

###### 5.2.13.7.1.1.0-1 Loner FFT window shift value depends on the frequency band as follows: For FR1, it equals to 64Ts/4 For FR2, it equals to 16Ts/4 gNB 5G-L1-UL shall perform an initial timing offset estimation from PRACH reception and report it to 5G-L2-PS within the field initialTa in the UlData_PrachReceiveInd message. The PRACH TO estimate shall be reported to 5G-L2-PS with a granularity of Ns*Ts, where Ns=16/2μ , where μ is the numerology and Ts is defined in 4.1 3GPP 38.211 (for a latest supported version see 5G_UP_IF_7). The initial timing offset estimation algorithm on PRACH is described in section 2.5 of the 5GMax algorithm specifications (see 5G_L1_5G21A_916 5G_L1_7703_replaced( 11396538 )). (ID: 11450660)

##### 5.2.13.7.1.2 Loki

**5.2.13.7.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `11450680`)

Loki
FFT window shift value depends on the frequency band as follows:

* For FR1, it equals to 64Ts/4
* For FR2, it equals to 16Ts/4

gNB 5G-L1-UL shall perform an initial timing offset estimation from PRACH reception and report it to 5G-L2-PS within the field *initialTa in the* UlData\_PrachReceiveInd message. The PRACH TO estimate shall be reported to 5G-L2-PS with a granularity of Ns*Ts, where Ns=16/2μ , where μ is the numerology and Ts is defined in 4.1 3GPP 38.211 (for a latest supported version see 5G\_UP\_IF\_7).*\*

[Before 04726839] For Short PRACH format, μ=μPRACH; [04726839] For Short PRACH format, μ=μPUSCH. [End 04726839]

For Long PRACH format, μ=μPUSCH.

The initial timing offset estimation algorithm on PRACH is described in section 2.5.14 of the 5GMax algorithm specifications (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**[5GC000836-E] For FDD, PRACH Format 0 is supported, and the TO estimate shall be processed with  =0.**[End 5GC000836-E]\*\*\*\*

**[RP003187-F] The requirement is also applicable for** Thor for FR1-TDD-eCPRI. **[End RP003187-F]**\*\*\*\*

**[RP003187-M] The requirement is also applicable for** Thor for FR1-FDD-CPRI for μ = 0. **[End RP003187-M]**\*\*\*\*

**[Before-CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB009443-C] This requirement for format B4 shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.** [End CB009443-C]\*\*\*\*

**[CB009881-CD, CB009881-W] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.** [End CB009881-CD, CB009881-W]\*\*\*\*

**[CB009444-I] This requirement for format 0 shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-FDD-eCPRI.** [End CB009444-I]\*\*\*\*

**[CNI-122313-A]**

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

**[End CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB011178-A] 5G-L1-UL shall also support requirements above for FR1 FDD 7-2a eCPRI for Thor.** [End CB011178-A]\*\*\*\*

#### 5.2.13.7.2 Received interference and thermal noise power

##### 5.2.13.7.2.1 Overview

#### 5.2.13.7.3 Improved Timing advance measured on PRACH for reporting UL NR E-CID

**5.2.13.7.3.0-7**  (ID: `11450782`)

Improved Timing advance measured on PRACH for reporting UL NR E-CID
Unit of initialUlEcidTAdv is Tc and unit of initialTa is (16/2^μ)\*Ts. In some cases, value of initialUlEcidTAdv  is converted from value of initialTa  directly. For condition, please refer to 5G\_L1\_19645\_replaced([11450766](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fALSk_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_19646\_replaced([11450774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fALSlPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Ts and Tc relationship is 64Tc = 1Ts(for detail please refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_1615\_replaced([11107907](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koj9nPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

L1 SW needs to do conversion based on this equation:

initialUlEcidTAdv =initialTa *(16/2^μ)*64

Value μ depends on the SCS.

For Short PRACH format, μ=μPRACH;

For Long PRACH format, μ=μPUSCH.

---

#### 5.2.13.7.4 PRACH beam id

##### 5.2.13.7.4.0-1 PRACH beam id When PRACH beam probing is active, in the indicator message the PRACH receiver shall report the beam probing results using a variable sized dynamic array of structure 12788173: prachBeamProbingResult_t . (ID: 12787267)

### 5.2.13.8 Receive indicator reporting

#### 5.2.13.8.1 Buffered UL processing (Loner)

**5.2.13.8.1.0-1**  (ID: `11450804`)

Buffered UL processing (Loner)
L1-SW shall send a single UlData\_PrachReceiveInd message per subcell (no bundle) to 5G-L2-PS containing, for all subcells receiving PRACH in the slot, in the IE bufferedUlRespStruct, 3 new IEs,

bufferedUlRespStruct.processInRealTime which is of type Bool, where True indicates PRACH process was done in RT (i.e., same as air interface time given by SFN and Slot IEs), and False indicates PRACH process was done in NRT (for FDD, RT processing is relevant, i.e., processInRealTime is set to True);

bufferedUlRespStruct.sfnForProcessing which is of type u16 [0..1023], which indicates the SFN at which PRACH processing was done;

bufferedUlRespStruct.slotForProcessing which is of type u8 [0..79], which indicates the Slot at which PRACH processing was done.

SubcellId parameter shall support any value 0 through 7 for Loner. Please refer to 5G\_UP\_1851, 5G\_UP\_1854 and 5G\_UP\_1859 for detail.

---

#### 5.2.13.8.2 Root index calculation

##### 5.2.13.8.2.0-1 Root index calculation [PR570884] The L1-SW of 5G-L1-UL of Loner shall calculate the root index of the detected preambles from the equation (root_index= floor(prachPreambleIndex/swCount) where prachPreambleIndex is sent by the FPGA, swCount = floor(LRA/Ncs), LRA refers to preamble length and Ncs is deduced from zero correlation zone flag received in the UlCell_SetupReq message. [End PR570884] (ID: 11450819)

#### 5.2.13.8.3 Special handling

##### 5.2.13.8.3.1 Zero preamble detected

**5.2.13.8.3.1.0-1**  (ID: `11450842`)

Zero preamble detected
**[CB008144, CB008827-5G-A]After activation of CB008144 (22R3 onwards), L1-SW in Loki and Loner shall send PRACH indication message to 5G\_L2 PS although no preambles are detected. The numOfPrachPreambles shall be set to 0 and noisePower is set to -140 dBm.**

Currently, there is no activation flag from high layer. This would mean that the L1-SW behavior will be changed from 22R3 onwards.

**[End CB008144, CB008827-5G-A]**

**[CB009514-KA] The requirement is also applicable for Thor(BB) for FR1-TDD-eCPRI 7.2e** [End CB009514-KA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-LA]\*\*\*\*

---

##### 5.2.13.8.3.2 Invalid noise power estimates

**5.2.13.8.3.2.0-1**  (ID: `11450859`)

Invalid noise power estimates
L1 (Loki and Loner) shall report ~~0 as PeakMetric, initialTa = 0 and~~ noisePower as -140dBm and noisePowerLinear as 10^(-17) W (Watt) as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_7421\_replaced([11109729](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ko7J_fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), when all IQ samples (frequency/time domain) of Rx branch are all zeros or measured values are below the invalid value.

PeakMetric invalid value is 0 and initialTA invalid value is 0 as defined in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_8426, but they are not reported if *numOfPrachPreambles equals zero.*

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-LA]\*\*\*\*

### 5.2.13.9 Robustness and message validation

#### 5.2.13.9.1 Preamble validity check

**5.2.13.9.1.0-1**  (ID: `11450885`)

Preamble validity check
For short formats, after a preamble has been detected, an additional validity check shall be perfromed.

The validity check is based on both peak metric and time offset, the detail algorithm is described in section 2.5.11 of 5GMAX algorithm specification (Version 11.074) (see 5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

**[5GC001868-A] 5G-L1-UL shall support PRACH preamble validity check as descripted above in Loki L1 HW**[End 5GC001868-A]\*\*\*\*

**[CB007814-G] This requirement also applies to ABIO FR1-FDD-eCPRI.** [End CB007814-G]\*\*\*\*

**[RP003187-B] 5G-L1-UL shall support PRACH preamble validity check as descripted above in** L1 Thor. **[End RP003187-B]**\*\*\*\*

**[Before-CNI-122313-A]**

**[CB009443-C] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI.**[End CB009443-C]\*\*\*\*

**[CNI-122313-A]**

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

**[End CNI-122313-A]**

## 5.2.16 RF Performance

### 5.2.16.1 Conformance testing

#### 5.2.16.1.1 General aspects

**5.2.16.1.1.0-1**  (ID: `11450979`)

General aspects
**3GPP Conformance**

This object is going to be replaced by the objects below for future releases to improve readability and traceability.

For new features please consider usage of the objects below.

1) **5GC001716 (system release** 5G19B, **5G20A): Conformance Test and Type Approval extension for** 5G19B/5G20A (**5GC001300-A,** 5GC001301-A: PRACH format C2 with 30 kHz and 120 kHz)***\******\***

2) **5GC002493 (system release** 5G20B): Conformance Test and Type Approval for **5G20B (no changes to PRACH)**\*\*\*\*

3) **CB005881 (system release** 5G21A): Conformance Test and Type Approval for **5G21A (**5GC001349-A/B: PRACH format 0 in TDD FR1, **5GC000938-A/C: PRACH format 1).*****\****\*

4) **CB007200 (system release** 5G21B, Loner Only):Conformance Test and Type Approvals for **5G21B (~~5GC002223-A~~~~: PRACH short format C2 with 60 kHz~~,** CB007146 40 MHz cell bandwidth - FR1-FDD legacy)***\****\*

~~5)~~ ~~CB007201-5G-B~~ ~~(system release~~ ~~22R1-5G~~~~): Conformance Test and Type Approvals for~~ ~~22R1-5G~~ ~~(~~~~5GC001305~~ ~~Frame structure enhancement: Preamble format C0 - 120 kHz)~~

~~- PRACH performance test for Preamble format C0 - 120 kHz~~

6) **CB008014-D (system release 22R2-5G): Conformance Test and Type Approval for 22R2-5G (**5GC001305 Frame structure enhancement: Preamble format C0 - 120 kHz)\*\*\*\*

* PRACH performance test for preamble format C0 - 120 kHz FR2

**This is applied to ASOE as well by CB007539-B.**

7) **[CB008093-B] (system release** 22R3-SR, ABIO ): Conformance Test and Type Approval for **22R3-SR**\*\*\*\*

###### 5.2.16.1.2.2.2 Timing translation

**5.2.16.1.2.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `11451044`)

Timing translation
For PRACH performance test, L1 ULPHY shall translate the timing parameter in the received eCPRI U-Plane message with PRACH payload when the flags '**ORANprachNumerology' and '** isConformanceTestEnable' in UlCell\_SetupReq are set to '**TRUE' (for more details about flags 'ORANprachNumerology' and   'isConformanceTestEnable' please see 5G\_L1\_IF\_152\_replaced([11513449](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_156\_replaced([11485532](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fD3fwPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), respectively).**\*\*\*\*

**Note 1: The timing parameters in eCPRI U-Plane messages with PRACH for BTS normal mode provided by MADE2 (STATIC\_PRACH\_V2) diverging from the standard scheme specified by 3GPP based numerology (STATIC\_PRACH), L1 PHY workaround is needed to adapt with this new timing (STATIC\_PRACH\_V2) scheme (for more detail please see BTSC\_L1\_Req\_10165\_replaced([11589393](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BRjPGPwGEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and BTSC\_L1\_Req\_7000\_replaced([11589398](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BRjPGfwGEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). *Please note that the STATIC\_PRACH\_V2 *for MADE 2 is already done by CB006941 in BTS normal mode. The STATIC\_PRACH\_V2* for Test dedicated mode shall be conducted in *CB011017*.***\*\*\*\*

**Note2: Basically, L1 UL PHY shall use** ‘**ORANprachNumerology = 'TRUE' and** isConformanceTestEnable='TRUE', to **determine the presence of MADE2 RU type for correct RACH occasion detection in PRACH performance (conformance) test since MADE 2 RU uses different PRACH occasion numerology than that of proposed by 3GPP.*****\****\*

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

|  |  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |

| FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI | Supported | Supported | **[CB012115-IA] Supported**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\* |
| FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI | Not supported | **[CB009936-J]Supported**[End CB009936-J]\*\*\*\* |  |

###### 5.2.16.2.1.3.2 L3 call

**5.2.16.2.1.3.2.0-1**  (ID: `11451381`)

L3 call

PUSCH SCS = 30 kHz, PRACH SCS = 1.25 kHz

Unrestricted set only

Ncs index = 1..15

PRACH occasion can be assigned on two 30 KHz consecutive UL slots.

PRACH FDM (several frequiency occasions): Not supported

SSB per RACH occasion: 1

Support both SA and NSA

Support bandwidths as per 5G\_L1\_6397\_replaced([11395568](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8noSvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Applicable for 5GC001116 and 5GC001070 frame structures, but not usable with 5GC001208 frame structure.

### 5.2.16.3 Testing adaptations

#### 5.2.16.3.0-1 Testing adaptations Since the SR performance is impacted when extended cell flag is enabled (CB007462), dtx threshold tuning is required during the I&amp;V phase. [CB010576-D] This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.[End CB010576-D] (ID: 11451428)

## 5.2.17 PRACH capacity

### 5.2.17.1 Root sequence capacity

**5.2.17.1.0-2**  (ID: `11451460`)

Root sequence capacity
**[Before CB006662-B]**

**Loki, FR1-FDD-CPRI case.**

Upon cell setup, L1 in **Loki shall check the number of roots per cell, accumulate this count across the cells in incremental fashion and record an error message when the accumulated value exceeds** [Before CB006913-W] 192 **[CB006913-W] 512 refer to 5G\_L1\_8419\_replaced([11451574](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAPkAfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**[End CB006913-W] When the count reaches the limit value (**[Before CB006913-W] 192** [CB006913-W] 512 refer to 5G\_L1\_8419\_replaced([11451574](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAPkAfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**[End CB006913-W]), concerned cell (last cell which break the limit) and beyond shall not be processed by L1.*****\******\***

Where number of roots per cell shall be calculated as follows:

Matlab code that could be used to find the number of consecutive root sequences when zero correlation zone flag > 0 is shown below for guideline:

number of roots = ceil(totalNumberOfRAPreambles. /floor(Lra./Ncs))

where

totalNumberOfRAPreambles is an IE of UlCell\_SetupReq message

Lra refers to preamble length. For long format Lra = 839 and for Short formats Lra = 139.

Ncs is a function of zero correlation zone flag which is an IE of UlCell\_SetupReq message

Long format:

Table: Ncs vs ZeroCorrelationZoneFlag

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| ZeroCorrelationZoneFlag | Ncs |
| 0 | 839 |
| 1 | 13 |
| 2 | 15 |
| 3 | 18 |
| 4 | 22 |
| 5 | 26 |
| 6 | 32 |
| 7 | 38 |
| 8 | 46 |
| 9 | 59 |
| 10 | 76 |
| 11 | 93 |
| 12 | 119 |
| 13 | 167 |
| 14 | 279 |
| 15 | 419 |

~~[RP003187-K]~~ ~~The requirement is also applicable for L1~~ ~~Thor~~~~.~~ ~~[End RP003187-K]~~

**[CB006662-B]**

**Rationale: with feature CB006662-B, the limitation in L1 SW related RACH root sequence capacity limitation is not needed any more. The total number of roots per Loki instance will be limited by RO capacity in Loki (see 5G\_RAN\_OP\_1838). Hence the check is obsoleted.**

**[End CB006662-B] See also 5G\_UP\_4194**

**[CB011178-A] 5G-L1-UL shall also support same requirements in CB006662-B for FR1 FDD 7-2a eCPRI for Thor.** [End CB011178-A]\*\*\*\*

---

| A2 | 3 | 192 | RP003187-D |

### 5.2.17.3 Mixed format capacity

**5.2.17.3.0-1**  (ID: `11451537`)

Mixed format capacity
For FDD, **5G-L1-UL of L1 instance shall assume that PRACH format 0 and format 1 can be mixed across cells (any combination including F1+F1 on the same cell). Where PRACH periodicities supported are 20ms and 40ms  (Format 0, 40ms: {8, 9, 10, 11}, Format 0, 20ms: {12, 13, 14, 15}, Format 1, 40ms: {36, 37, 38, 39}, Format 1, 20ms: {40, 41, 42, 43}**

**[RP003187-K] The requirement is also valid for Thor** [End RP003187-K]\*\*\*\*

**[CB007814-C] 5G-L1-UL shall also support *requirement above in ABIO for FR1 FDD eCPRI. \*\*[End CB007814-C]***\*\*

**[CB011178-A] 5G-L1-UL shall also support requirements above for FR1 FDD 7-2a eCPRI for Thor.** [End CB011178-A]\*\*\*\*

**[CB010969-SR-CB] This requirement shall be supported by L1 Thor in FR1-FDD-OBSAI.** [End CB010969-SR-CB]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-LA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-LA]\*\*\*\*

---

### 5.2.17.4 RACH occasion capacity

#### 5.2.17.4.1 RACH occasion capacity per L1 pool FDD

##### 5.2.17.4.1.1 Loki

**5.2.17.4.1.1.0-3**  (ID: `11451581`)

Loki
After introduction of CB006913 for FDD cells, L1 in Loki shall support the following combinations & conditions(including 4Rx diversity receiver):

i. Maximum  [Before CB009543-A]  3x  [CB009543-A] 6x (1) [End CB009543-A] Format 0 ROs /slot /Loki for given slot OR

ii. 2x PRACH Format 1 ROs /slot /Loki for given slot OR

iii. 2x PRACH Format 0 + 1x PRACH Format 1 ROs /slot /Loki

Note 1: The 5G-L1-UL shall processing of up to 6 RO for long format 0 per slot per L1 instance when the scheduled subcells are in a supercell. Otherwise, it still keeps 3 RO for long format 0 per slot per L1 instance.

See also 5G\_UP\_11542

L1 shall support the maximum number of RACH occasions per L1 pool as presented in the table:

L1 shall support the maximum number of RACH occasions per L1 pool as presented in the table:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| Maximum number of time occasions per **L1 pool** | Maximum number of detected preambles **per PRACH slot per L1 pool** |
| **For NR-LTE concurrent tri-mode (5G\_UP\_11197):** 3 ROs for long format 0. 1 ROs for long format 1. The mix of long format 0 and format 1 in the same PRACH group is not supported, but format mixing is supported across different PRACH groups. For reference on PRACH groups and configuration examples, refer to 5G\_UP\_5097 and 5G\_UP\_5834 respectively.   In other deployments: **[Before CB009543-A]** 4 **[CB009543-A]** 6 **(**3)***\** \*[End CB009543-A]** ROs for format 0. 2 ROs for format 1. 2 ROs for format 0 in combination with 1 ROs for format 1. | 64(preambles per PRACH slot) \* minimum {X; RO} |

**Note 1:**

PRACH preamble capacity per PRACH slot per L1 pool = PRACH preamble capacity per PRACH slot per subcell (=64, refer to 5G\_UP\_3302 ) \* minimum{X; RO}.

X =  the maximum number of supported cells/subcells per L1 pool.

RO =  the **maximum number of RACH Occasions "at same time" as defined in the table above per L1 pool.**

**Note 2:**

The following is a graphical representation of the term PRACH group, 15 kHz PUSCH scs is assumed for the slot and subframe numbering (in this case one subframe consists of one slot):

[image-0][image\_desc]The image is a spreadsheet-like grid that displays information about FDD PRACH groups. The grid has rows labeled "F0" and "F1", and columns labeled "SF0" through "SF9". The columns are grouped into "Group 1", "Group 4", "Group 7", and "Group 9", indicated by colored headers (red, yellow, green, and blue, respectively).
The first column under the main header lists "supported prach config index with scs=15kHz" and contains numerical ranges: "8, 12", "9, 13", "10, 14", "11, 15", "36, 40", "37, 41", "38, 42", and "39, 43".
The cells within the grid contain "x" marks, indicating support or association between the PRACH config index and the specific SF (Subframe) within a group.
Below the grid, there are two lines of text describing the duration of "Format 0" and "Format 1", including specific time values in microseconds (us) and milliseconds (ms). The final line states that "FDD PRACH groups are defined in 5G\_UP\_11545".
Here is the table represented in markdown:

| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| F0 | 8, 12 |  | X |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
| F0 | 9, 13 |  | X |  |  | X | X |  |  |  |  |
| F0 | 10, 14 |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

| F1 | 37, 41 |  |  |  |  | X | X | X | X | X | X |
| F1 | 38, 42 |  |  |  |  |  |  | X | X | X | X |
| F1 | 39, 43 | X | X | X | X | X | X | X | X | X | X |
| **Format Durations:** |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

**Note 3:**

#### 5.2.17.4.2 PRACH occasion capacity per L1 pool TDD FR1

##### 5.2.17.4.2.1 Thor

**5.2.17.4.2.1.0-3**  (ID: `11451683`)

Thor
L1 shall support the maximum number of RACH occasions per L1 pool as presented in the table:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **PRACH occasion capacity** **per L1 pool** | **Maximum number of detected preambles per PRACH slot per L1 pool** |
| **[Before CB009142-A]** ***\*[Before CB009055-5G-G]*** *3 ROs for all supported PRACH formats* ***[CB009055-5G-G]*** *4 ROs for all supported PRACH                       formats* ***[End CB009055-5G-G]****[CB009142-A]* *6 ROs for all supported PRACH formats* *[End CB009142-A]*\* | **[Before CB009142-A]** ***\*[Before CB009055-5G-G]*** *64(preambles per PRACH slot)*3 (cells per L1 pool) = **192** ***\*[CB009055-5G-G]*** *64(preambles per PRACH slot)*4 (cells per L1 pool) = **256** ***\*[End CB009055-5G-G]****[CB009142-A]* *64(preambles per PRACH slot)*6 (cells per L1 pool) = **384** **[End CB009142-A]** |

**Note:**

PRACH occsion capacity per L1 pool refers to simultaneous/parallel PRACH occasions per L1 pool **where simultaneous means a full or partial overlap in time.**

PRACH capacity per PRACH slot per L1 pool = PRACH capacity per PRACH slot per **subcell (= 64 according to 5G\_UP\_3302) \* minumum{X ; RO}.**

X =  the maximum number of supported cells/subcells per L1 pool.

RO =  the **maximum number of RACH Occasions "at same time" as defined in the table above per L1 pool.**

Where "at same time" means “in one PRACH duration time”.

For further details please refer to 5G\_UP\_5110.

For further details please refer to 5G\_UP\_5796.

Technology Map:

|  |  |
| --- | --- |
| **FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI** | Supported |
| **FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI** | **[CB011026-B] Supported** [End CB011026-B]\*\*\*\* |

**[CB013288-D-UPD001] For L1-Thor, If the number of L1 pools per L1 instance is equal to 1, it is assumed the number of L1 pools/L1 instance is equal or higher than 2, see 5G\_UP\_4005. When this number is equal to 1, the capacity per L1 pool is doubled.** [End CB013288-D-UPD001]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-IA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-IA]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-GA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI.**[End CB012115-GA]\*\*\*\*

-rdAntInactiveThresDb (5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1464)

-rdSwOffset (5G\_L1\_3843\_replaced([11451979](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fARZNPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), original location: 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1462)

-rdGuard (5G\_L1\_3820\_replaced([11451962](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fARZMvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_3824\_replaced([11452160](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fASATfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), original location: 5G\_L1\_5G21A\_1463)

-MAD\_e (5G\_L1\_3842\_replaced([11451789](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAQLG_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

#### 5.2.19.1.2 Loki

**5.2.19.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `11451741`)

Loki

rdPrachThresholdOffsetDb, rdAntInactiveThresDb, rdSwOffset, rdGuard, rdMinDetThreshold, pCorPrach and rdPrachMadEnable. The test team shall use other than recommended values but only for debugging purpose. All values must be reverted back the ones defined in L1 specification.

[CNI-122313-A]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313-A]

##### 5.2.19.2.2.3 rdPrachThresholdOffsetDb

###### 5.2.19.2.2.3.1 Parameter rationale

**5.2.19.2.2.3.1.0-2**  (ID: `11451888`)

Parameter rationale
The L1-SW (in Loner, Loki [RP003187-B, RP003187-I] and Thor [End RP003187-B, RP003187-I]) shall adjust the DTX threshold together with an offset rdPrachThresholdOffsetDb when MAD algorithm is enabled. Where rdPrachThresholdOffsetDb is a L1 RAD parameter defined in 5G\_L1\_3841\_replaced([11451805](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAQLHfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[CB007814-G] This requirement also applies to ABIO FR1-FDD-eCPRI. [End CB007814-G]

[Before-CNI-122313-A]

[CB009881-A, CB009881-CG, CB009881-W] This requirement shall be supported in RINLINE1 HW for FR1-TDD-eCPRI as part of CB009443.[End CB009881-A, CB009881-CG, CB009881-W]

[CB009444-B] This requirement is applicable for RINLINE1 for FR1-FDD-eCPRI. [End CB009444-B]

[CNI-122313-A]

RINLINE1 HW is supported until 24R1 inclusive. RINLINE1 HW is not supported since 24R2.

[End CNI-122313-A]

---

###### 5.2.19.2.2.3.2 Parameter definition

**5.2.19.2.2.3.2.0-1**  (ID: `11451906`)

Parameter definition
rdPrachThresholdOffsetDb

[01877927]

[From 22R1-5G] The values are defined in L1 internally in code as defined in 2.5.12 of 5Gmax algorithm specification document (5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and rdPrachThresholdOffsetDb was NOT used as R&D parameter.

[End 22R1-5G]

[End 01877927]

Value range: 0..15

Default value:

[Before  22R1-5G]

Short formats: 1 dB (default value) for TDD FR1 and 2dB for TDD FR2.

Long formats TDD/FDD: 2dB for 2Rx and 3 dB for 4Rx

[End Before 22R1-5G]

Unit: 1dB

Online modifiable: No

Step Size: 1

Specified in: 5G\_L1\_4113\_replaced([11449831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAGaH_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))(FDD)/5G\_L1\_4791\_replaced([11449850](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAHBIfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))(TDD)

#### 5.2.19.2.3 High power mitigation

**5.2.19.2.3.0-2**  (ID: `11451930`)

High power mitigation
rdEnableHighPowerMitigation

Value range: {0, 1}

Default value: 1

Unit: -

Online modifiable: No

Step Size: -

---

#### 5.2.19.2.4 Extended cell range

**5.2.19.2.4.0-1**  (ID: `11451946`)

Extended cell range
L1-SW (Loner and Loki) shall support the following RAD parameters to support extended cell range (CB007462):

a. PrachDoubleCellThreshold: this parameter is used to select peak14/initialTaFpga14 or peak25/initialTaFpga25, range [0...1], Step size =0.01, Default value is 0.9

b. PrachDoubleCellPowerError: this parameter is to set tolerance for power estimation error. range [0...1], Step size =0.01, Default value is 0.1

c. PrachDoubleCellTimeError: this parameter is to set tolerance for time estimation error. range [0...64], Step size = 1, Default value is 2

[CB010576-D] This requirement shall be supported in Thor HW for FR2-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI.[End CB010576-D]

---

#### 5.2.19.2.5 Peak detection

**5.2.19.2.5.0-1**  (ID: `11451962`)

Peak detection
rdGuard

Value range: 0…255

Default value:

As defined in 2.5.11 of 5Gmax algorithm specification document (5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

PRACH short format: 8

PRACH long format: 1 for 1024 IFFT and 2 for 2048 IFFT. e.g. in 21A, FDD is implemented with 1024 IFFT and TDD is with 2048.

Unit: one sample after 256 IFFT for short format or 1024/2048 IFFT for long format

Online modifiable: No

Step Size: 1

---

#### 5.2.19.2.6 Search window

**5.2.19.2.6.0-1**  (ID: `11451979`)

Search window
rdSwOffset

Value range: -128..512

As defined in 2.5.11 of 5Gmax algorithm specification document (5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Default value:

- PRACH short format: -32 -96 for FR1, -64 for FR2

- PRACH long format: -2 (1024 IFFT), -4 (2048 IFFT)

Please note that in 5G21A 1024 IFFT is used for FDD and 2048 is for TDD.

Unit: one sample after 256 IFFT for short format or 1024/2048 IFFT for long format

Online modifiable: No

Step Size: 1

Enabling and disabling
rdPrachMadEnable

Value range:  {0, 1}, where 1 enabled and  0  disabled

Default value: 1 for FDD (via 5GC002481-AA since 5G21A) and 1 for TDD (via 5GC005927-A since 5G20B)

Unit: -

##### 5.2.19.3.1.2 Max MAD

###### 5.2.19.3.1.2.1 Parameter name and description

**5.2.19.3.1.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11452050`)

Parameter name and description
In Loki and Thor, the L1 shall support the following MAD algorithm configuration parameter:

rdShortPrachMaxMadFlag

This parameter indicates whether the MaxMAD function is enabled or not for PRACH short formats. Detailed reference is found in 5G\_UP\_ALG\_27628\_replaced([11110548](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpFiDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

###### 5.2.19.3.1.2.2 Parameter interactions

**5.2.19.3.1.2.2.0-1**  (ID: `11452066`)

Parameter interactions
In Loki and Thor, the r&d parameter rdShortPrachMaxMadFlag shall be supported. When rdShortPrachMaxMadFlag is set to TRUE, the MaxMAD is used where the MAD statistic is derived using the maximum over all available root sequences. Whereas when rdShortPrachMaxMadFlag is set to FALSE, the MAD statistic is derived using the first available root sequence. An exception is when NRBTS/NRCELL/actPrachMultiplexingLevel (refer to 5G\_L1\_IF\_153\_replaced([11513459](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRwhwvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to enabled\_Level1 in which case MaxMAD is used and this rad parameter has no effect.

As indicated by the parameter naming, the parameter is applicable only with short formats.

For more information, refer to 5G\_UP\_ALG\_15428\_replaced([11105885](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koRCp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 5.2.19.3.2 Dtx threshold adjustment

##### 5.2.19.3.2.1 rdPrachThresholdOffsetDb

###### 5.2.19.3.2.1.1 Parameter rationale

###### 5.2.19.3.2.1.1.0-1 Parameter rationale The PFA and MD performance shall meet the 3GPP conformance test requirement defined in Section 8 and 11 of TS38.104 when the extended cell range flag is set to False (Normal mode). So, L1 is expected to offer tuning capability via RAD parameter (rdPrachThresholdOffsetDb) to balance the Msg1 vs Msg3 Note: this object is the Loki version of the original requirement written for Loner, Loki and Thor (refer to 5G_L1_5917_replaced( 11451922 )) created by the refactoring CNI. Under further refinement. (ID: 11452098)

###### 5.2.19.3.2.1.2 Parameter definition

**5.2.19.3.2.1.2.0-1**  (ID: `11452113`)

Parameter definition
rdPrachThresholdOffsetDb

rdPrachThresholdOffsetDbLong2Rx, rdPrachThresholdOffsetDbLong4Rx, rdPrachThresholdOffsetDbFr1Short2Rx, rdPrachThresholdOffsetDbFr1Short4Rx, rdPrachThresholdOffsetDbFr2Short2Rx

[01877927]

[From 22R1-5G] The values are defined in L1 internally in code as defined in 2.5.12 and 2.5.13 of 5Gmax algorithm specification document (5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and directly refer the value of PrachThresholdOffsetDb and for more detail refer to 5G\_L1\_8896\_replaced([11449868](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAHBI_vvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G\_L1\_8897\_replaced([11449880](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAHBJPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).[End 22R1-5G][End 01877927]

Value range: 0...100

Default value: Please see below

Unit: dB

Online modifiable: Require Cell Setup

Step Size: 1 (0.1dB)

Or short names in "()" due to name length limitation of framework:

rdPrachThresholdOffsetDbLong2Rx (rdPrchThrOffDbLong2Rx) = 20

rdPrachThresholdOffsetDbLong4Rx (rdPrchThrOffDbLong4Rx) = 30

rdPrachThresholdOffsetDbFr1Short2Rx (rdPrchThrOffDbFr1Short2Rx) = [PR621712]2015[End PR621712]

rdPrachThresholdOffsetDbFr1Short4Rx (rdPrchThrOffDbFr1Short4Rx) = 10

rdPrachThresholdOffsetDbFr2Short2Rx (rdPrchThrOffDbFr2Short2Rx) = 20

Note: the values mentioned are actual multipled by 10. e.g. 30 refers to 3 dB.

#### 5.2.19.3.6 Search window

**5.2.19.3.6.0-1**  (ID: `11452183`)

Search window
[PR583825] 5G-L1-UL of Loki shall support configurable PRACH search window offset (rdSwOffset) such that preamble with negative time offset can be detected. This has dependency with the PRACH formats and SCS. Applicable to both CPRI and eCPRI.

As defined in 2.5.12 and 2.5.13 of 5Gmax algorithm specification document (5G\_L1\_7703\_replaced([11396538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e8tH1vvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

rdSwOffsetLong1\_25

default value: -2

units: samples

value range: -64 ... 64

effective range: -2 … 0

step: 1

Note:

Used in LTE F0,F1,F2,F3; NR F0,F1,F2 with SCS = 1.25 kHz

Effective time offset range: -781.25 ... 0 ns

Time offset step value: 390.63 ns

Conversion formulas:

samples = round( time\_offset\_ns \* 0.00256 )

time\_offset\_ns = samples / 0.00256

rdSwOffsetShort15 (

default value: -4

units: samples

value range: -64 ... 64

effective range: -4 ... 0

step: 1

Note:

Used in NR Format A,B,C with SCS = 15 kHz

Effective time offset range: -520.83 ... 0 ns

Time offset step value: 130.21 ns

Conversion formulas:

samples = round( time\_offset\_ns \* 0.00768 )

time\_offset\_ns = samples / 0.00768

rdSwOffsetShort30

default value: -7

units: samples

value range: -64 ... 64

effective range: -7 ... 0

step: 1

Note:

Used in NR Format A,B,C with SCS = 30 kHz

Effective time offset range: -455.729 ... 0 ns

Time offset step value: 65.10 ns

Conversion formulas:

samples = round( time\_offset\_ns \* 0.01536 )

time\_offset\_ns = samples / 0.01536

rdSwOffsetShort120

default value: -14

units: samples

value range: -64 ... 64

effective range: -14 ... 0

step: 1

Note:

Used in NR Format A,B,C with SCS = 120 kHz

Effective time offset range: -227.865 ... 0 ns

Time offset step value: 16.28 ns

Conversion formulas:

samples = round( time\_offset\_ns \* 0.06144 )

time\_offset\_ns = samples / 0.06144

Value range: -64...64

Default value:

* rdSwOffsetLong1\_25 -2 (PRACH Long format, scs=1.25 kHz)
* rdSwOffsetShort30       -7 (PRACH Short format, scs=30 kHz)
* rdSwOffsetShort120     -14 (PRACH Short format, scs=120 kHz)

Unit: number of samples

Online modifiable: No

Step Size: 1

#### 5.2.19.3.7 FDAGC

**5.2.19.3.7.0-1**  (ID: `11452200`)

FDAGC
In L1 internally, FDAGC PRACH algorithm is always on for LOKI in case of HST for short PRACH and FDD eCPRI when extended cell feature is deactivated (cellExtension = 10).

Note: R&D parameter (rdFdagcEnable) is no more valid and shall be removed from R&D parameter.

For more details, please check 5G\_L1\_15212\_replaced([11449596](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAFzAPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

##### 5.2.19.4.2.1 rdPrachThresholdOffsetDb

**5.2.19.4.2.1.0-1**  (ID: `11452345`)

rdPrachThresholdOffsetDb
The L1-SW  **[RP003187-B, RP003187-I] and Thor [End RP003187-B, RP003187-I]) shall adjust the DTX threshold together with an offset rdPrachThresholdOffsetDb when MAD algorithm is enabled. Where rdPrachThresholdOffsetDb is a L1 RAD parameter defined in 5G\_L1\_3841\_replaced([11451805](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fAQLHfvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

**[RP003187-I] The requirement is also valid for** L1 Thor for FR1 FDD CPRI **[End RP003187-I]**\*\*\*\*

**[CB010575-A] This requirement for L3 Call shall be supported in L1 Thor HW for FR1-TDD-CPRI. For L3 call MAD algorithm is always on.** [End CB010575-A]\*\*\*\*

**[CB012115-JA] The requirement is also applicable for Odin FR1-FDD-CPRI.**[End CB012115-JA]\*\*\*\*

#### 5.2.19.4.8 Power measurement adjustment

**5.2.19.4.8.0-1**  (ID: `11452461`)

Power measurement adjustment
pCorPrach (This is used to adjust any offset/bias in the L1 power measurements during the calibration)

Value range: -10...10

Default value: 0

Unit: dB

Online modifiable: No

Step Size: 0.5

|  |  |  |
| --- | --- | --- |
|  | **Thor** | Odin |
| **FR1-FDD-CPRI** | Supported | [CB012115-JA]Supported [End CB012115-JA] |
| **FR1-FDD-OBSAI** | **[CB010969-SR-CB] Supported** [End CB010969-SR-CB]\*\*\*\* |  |
| **FR1-FDD-7-2a-eCPRI** |  | [CB012115-LA]Supported [End CB012115-LA] |
| **FR1-TDD-7-2a-eCPRI** | Supported | [CB012115-IA]Supported [End CB012115-IA] |
| **FR1-TDD-7-2e-eCPRI** | **[CB009514-F] Supported** [End CB009514-F]\*\*\*\* | [CB012115-GA]Supported [End CB012115-GA] |

#### 5.2.19.4.9 Tadv estimation resolution improvement algorithms

**5.2.19.4.9.0-1**  (ID: `11452476`)

Tadv estimation resolution improvement algorithms
[Before CB013507-C]

*rdTadvresolution(This is used to control whether L1 support Tadv estimation resolution improvement algorithms or not)*

Value range: **0,1 (0: algorithm will not be supported. 1:algorithm will be supported, decided together with parameter actUlNrEcidTAdv**

, for detailed logic refer to 5G\_L1\_19644\_replaced([11450757](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_fALSkvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Default value: 1

[End CB013507-C]
